# PART 1: ARCHITECTURE

# GrandCafe Cheers -- Employee Mobile App Architecture\n\n**Version:** 1.0.0\n**Date:** 2026-03-14\n**Status:** Draft\n**Stack:** Expo (managed) + Expo Router v4 + NativeWind v4 + TanStack Query v5 + Zustand + MMKV + Supabase + Expo Notifications + i18next\n\n---\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Project Structure](#1-project-structure)\n2. [Navigation Architecture](#2-navigation-architecture)\n3. [Supabase Client Setup](#3-supabase-client-setup)\n4. [State Management Architecture](#4-state-management-architecture)\n5. [Offline Strategy](#5-offline-strategy)\n6. [Security Considerations](#6-security-considerations)\n7. [Key Architectural Decisions](#7-key-architectural-decisions)\n\n---\n\n## 1. Project Structure\n\n```\ngrandcafe-cheers-mobile/\n├── app.json                          # Expo config (scheme, plugins, splash)\n├── babel.config.js                   # NativeWind preset\n├── metro.config.js                   # NativeWind Metro integration\n├── tailwind.config.ts                # Shared color tokens from web app\n├── tsconfig.json                     # Strict mode, path aliases\n├── eas.json                          # EAS Build profiles (dev, preview, production)\n├── global.css                        # NativeWind global styles\n├── .env.example                      # Required env vars template\n│\n├── app/                              # Expo Router — file-based routing\n│   ├── _layout.tsx                   # Root layout: providers wrapper\n│   ├── index.tsx                     # Entry redirect: auth check → /login or /(tabs)\n│   │\n│   ├── (auth)/                       # Unauthenticated group\n│   │   ├── _layout.tsx               # Auth stack layout (no tabs)\n│   │   ├── login.tsx                 # Email + password login\n│   │   └── forgot-password.tsx       # Password reset flow\n│   │\n│   ├── (tabs)/                       # Authenticated tab group\n│   │   ├── _layout.tsx               # Tab bar with 5 tabs\n│   │   │\n│   │   ├── index.tsx                 # Tab 1: Home (dashboard)\n│   │   │\n│   │   ├── schedule/                 # Tab 2: Schedule\n│   │   │   ├── _layout.tsx           # Stack navigator for schedule tab\n│   │   │   ├── index.tsx             # Weekly schedule view\n│   │   │   ├── [date].tsx            # Day detail with all shifts\n│   │   │   └── shift/[id].tsx        # Individual shift detail\n│   │   │\n│   │   ├── clock.tsx                 # Tab 3: Clock in/out (center FAB)\n│   │   │\n│   │   ├── chat/                     # Tab 4: AI Chat\n│   │   │   ├── _layout.tsx           # Stack navigator for chat tab\n│   │   │   ├── index.tsx             # Conversation list\n│   │   │   └── [conversationId].tsx  # Active conversation\n│   │   │\n│   │   └── more/                     # Tab 5: More menu\n│   │       ├── _layout.tsx           # Stack navigator for more tab\n│   │       ├── index.tsx             # Settings grid/list\n│   │       ├── profile.tsx           # Edit profile\n│   │       ├── notifications.tsx     # Notification center\n│   │       ├── leave/                # Leave management\n│   │       │   ├── index.tsx         # Leave balance + request list\n│   │       │   └── request.tsx       # New leave request form\n│   │       ├── availability.tsx      # Set weekly availability\n│   │       ├── swap-requests.tsx     # Shift swap inbox\n│   │       ├── tasks.tsx             # Assigned tasks checklist\n│   │       ├── training.tsx          # Training materials & compliance\n│   │       ├── hours-summary.tsx     # Monthly hours overview\n│   │       └── settings.tsx          # App settings (locale, theme, biometric)\n│   │\n│   └── +not-found.tsx                # 404 fallback\n│\n├── components/                       # Shared + feature components\n│   ├── ui/                           # Design system primitives\n│   │   ├── button.tsx\n│   │   ├── card.tsx\n│   │   ├── input.tsx\n│   │   ├── badge.tsx\n│   │   ├── avatar.tsx\n│   │   ├── bottom-sheet.tsx          # @gorhom/bottom-sheet wrapper\n│   │   ├── loading-spinner.tsx\n│   │   ├── empty-state.tsx\n│   │   ├── error-boundary.tsx\n│   │   └── haptic-tab.tsx            # Tab bar button with haptic feedback\n│   │\n│   ├── home/                         # Home tab components\n│   │   ├── today-shift-card.tsx      # Current/next shift summary\n│   │   ├── clock-status-banner.tsx   # \"Clocked in since 09:00\"\n│   │   ├── quick-actions.tsx         # Clock in, request leave, etc.\n│   │   ├── notification-feed.tsx     # Recent notifications preview\n│   │   └── weather-widget.tsx        # Mallorca weather (optional)\n│   │\n│   ├── schedule/                     # Schedule tab components\n│   │   ├── week-strip.tsx            # Horizontal scrollable week selector\n│   │   ├── day-schedule-card.tsx     # Single day with shifts\n│   │   ├── shift-detail-card.tsx     # Expanded shift info\n│   │   ├── shift-type-badge.tsx      # Morning/Afternoon/Night pill\n│   │   └── colleague-list.tsx        # Who else is working\n│   │\n│   ├── clock/                        # Clock tab components\n│   │   ├── clock-button.tsx          # Large clock in/out button\n│   │   ├── elapsed-timer.tsx         # Live timer since clock-in\n│   │   ├── break-controls.tsx        # Start/end break\n│   │   ├── geolocation-status.tsx    # Geofence indicator\n│   │   └── shift-summary-modal.tsx   # Post-clock-out summary\n│   │\n│   ├── chat/                         # Chat tab components\n│   │   ├── message-bubble.tsx        # Single message\n│   │   ├── message-input.tsx         # Input bar with send\n│   │   ├── streaming-indicator.tsx   # Typing/tool-use animation\n│   │   ├── tool-status-pill.tsx      # Active tool indicator\n│   │   ├── pending-action-card.tsx   # Confirm/reject write action\n│   │   └── conversation-list-item.tsx\n│   │\n│   ├── tasks/                        # Task components\n│   │   ├── task-card.tsx\n│   │   ├── task-checklist-item.tsx\n│   │   └── task-priority-badge.tsx\n│   │\n│   ├── leave/                        # Leave components\n│   │   ├── leave-balance-card.tsx\n│   │   ├── leave-request-card.tsx\n│   │   └── leave-calendar-strip.tsx\n│   │\n│   └── providers/                    # Context providers\n│       ├── app-providers.tsx         # Composes all providers\n│       ├── auth-provider.tsx         # Supabase auth session\n│       ├── query-provider.tsx        # TanStack Query client\n│       ├── notification-provider.tsx # Push notification registration\n│       └── realtime-provider.tsx     # Supabase Realtime channels\n│\n├── lib/                              # Core libraries\n│   ├── supabase/\n│   │   ├── client.ts                 # createClient() with SecureStore adapter\n│   │   ├── realtime.ts              # Channel subscription helpers\n│   │   └── types.ts                 # Re-export Database types\n│   │\n│   ├── api/                          # Next.js API route callers\n│   │   ├── client.ts                # Authenticated fetch wrapper\n│   │   ├── clock.ts                 # Clock in/out/break API calls\n│   │   ├── shifts.ts                # Shift CRUD\n│   │   ├── leave.ts                 # Leave request API calls\n│   │   ├── swap-requests.ts         # Shift swap API calls\n│   │   ├── tasks.ts                 # Task API calls\n│   │   ├── notifications.ts        # Notification API calls\n│   │   └── chat.ts                  # AI chat SSE stream\n│   │\n│   ├── hooks/                        # Custom React hooks\n│   │   ├── use-auth.ts              # Auth state + actions\n│   │   ├── use-profile.ts           # Profile query hook\n│   │   ├── use-shifts.ts            # Shifts queries (my shifts, week, day)\n│   │   ├── use-clock.ts             # Clock status + actions\n│   │   ├── use-notifications.ts     # Notification queries + realtime\n│   │   ├── use-tasks.ts             # Tasks queries\n│   │   ├── use-leave.ts             # Leave balance + requests\n│   │   ├── use-swap-requests.ts     # Swap requests queries\n│   │   ├── use-chat-stream.ts       # AI chat SSE streaming hook\n│   │   ├── use-geolocation.ts       # expo-location wrapper\n│   │   ├── use-haptics.ts           # Haptic feedback helper\n│   │   └── use-network-status.ts    # Online/offline detection\n│   │\n│   └── utils/\n│       ├── date.ts                   # date-fns wrappers, timezone (Europe/Madrid)\n│       ├── format.ts                 # Currency, hours formatting\n│       ├── shift-colors.ts           # Shift type → color mapping\n│       └── validation.ts             # Shared Zod schemas\n│\n├── stores/                           # Zustand stores (client state)\n│   ├── auth-store.ts                # Session, user, employee\n│   ├── app-store.ts                 # Locale, theme, selected date\n│   ├── clock-store.ts              # Clock-in state, timer\n│   └── offline-queue-store.ts       # Queued offline actions\n│\n├── i18n/                             # Internationalization\n│   ├── config.ts                     # i18next setup + language detection\n│   ├── en/                           # English translations\n│   │   ├── common.json\n│   │   ├── home.json\n│   │   ├── schedule.json\n│   │   ├── clock.json\n│   │   ├── chat.json\n│   │   ├── leave.json\n│   │   ├── tasks.json\n│   │   └── settings.json\n│   ├── nl/                           # Dutch translations (same structure)\n│   ├── es/                           # Spanish translations\n│   └── de/                           # German translations\n│\n├── constants/\n│   ├── theme.ts                      # OKLch tokens matching web app\n│   ├── colors.ts                     # Role colors, shift type colors\n│   ├── config.ts                     # API URL, geofence radius, timezone\n│   ├── query-keys.ts                # TanStack Query key factory\n│   └── roles.ts                     # Role definitions, permissions\n│\n├── assets/\n│   ├── images/\n│   │   ├── logo.png\n│   │   ├── splash.png\n│   │   └── icon.png\n│   └── fonts/\n│       └── (custom fonts if any)\n│\n└── types/\n    ├── index.ts                      # Domain types (copied/shared from web app)\n    ├── navigation.ts                # Route params type definitions\n    └── api.ts                       # API response types\n```\n\n### File Organization Principles\n\n- **Feature-first** organization within `components/` -- each tab has its own directory.\n- **lib/hooks/** contains one hook per data domain, each under 200 lines.\n- **lib/api/** contains thin wrappers around fetch calls to the existing Next.js API routes.\n- **stores/** contains Zustand stores for purely client-side state; server state lives in TanStack Query.\n- **types/** shares types with the web app. The `types/index.ts` file is a copy of the web app's `src/types/index.ts` to avoid runtime import dependencies. A shared npm package can be extracted later.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Navigation Architecture\n\n### 2.1 Route Structure\n\n```\n/                           → Redirect: session exists → /(tabs) : /(auth)/login\n/(auth)/login               → Login screen\n/(auth)/forgot-password     → Password reset\n/(tabs)/                    → Home tab (index.tsx)\n/(tabs)/schedule/           → Weekly schedule\n/(tabs)/schedule/[date]     → Day detail\n/(tabs)/schedule/shift/[id] → Shift detail\n/(tabs)/clock               → Clock in/out\n/(tabs)/chat/               → Conversation list\n/(tabs)/chat/[conversationId] → Chat thread\n/(tabs)/more/               → More menu grid\n/(tabs)/more/profile        → Edit profile\n/(tabs)/more/notifications  → All notifications\n/(tabs)/more/leave/         → Leave overview\n/(tabs)/more/leave/request  → Leave request form\n/(tabs)/more/availability   → Availability editor\n/(tabs)/more/swap-requests  → Swap request inbox\n/(tabs)/more/tasks          → Tasks checklist\n/(tabs)/more/training       → Training materials\n/(tabs)/more/hours-summary  → Monthly hours\n/(tabs)/more/settings       → App settings\n```\n\n### 2.2 Root Layout (`app/_layout.tsx`)\n\n```typescript\n// Pseudo-structure — wraps everything in providers\nexport default function RootLayout() {\n  return (\n    <AppProviders>\n      {/* AuthProvider checks session, redirects if needed */}\n      <Slot />\n    </AppProviders>\n  );\n}\n```\n\nThe root layout initializes:\n1. **i18next** with persisted locale from MMKV\n2. **TanStack QueryClientProvider** with MMKV-backed persister\n3. **AuthProvider** wrapping Supabase session listener\n4. **RealtimeProvider** subscribing to relevant channels\n5. **NotificationProvider** registering push token on mount\n6. NativeWind theme provider\n\n### 2.3 Tab Layout (`app/(tabs)/_layout.tsx`)\n\n| Tab | Icon | Label | Route |\n|-----|------|-------|-------|\n| Home | `House` | Home | `/(tabs)/` |\n| Schedule | `Calendar` | Schedule | `/(tabs)/schedule` |\n| Clock | `Clock` (center, raised) | Clock | `/(tabs)/clock` |\n| Chat | `MessageCircle` | Chat | `/(tabs)/chat` |\n| More | `MoreHorizontal` | More | `/(tabs)/more` |\n\nThe center Clock tab uses a custom `tabBarButton` with a raised circular design and haptic feedback. The Chat tab shows an unread badge count from the notifications query.\n\n### 2.4 Auth Flow\n\n```\nApp Launch\n    │\n    ├─ SecureStore has refresh_token?\n    │   ├─ YES → supabase.auth.getSession() → valid?\n    │   │           ├─ YES → router.replace('/(tabs)')\n    │   │           └─ NO  → router.replace('/(auth)/login')\n    │   └─ NO  → router.replace('/(auth)/login')\n    │\nLogin Screen\n    │\n    ├─ supabase.auth.signInWithPassword()\n    │   ├─ Success → store session → register push token → router.replace('/(tabs)')\n    │   └─ Failure → show error\n```\n\nRoute protection is handled at the layout level. The `(tabs)` group layout checks for an active Supabase session. If none exists, it redirects to `/(auth)/login`. The `(auth)` group layout checks for an existing session and redirects to `/(tabs)` if found.\n\n### 2.5 Deep Linking Schema\n\n**URI scheme:** `cheers://`\n\n| Deep Link | Target Route | Trigger |\n|-----------|-------------|---------|\n| `cheers://schedule/2026-03-14` | `/(tabs)/schedule/2026-03-14` | Shift assigned notification |\n| `cheers://schedule/shift/uuid` | `/(tabs)/schedule/shift/uuid` | Shift changed notification |\n| `cheers://clock` | `/(tabs)/clock` | Clock reminder notification |\n| `cheers://chat/uuid` | `/(tabs)/chat/uuid` | AI response notification |\n| `cheers://swap-requests` | `/(tabs)/more/swap-requests` | Swap request notification |\n| `cheers://tasks` | `/(tabs)/more/tasks` | Task assigned notification |\n| `cheers://leave` | `/(tabs)/more/leave` | Leave approved/rejected |\n| `cheers://notifications` | `/(tabs)/more/notifications` | Generic notification tap |\n\nConfiguration in `app.json`:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"expo\": {\n    \"scheme\": \"cheers\",\n    \"plugins\": [\n      \"expo-router\",\n      [\n        \"expo-notifications\",\n        {\n          \"icon\": \"./assets/images/notification-icon.png\",\n          \"color\": \"#1a1a2e\"\n        }\n      ]\n    ]\n  }\n}\n```\n\nPush notifications include a `url` field in their data payload. The notification handler in `NotificationProvider` calls `router.push(notification.data.url)` on tap.\n\n### 2.6 Modal Routes\n\nModals are presented using Expo Router's `presentation: 'modal'` on specific stack screens within each tab. For example, shift detail opens as a modal card on iOS. Leave request form also presents as a modal from the leave index.\n\nThe `shift-summary-modal` (post-clock-out) is not a route -- it is a React component rendered conditionally over the clock screen using `@gorhom/bottom-sheet`.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Supabase Client Setup\n\n### 3.1 Client Configuration (`lib/supabase/client.ts`)\n\n```typescript\nimport { createClient as createSupabaseClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js';\nimport * as SecureStore from 'expo-secure-store';\nimport { Platform } from 'react-native';\nimport type { Database } from './types';\n\nconst SUPABASE_URL = process.env.EXPO_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!;\nconst SUPABASE_ANON_KEY = process.env.EXPO_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY!;\n\nconst ExpoSecureStoreAdapter = {\n  getItem: async (key: string): Promise<string | null> => {\n    if (Platform.OS === 'web') {\n      return localStorage.getItem(key);\n    }\n    return SecureStore.getItemAsync(key);\n  },\n  setItem: async (key: string, value: string): Promise<void> => {\n    if (Platform.OS === 'web') {\n      localStorage.setItem(key, value);\n      return;\n    }\n    await SecureStore.setItemAsync(key, value);\n  },\n  removeItem: async (key: string): Promise<void> => {\n    if (Platform.OS === 'web') {\n      localStorage.removeItem(key);\n      return;\n    }\n    await SecureStore.deleteItemAsync(key);\n  },\n};\n\nexport const supabase = createSupabaseClient<Database>(\n  SUPABASE_URL,\n  SUPABASE_ANON_KEY,\n  {\n    auth: {\n      storage: ExpoSecureStoreAdapter,\n      autoRefreshToken: true,\n      persistSession: true,\n      detectSessionInUrl: false, // No URL-based auth in React Native\n    },\n  }\n);\n```\n\n**Critical:** The mobile app uses ONLY the **anon key**. The service role key never exists on the device.\n\n### 3.2 API Call Strategy: When to Use Direct Supabase vs Next.js API Routes\n\nThe existing backend has two access patterns. The mobile app must choose the right one for each operation.\n\n#### Direct Supabase Queries (preferred for reads)\n\nUse direct Supabase client queries when:\n- The operation is a **simple read** covered by existing RLS policies.\n- No server-side business logic is needed beyond data filtering.\n- The table is in the `supabase_realtime` publication (for live updates).\n\n| Operation | Table | RLS Covers It? | Use Direct? |\n|-----------|-------|---------------|-------------|\n| My shifts this week | `shifts` | Yes (staff see own via employee_id join) | Yes |\n| My clock records | `clock_in_out` | Yes (staff see own) | Yes |\n| My leave requests | `leave_requests` | Yes (staff see own) | Yes |\n| My leave entitlements | `leave_entitlements` | Yes (staff see own) | Yes |\n| My notifications | `notifications` | Yes (user_id = auth.uid()) | Yes |\n| My availability | `availability` | Yes (staff see own) | Yes |\n| My swap requests | `shift_swap_requests` | Yes (staff see own + involved) | Yes |\n| My tasks | `staff_tasks` | Partial (role-based visibility) | Yes |\n| Published schedule plans | `schedule_plans` | Yes (status = 'published') | Yes |\n| My profile | `profiles` | Yes (own row) | Yes |\n| Mark notification read | `notifications` update | Yes (own row) | Yes |\n\n#### Next.js API Routes (required for writes with business logic)\n\nUse the existing Next.js API routes when:\n- The operation has **server-side business logic** (validation, grace periods, geolocation, side effects).\n- The operation touches **multiple tables** atomically.\n- The operation uses `createAdminClient()` on the server to bypass RLS.\n\n| Operation | API Route | Why Not Direct? |\n|-----------|-----------|----------------|\n| Clock in | `POST /api/staff/clock?action=in` | Geofence validation, shift auto-link, grace period check, metadata injection |\n| Clock out | `POST /api/staff/clock?action=out` | Auto-close breaks, calculate summary, audit log |\n| Start/end break | `POST /api/staff/clock/break` | Ownership validation, active-break guard |\n| Create leave request | Via direct insert | RLS allows staff insert on own employee_id |\n| Cancel leave request | `PATCH /api/staff/leave/[id]` | Status transition validation |\n| Create swap request | Via direct insert | RLS allows staff insert when requested_by = own |\n| Update swap status | Via direct + realtime | RLS allows update for involved parties |\n| AI chat | `POST /api/ai/chat/stream` | Anthropic SDK, system prompt, tool execution -- all server-side |\n| Update profile | Via direct update | RLS allows own-row update |\n| Register push token | `POST /api/notifications/subscribe` | Endpoint + key registration |\n\n#### Authenticated Fetch Wrapper (`lib/api/client.ts`)\n\n```typescript\nimport { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase/client';\n\nconst API_BASE_URL = process.env.EXPO_PUBLIC_API_URL!;\n// e.g., 'https://grandcafe-cheers.vercel.app' or Cloud Run URL\n\nexport async function authenticatedFetch(\n  path: string,\n  options: RequestInit = {}\n): Promise<Response> {\n  const { data: { session } } = await supabase.auth.getSession();\n\n  if (!session?.access_token) {\n    throw new Error('Not authenticated');\n  }\n\n  const url = `${API_BASE_URL}${path}`;\n\n  return fetch(url, {\n    ...options,\n    headers: {\n      'Content-Type': 'application/json',\n      Authorization: `Bearer ${session.access_token}`,\n      ...options.headers,\n    },\n  });\n}\n```\n\n**Important note on auth forwarding:** The web app uses cookie-based auth (`createServerClient` with cookies). The mobile app cannot send cookies. Instead, it sends the JWT as a `Bearer` token in the `Authorization` header. This requires a small change on the server side for API routes that the mobile app calls.\n\nThe existing `createClient()` in `src/lib/supabase/server.ts` uses `cookies()`. For mobile compatibility, API routes called by both web and mobile need a helper that checks for the `Authorization` header first, falling back to cookies:\n\n```typescript\n// Server-side helper: createClientFromRequest(request)\n// Checks Authorization header → if JWT present, create client with that token\n// Falls back to cookie-based auth for web requests\n```\n\nThis is a **one-time backend change** affecting approximately 5-8 API routes that the mobile app calls (clock, break, leave, AI chat, push subscribe).\n\n### 3.3 Realtime Subscriptions (`lib/supabase/realtime.ts`)\n\nThe database already publishes these tables to `supabase_realtime`:\n- `shifts` -- schedule changes\n- `shift_swap_requests` -- swap status updates\n- `clock_in_out` -- clock status (for manager views)\n- `clock_breaks` -- break status\n- `notifications` -- instant notification delivery\n- `staff_tasks` -- task assignments\n- `staff_task_items` -- task completion\n- `training_assignments` -- training assignments\n\nThe mobile app subscribes to filtered channels:\n\n```typescript\n// Example: Subscribe to own notifications\nconst channel = supabase\n  .channel('my-notifications')\n  .on(\n    'postgres_changes',\n    {\n      event: 'INSERT',\n      schema: 'public',\n      table: 'notifications',\n      filter: `user_id=eq.${userId}`,\n    },\n    (payload) => {\n      // Invalidate notifications query → TanStack Query refetches\n      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.notifications.all });\n      // Show local notification if app is backgrounded\n      showLocalNotification(payload.new);\n    }\n  )\n  .subscribe();\n```\n\n**Channels the app subscribes to on login:**\n\n| Channel | Table | Filter | Purpose |\n|---------|-------|--------|---------|\n| `my-notifications` | `notifications` | `user_id=eq.${userId}` | Instant notification delivery |\n| `my-shifts` | `shifts` | `employee_id=eq.${employeeId}` | Schedule changes |\n| `my-swaps` | `shift_swap_requests` | `requested_by=eq.${empId}` OR `offered_to=eq.${empId}` | Swap updates |\n| `my-tasks` | `staff_tasks` | `assigned_to=eq.${empId}` | Task assignments |\n\nAll channels are torn down on logout via `supabase.removeAllChannels()`.\n\n### 3.4 Reusing Existing RLS Policies\n\nThe mobile Supabase client authenticates with the same JWT as the web client. The `auth.uid()` function in RLS policies works identically because the JWT is issued by the same Supabase Auth instance.\n\n**No RLS changes required.** All existing policies referencing `auth.uid()`, `profiles.role`, and `employees.profile_id` work as-is for mobile clients.\n\nKey RLS patterns already in place:\n- Staff see own shifts: `employee_id = (SELECT id FROM employees WHERE profile_id = auth.uid())`\n- Staff see own clock records: same pattern\n- Staff see own notifications: `user_id = auth.uid()`\n- Staff can insert own availability, swap requests, leave requests\n- Published schedule plans visible to all authenticated users\n- Managers see everything (no mobile-specific manager features in v1)\n\n---\n\n## 4. State Management Architecture\n\n### 4.1 State Ownership Matrix\n\n| Data | Owner | Persistence | Sync |\n|------|-------|-------------|------|\n| Auth session + JWT | Zustand `auth-store` | SecureStore (via Supabase SDK) | Supabase auto-refresh |\n| User profile | TanStack Query | MMKV cache | Refetch on focus |\n| My shifts (current week) | TanStack Query | MMKV cache | Realtime + refetch |\n| Clock status (am I clocked in?) | TanStack Query + Zustand `clock-store` | MMKV for timer state | Realtime on `clock_in_out` |\n| Notifications | TanStack Query | MMKV cache | Realtime INSERT |\n| Leave balance | TanStack Query | MMKV cache | Refetch on focus |\n| Leave requests | TanStack Query | MMKV cache | Refetch on mutation |\n| Swap requests | TanStack Query | MMKV cache | Realtime |\n| Tasks | TanStack Query | MMKV cache | Realtime |\n| AI chat messages | TanStack Query per conversation | No persistence | SSE stream |\n| AI conversations list | TanStack Query | No persistence | Refetch on focus |\n| Selected date (schedule) | Zustand `app-store` | None (ephemeral) | N/A |\n| Locale preference | Zustand `app-store` | MMKV | N/A |\n| Theme preference | Zustand `app-store` | MMKV | N/A |\n| Biometric enabled | Zustand `app-store` | MMKV | N/A |\n| Offline action queue | Zustand `offline-queue-store` | MMKV | Flush on reconnect |\n\n### 4.2 Zustand Stores\n\n#### `stores/auth-store.ts`\n\n```typescript\ninterface AuthState {\n  session: Session | null;\n  user: User | null;\n  profile: Profile | null;\n  employee: Employee | null;\n  isLoading: boolean;\n\n  // Actions (return new state, no mutation)\n  setSession: (session: Session | null) => void;\n  setProfile: (profile: Profile) => void;\n  setEmployee: (employee: Employee) => void;\n  signOut: () => Promise<void>;\n}\n```\n\n#### `stores/app-store.ts`\n\n```typescript\ninterface AppState {\n  locale: 'en' | 'nl' | 'es' | 'de';\n  theme: 'light' | 'dark' | 'system';\n  selectedDate: string; // YYYY-MM-DD, for schedule navigation\n  biometricEnabled: boolean;\n\n  setLocale: (locale: AppState['locale']) => void;\n  setTheme: (theme: AppState['theme']) => void;\n  setSelectedDate: (date: string) => void;\n  setBiometricEnabled: (enabled: boolean) => void;\n}\n```\n\nPersisted to MMKV using Zustand's `persist` middleware with an MMKV storage adapter.\n\n#### `stores/clock-store.ts`\n\n```typescript\ninterface ClockState {\n  activeClockRecordId: string | null;\n  clockInTime: string | null;  // ISO timestamp\n  isOnBreak: boolean;\n  activeBreakId: string | null;\n  breakStartTime: string | null;\n\n  setClockIn: (recordId: string, clockInTime: string) => void;\n  setClockOut: () => void;\n  setBreakStart: (breakId: string, startTime: string) => void;\n  setBreakEnd: () => void;\n}\n```\n\nThis store is hydrated on app launch by querying `clock_in_out` for an open record (where `clock_out_time IS NULL`). The elapsed timer in the UI reads `clockInTime` and computes the difference to `Date.now()` every second using `setInterval`.\n\n#### `stores/offline-queue-store.ts`\n\n```typescript\ninterface QueuedAction {\n  id: string;\n  type: 'availability_update' | 'task_complete' | 'notification_read';\n  payload: Record<string, unknown>;\n  createdAt: string;\n  retryCount: number;\n}\n\ninterface OfflineQueueState {\n  queue: QueuedAction[];\n  enqueue: (action: Omit<QueuedAction, 'id' | 'createdAt' | 'retryCount'>) => void;\n  dequeue: (id: string) => void;\n  flush: () => Promise<void>;\n}\n```\n\n### 4.3 TanStack Query Configuration\n\n#### Query Client (`components/providers/query-provider.tsx`)\n\n```typescript\nimport { QueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';\nimport { createSyncStoragePersister } from '@tanstack/query-sync-storage-persister';\nimport { PersistQueryClientProvider } from '@tanstack/react-query-persist-client';\nimport { mmkvStorage } from '@/lib/utils/mmkv';\n\nconst queryClient = new QueryClient({\n  defaultOptions: {\n    queries: {\n      staleTime: 30_000,         // 30s — same as web app's SWR config\n      gcTime: 24 * 60 * 60_000,  // 24h — keep cache for offline\n      retry: 2,\n      refetchOnWindowFocus: false, // Disabled — Realtime handles updates\n      refetchOnReconnect: true,\n    },\n    mutations: {\n      retry: 1,\n    },\n  },\n});\n\nconst persister = createSyncStoragePersister({\n  storage: {\n    getItem: (key) => mmkvStorage.getString(key) ?? null,\n    setItem: (key, value) => mmkvStorage.set(key, value),\n    removeItem: (key) => mmkvStorage.delete(key),\n  },\n  // Only persist queries that are marked as persistable\n  // via queryKey convention\n});\n```\n\n#### Query Key Factory (`constants/query-keys.ts`)\n\n```typescript\nexport const queryKeys = {\n  profile: {\n    me: ['profile', 'me'] as const,\n  },\n  shifts: {\n    all: ['shifts'] as const,\n    week: (weekStart: string) => ['shifts', 'week', weekStart] as const,\n    day: (date: string) => ['shifts', 'day', date] as const,\n    detail: (id: string) => ['shifts', 'detail', id] as const,\n  },\n  clock: {\n    status: ['clock', 'status'] as const,\n    history: (params: { startDate?: string; endDate?: string }) =>\n      ['clock', 'history', params] as const,\n  },\n  notifications: {\n    all: ['notifications'] as const,\n    unreadCount: ['notifications', 'unread-count'] as const,\n  },\n  leave: {\n    entitlements: (year: number) => ['leave', 'entitlements', year] as const,\n    requests: ['leave', 'requests'] as const,\n  },\n  swapRequests: {\n    all: ['swap-requests'] as const,\n  },\n  tasks: {\n    mine: ['tasks', 'mine'] as const,\n  },\n  chat: {\n    conversations: ['chat', 'conversations'] as const,\n    messages: (conversationId: string) =>\n      ['chat', 'messages', conversationId] as const,\n  },\n  training: {\n    materials: ['training', 'materials'] as const,\n    progress: ['training', 'progress'] as const,\n  },\n} as const;\n```\n\n### 4.4 Cache Invalidation Strategy\n\nCache invalidation is driven by three mechanisms:\n\n1. **Realtime subscriptions** -- Supabase Postgres Changes trigger `queryClient.invalidateQueries()` for the affected query key. This is the primary mechanism for live data.\n\n2. **Optimistic updates** -- For mutations with immediate visual feedback (marking notification read, completing task item), the query cache is updated optimistically via `onMutate`, with rollback on error.\n\n3. **Refetch on reconnect** -- When the device comes back online (detected via `NetInfo`), all stale queries are refetched. The offline queue is flushed first.\n\n| Event | Invalidation Target |\n|-------|-------------------|\n| Realtime: `notifications` INSERT | `queryKeys.notifications.all`, `queryKeys.notifications.unreadCount` |\n| Realtime: `shifts` INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE | `queryKeys.shifts.all`, `queryKeys.shifts.week(affected)` |\n| Realtime: `shift_swap_requests` UPDATE | `queryKeys.swapRequests.all` |\n| Realtime: `staff_tasks` UPDATE | `queryKeys.tasks.mine` |\n| Realtime: `clock_in_out` INSERT/UPDATE | `queryKeys.clock.status` |\n| Mutation: clock in | `queryKeys.clock.status`, `queryKeys.clock.history(...)` |\n| Mutation: clock out | Same + refetch shift for summary |\n| Mutation: create leave request | `queryKeys.leave.requests` |\n| Mutation: complete task item | `queryKeys.tasks.mine` (optimistic) |\n| App foreground | Refetch stale queries (staleTime = 30s) |\n| Network reconnect | Flush offline queue, then refetch all |\n\n---\n\n## 5. Offline Strategy\n\n### 5.1 What Works Offline\n\n| Feature | Offline Behavior | Data Source |\n|---------|-----------------|-------------|\n| View schedule (current + next week) | Fully available from MMKV-persisted TanStack Query cache | Last fetched data |\n| View profile | Available from cache | Last fetched data |\n| View notification history | Available from cache | Last fetched data |\n| View leave balance | Available from cache | Last fetched data |\n| View task list | Available from cache | Last fetched data |\n| View clock history | Available from cache | Last fetched data |\n| View training materials | Available if previously loaded | Cache |\n\n### 5.2 What Requires Connectivity\n\n| Feature | Why | Offline UX |\n|---------|-----|-----------|\n| Clock in/out | Server-side geofence validation, shift linking, audit trail | Button disabled + \"No connection\" banner. Rationale: Spanish labor law (Registro de jornada) requires accurate timestamps verified server-side. Queuing would compromise legal compliance. |\n| Start/end break | Server-side ownership check, active-break guard | Same -- disabled |\n| AI chat | SSE streaming to Anthropic API | Input disabled + \"Offline\" indicator |\n| Create leave request | Immediate confirmation needed | Could be queued (see below) |\n| Shift swap actions | Real-time coordination between employees | Disabled |\n| Push token registration | Network-only operation | Retried on reconnect |\n\n### 5.3 Offline Action Queue\n\nA limited set of actions can be safely queued when offline and replayed on reconnect:\n\n| Action | Queueable? | Conflict Risk |\n|--------|-----------|---------------|\n| Mark notification as read | Yes | None -- idempotent |\n| Update availability | Yes | Low -- overwrites |\n| Complete task checklist item | Yes | Low -- timestamp matters but not critical |\n| Create leave request | Maybe | Medium -- balance could change; show warning |\n\nThe queue is implemented in `stores/offline-queue-store.ts` and persisted to MMKV. On reconnect (detected via `@react-native-community/netinfo`), the `flush()` method processes items sequentially, dequeuing on success, incrementing `retryCount` on failure. Items are discarded after 3 retries.\n\n### 5.4 Network Status UI\n\nA persistent banner component at the top of the screen (inside the tab layout) shows connection status:\n\n- **Online:** Hidden\n- **Offline:** Red banner: \"You are offline. Some features are unavailable.\"\n- **Reconnecting:** Yellow banner: \"Reconnecting...\" with spinner\n- **Syncing:** Blue banner: \"Syncing X queued actions...\" with progress\n\n---\n\n## 6. Security Considerations\n\n### 6.1 Token Storage\n\n| Secret | Storage | Justification |\n|--------|---------|---------------|\n| Supabase access token (JWT) | `expo-secure-store` (Keychain on iOS, Keystore on Android) | Encrypted at rest by OS |\n| Supabase refresh token | `expo-secure-store` | Same |\n| Anon key | Compiled into app bundle via `EXPO_PUBLIC_` env var | Not a secret -- public by design, RLS provides security |\n\n**Never stored on device:**\n- Supabase service role key\n- Anthropic API key\n- Any server-side secrets\n\n### 6.2 Authentication Security\n\n- **Session auto-refresh:** Supabase SDK handles token refresh transparently. The refresh token is stored in SecureStore and used to obtain new access tokens before expiry.\n- **Session expiry:** Access tokens expire per Supabase project settings (default 1 hour). Refresh tokens have a configurable lifetime.\n- **Sign-out:** Calls `supabase.auth.signOut()`, which clears tokens from SecureStore, removes all Realtime channels, and clears the TanStack Query cache.\n- **No magic links / OAuth in v1:** Only email + password auth. This avoids deep link interception attacks for auth callbacks.\n\n### 6.3 Certificate Pinning\n\n**Recommendation: Do not implement certificate pinning in v1.**\n\nRationale:\n- The app communicates with Supabase's managed infrastructure and the Next.js deployment (Vercel/Cloud Run). Both use standard TLS.\n- Certificate pinning on managed services is fragile -- certificate rotation by Supabase or the CDN would break the app, requiring an emergency update.\n- For a team of 20-30 internal employees, the threat model does not justify the operational risk of pinning.\n- If required later (regulatory), implement via `expo-network` or a custom native module with backup pins.\n\n### 6.4 Biometric Unlock\n\n**Recommended for v2, optional in v1.**\n\nPattern:\n1. On first login, after successful auth, prompt: \"Enable Face ID / fingerprint to unlock?\"\n2. If accepted, store a flag in MMKV (`biometricEnabled: true`).\n3. On subsequent app launches, if the session is valid but the app was backgrounded for >5 minutes, require biometric authentication before showing the UI.\n4. Use `expo-local-authentication` for the biometric prompt.\n5. This does NOT store credentials biometrically -- it only gates UI access while the session is already valid. The Supabase session in SecureStore is the real auth.\n\nImplementation detail:\n```\nApp Foreground Event\n    │\n    ├─ biometricEnabled && (now - lastActiveTime > 5min)?\n    │   ├─ YES → show biometric prompt\n    │   │           ├─ Success → show app\n    │   │           └─ Failure → allow retry or fallback to PIN\n    │   └─ NO → show app immediately\n```\n\n### 6.5 Geolocation Security\n\nThe clock-in endpoint already validates geolocation server-side (see `src/app/api/staff/clock/route.ts`, lines 8-20). The mobile app sends lat/lng; the server computes haversine distance and flags if outside the 200m geofence.\n\nThe mobile app should:\n1. Request location permission only when the user navigates to the Clock tab.\n2. Use `expo-location` with `Accuracy.High` for clock-in.\n3. Show the geofence status visually (green checkmark if within range, yellow warning if outside).\n4. Never cache or persist location data on device.\n\n### 6.6 Data Protection\n\n- **No sensitive employee data on device:** The mobile app queries profiles with limited columns (no salary, social security number, IBAN, or PIN). The existing `getCurrentUser()` function in the web app already excludes these fields. Direct Supabase queries from mobile are restricted by RLS to the user's own data.\n- **MMKV encryption:** MMKV supports encryption. Enable it for the query cache persister to encrypt cached schedule and profile data at rest.\n- **Memory:** Sensitive data (tokens, user data) should not be logged. Disable console logging in production builds.\n- **Screenshots:** Consider disabling screenshots on the Clock tab to prevent clock-in timestamp disputes. Use `expo-screen-capture` if needed.\n\n### 6.7 API Security\n\n- All API calls use HTTPS (enforced by Supabase and the hosting provider).\n- The mobile app does not bypass RLS -- it uses the anon key, which enforces policies.\n- Rate limiting on the AI chat endpoint (20 req/min per user) applies equally to mobile and web clients.\n- Input validation happens server-side via Zod schemas on all API routes. The mobile app should also validate locally for UX (instant feedback) but the server is the authority.\n\n---\n\n## 7. Key Architectural Decisions\n\n### ADR-001: Direct Supabase Queries for Reads, Next.js API for Complex Writes\n\n**Context:** The mobile app needs to read shifts, notifications, profile, etc. The web app has both direct Supabase queries (server components) and API routes.\n\n**Decision:** Use direct Supabase client queries for reads (leveraging existing RLS) and call Next.js API routes for writes that have server-side business logic.\n\n**Consequences:**\n- (+) No API duplication. Reads are fast -- direct to Postgres.\n- (+) RLS is already configured and battle-tested.\n- (+) Realtime subscriptions work natively with direct Supabase.\n- (-) Requires a small backend change for JWT-based auth on ~5 API routes that currently only support cookies.\n- (-) Two data access patterns to understand, but the matrix in Section 3.2 makes this explicit.\n\n### ADR-002: TanStack Query + MMKV for Server State Persistence\n\n**Context:** Need offline access to schedules and profile data.\n\n**Decision:** Use TanStack Query with `gcTime: 24h` and an MMKV-based persister.\n\n**Consequences:**\n- (+) Stale-while-revalidate gives instant UI with background refresh.\n- (+) MMKV is synchronous and fast (10x faster than AsyncStorage).\n- (+) 24h cache means the app is usable for a full day without connectivity.\n- (-) Cache can become stale. Realtime subscriptions mitigate this when online.\n\n### ADR-003: No Service Role Key on Mobile\n\n**Context:** Some web API routes use `createAdminClient()` to bypass RLS.\n\n**Decision:** The mobile app never has access to the service role key. All operations that require admin access must go through the Next.js API routes.\n\n**Consequences:**\n- (+) Eliminates the most severe security risk (compromised service role key = full database access).\n- (+) Follows principle of least privilege.\n- (-) Some operations require an extra network hop through the Next.js API.\n\n### ADR-004: Clock In/Out Not Queueable Offline\n\n**Context:** Should clock-in/out work offline with eventual sync?\n\n**Decision:** No. Clock in/out requires connectivity.\n\n**Consequences:**\n- (+) Spanish labor law (Real Decreto-ley 8/2019) requires accurate, tamper-resistant time records. Server-generated timestamps are the legal authority.\n- (+) Geofence validation prevents remote clock-in fraud.\n- (+) No clock-in disputes from timestamp drift.\n- (-) Employees cannot clock in during network outages. Mitigation: the restaurant has WiFi; cellular is reliable in El Arenal. Manager can create manual clock records via the web app if needed.\n\n### ADR-005: i18next Instead of next-intl\n\n**Context:** The web app uses `next-intl`. React Native cannot use `next-intl`.\n\n**Decision:** Use `i18next` + `react-i18next` with the same 4 locales (en, nl, es, de).\n\n**Consequences:**\n- (+) i18next is the React Native standard for i18n.\n- (+) Translation JSON files can share keys with the web app's `src/i18n/messages/` -- not identical files, but the same key naming conventions.\n- (-) Two i18n systems to maintain. Mitigation: the mobile app has fewer screens (~20) than the web app (~50+), so the translation surface is smaller. Mobile-specific namespaces (home, clock, chat, schedule, leave, tasks, settings) reuse many keys.\n\n### ADR-006: SSE Streaming for AI Chat (Not WebSocket)\n\n**Context:** The web app uses SSE for AI chat streaming. The mobile app needs the same capability.\n\n**Decision:** Use the same SSE endpoint (`POST /api/ai/chat/stream`) from the mobile app. Parse SSE events using the same `parseSSEBuffer` logic ported to the `use-chat-stream` hook.\n\n**Consequences:**\n- (+) Zero backend changes for AI chat.\n- (+) Same 11 event types, same tool/sub-agent patterns.\n- (-) SSE over `fetch` in React Native requires `TextDecoder` polyfill and manual stream reading. This is well-documented and supported by Expo.\n\n---\n\n## Appendix A: Backend Changes Required\n\nThe mobile app requires minimal backend changes. Here is the exhaustive list:\n\n### A.1 JWT Auth Support for API Routes (REQUIRED)\n\nCreate a utility function `createClientFromRequest(request: NextRequest)` that:\n1. Checks for `Authorization: Bearer <token>` header.\n2. If present, creates a Supabase client with `supabase.auth.getUser(token)`.\n3. Falls back to cookie-based auth for web requests.\n\nAffected routes (those called by mobile app):\n- `POST /api/staff/clock` (clock in/out)\n- `POST /api/staff/clock/break` (start/end break)\n- `PATCH /api/staff/leave/[id]` (cancel leave)\n- `POST /api/ai/chat/stream` (AI chat)\n- `POST /api/notifications/subscribe` (push registration)\n- `GET /api/notifications/subscribe` (list subscriptions)\n- `DELETE /api/notifications/subscribe` (unsubscribe)\n\n### A.2 Push Notification for Mobile (OPTIONAL, v2)\n\nThe existing `push_subscriptions` table stores Web Push endpoints. For mobile push via Expo Notifications:\n1. Add a `platform` column to `push_subscriptions` (`'web' | 'ios' | 'android'`).\n2. Add an `expo_push_token` column.\n3. The notification sending logic (currently Web Push API) needs a branch for Expo Push API.\n\n### A.3 Deep Link URLs in Notification Data\n\nUpdate the `create_notification` SQL function and triggers to include mobile-compatible deep links in the `data` JSONB column. The current `action_url` field uses web paths like `/staff/schedule`. Add a `mobile_url` field with the `cheers://` scheme equivalent.\n\n---\n\n## Appendix B: Shared Type Strategy\n\nThe web app's `src/types/index.ts` (1543 lines) defines all domain types. The mobile app needs a subset of these types.\n\n**Short-term (v1):** Copy the relevant types into `types/index.ts` in the mobile repo. The mobile app uses approximately 30% of the web app's types (Profile, Employee, Shift, ClockInOut, ClockBreak, LeaveRequest, LeaveEntitlement, Notification, StaffTask, StaffTaskItem, SwapRequest, ChatMessage, etc.).\n\n**Long-term (v2+):** Extract shared types into a `@grandcafe/types` package published to a private npm registry. Both the web app and mobile app import from this package. This also includes shared Zod schemas for validation.\n\n---\n\n## Appendix C: Environment Variables\n\n```env\n# .env.example for mobile app\nEXPO_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL=https://dedxavxwzlchapamgjov.supabase.co\nEXPO_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY=eyJ...\nEXPO_PUBLIC_API_URL=https://grandcafe-cheers.vercel.app\nEXPO_PUBLIC_GEOFENCE_LAT=39.5021\nEXPO_PUBLIC_GEOFENCE_LNG=2.7392\nEXPO_PUBLIC_GEOFENCE_RADIUS=200\n```\n\nNo server-side secrets. No service role key. No Anthropic API key.\n\n---\n\n## Appendix D: Key Files Referenced in This Document\n\nThese files from the existing web app codebase informed the architecture:\n\n- [Supabase Client Setup](#4-supabase-client-setup)\n5. [State Management Architecture](#5-state-management-architecture)\n6. [Offline Strategy](#6-offline-strategy)\n7. [Security Considerations](#7-security-considerations)\n8. [Data Flow Diagrams](#8-data-flow-diagrams)\n9. [Key Design Decisions (ADRs)](#9-key-design-decisions-adrs)\n\n---\n\n## 1. Executive Summary\n\nThis document defines the architecture for a React Native mobile app targeting the 20-30 mostly Dutch staff members of GrandCafe Cheers, a seasonal beachfront restaurant in El Arenal, Mallorca. The app connects to the **existing** Supabase backend (PostgreSQL 17, 120+ tables, full RLS) -- no API duplication. The web management platform (`/Users/lr0y/Movies/claude-quickstarts-main/grandcafe-cheers-platform/app/grandcafe-cheers-app`) continues to serve as the admin/manager dashboard; the mobile app is employee-focused.\n\n**Core use cases:** View schedule, clock in/out with geolocation, receive push notifications, request leave, swap shifts, complete tasks, submit post-shift surveys, team chat (via AI assistant), and view profile/payslips.\n\n**Tech stack:** Expo SDK 53 (managed workflow) | Expo Router v4 | NativeWind v4 | TanStack Query v5 | Zustand v5 + MMKV | Supabase JS v2 with SecureStore | Expo Notifications | i18next + react-i18next\n\n---\n\n## 2. Project Structure\n\n```\ngrandcafe-cheers-mobile/\n├── app/                              # Expo Router file-based routing\n│   ├── _layout.tsx                   # Root layout: providers, fonts, splash\n│   ├── index.tsx                     # Entry redirect: auth check -> /login or /(tabs)\n│   │\n│   ├── (auth)/                       # Unauthenticated routes (no tabs)\n│   │   ├── _layout.tsx               # Auth layout: no header, centered\n│   │   ├── login.tsx                 # Email + password login\n│   │   └── forgot-password.tsx       # Password reset flow\n│   │\n│   ├── (tabs)/                       # Authenticated tab navigator\n│   │   ├── _layout.tsx               # Tab bar layout: 5 tabs, auth guard\n│   │   │\n│   │   ├── (home)/                   # Tab 1: Home\n│   │   │   ├── _layout.tsx           # Stack navigator for Home tab\n│   │   │   ├── index.tsx             # Dashboard: today's shift, alerts, tasks\n│   │   │   ├── notifications.tsx     # Notification center\n│   │   │   └── notification/[id].tsx # Single notification detail\n│   │   │\n│   │   ├── (schedule)/               # Tab 2: Schedule\n│   │   │   ├── _layout.tsx           # Stack navigator for Schedule tab\n│   │   │   ├── index.tsx             # Weekly schedule view (own shifts)\n│   │   │   ├── shift/[id].tsx        # Shift detail (times, notes, team)\n│   │   │   ├── availability.tsx      # Set availability calendar\n│   │   │   ├── swap-requests.tsx     # List swap requests\n│   │   │   └── swap-request/[id].tsx # Swap request detail + accept/reject\n│   │   │\n│   │   ├── clock.tsx                 # Tab 3: Clock (center, prominent)\n│   │   │                             # Single screen: big button, geolocation,\n│   │   │                             # break toggle, shift summary\n│   │   │\n│   │   ├── (chat)/                   # Tab 4: Chat (AI Assistant)\n│   │   │   ├── _layout.tsx           # Stack navigator for Chat tab\n│   │   │   ├── index.tsx             # Conversation list\n│   │   │   └── conversation/[id].tsx # Chat thread with SSE streaming\n│   │   │\n│   │   └── (more)/                   # Tab 5: More\n│   │       ├── _layout.tsx           # Stack navigator for More tab\n│   │       ├── index.tsx             # Menu grid: profile, leave, tasks, etc.\n│   │       ├── profile.tsx           # View/edit own profile\n│   │       ├── leave.tsx             # Leave balance + request list\n│   │       ├── tasks.tsx             # My assigned tasks\n│   │       ├── task/[id].tsx         # Task detail + checklist items\n│   │       ├── training.tsx          # Training assignments\n│   │       ├── training/[code].tsx   # Training course viewer\n│   │       ├── hours-summary.tsx     # Monthly hours/clock history\n│   │       ├── documents.tsx         # Pay slips, contracts (when available)\n│   │       ├── settings.tsx          # Language, theme, notification prefs\n│   │       └── about.tsx             # App version, legal\n│   │\n│   ├── (modals)/                     # Modal routes (presented as modals)\n│   │   ├── _layout.tsx               # Modal presentation (transparentModal)\n│   │   ├── leave-request.tsx         # Create leave request form\n│   │   ├── swap-create.tsx           # Create swap request form\n│   │   ├── shift-survey.tsx          # Post-shift survey (after clock-out)\n│   │   └── task-complete.tsx         # Task completion with notes\n│   │\n│   └── +not-found.tsx                # 404 fallback\n│\n├── components/                       # Shared UI components\n│   ├── ui/                           # Design system primitives\n│   │   ├── button.tsx\n│   │   ├── card.tsx\n│   │   ├── input.tsx\n│   │   ├── text.tsx\n│   │   ├── badge.tsx\n│   │   ├── avatar.tsx\n│   │   ├── bottom-sheet.tsx\n│   │   ├── loading-spinner.tsx\n│   │   ├── empty-state.tsx\n│   │   ├── error-boundary.tsx\n│   │   ├── pull-to-refresh.tsx\n│   │   └── haptic-button.tsx         # Button with haptic feedback\n│   │\n│   ├── home/                         # Home tab components\n│   │   ├── today-shift-card.tsx\n│   │   ├── alerts-banner.tsx\n│   │   ├── quick-actions.tsx\n│   │   └── upcoming-events.tsx\n│   │\n│   ├── schedule/                     #
