Clock tab components\n│   │   ├── clock-button.tsx          # Large animated clock in/out button\n│   │   ├── break-toggle.tsx\n│   │   ├── shift-timer.tsx           # Live elapsed time\n│   │   ├── geolocation-indicator.tsx\n│   │   └── clock-summary.tsx         # Post clock-out summary\n│   │\n│   ├── chat/                         # Chat tab components\n│   │   ├── message-bubble.tsx\n│   │   ├── streaming-text.tsx\n│   │   ├── tool-indicator.tsx\n│   │   ├── pending-action.tsx\n│   │   ├── conversation-item.tsx\n│   │   └── chat-input.tsx\n│   │\n│   ├── tasks/                        # Task components\n│   │   ├── task-card.tsx\n│   │   ├── checklist-item.tsx\n│   │   └── task-priority-badge.tsx\n│   │\n│   ├── leave/                        # Leave components\n│   │   ├── leave-balance-card.tsx\n│   │   ├── leave-request-card.tsx\n│   │   └── leave-calendar.tsx\n│   │\n│   └── providers/                    # Context providers\n│       ├── auth-provider.tsx         # Supabase auth state, session refresh\n│       ├── query-provider.tsx        # TanStack QueryClientProvider\n│       ├── realtime-provider.tsx     # Supabase Realtime subscriptions\n│       ├── notification-provider.tsx # Push notification handler\n│       └── theme-provider.tsx        # NativeWind theme (light/dark)\n│\n├── lib/                              # Core library code\n│   ├── supabase/\n│   │   ├── client.ts                 # Supabase client (anon key + SecureStore)\n│   │   └── realtime.ts              # Typed channel subscriptions\n│   │\n│   ├── api/                          # API layer (thin wrappers over Supabase)\n│   │   ├── auth.ts                   # signIn, signOut, resetPassword\n│   │   ├── shifts.ts                 # getMyShifts, getShiftById\n│   │   ├── clock.ts                  # clockIn, clockOut, startBreak, endBreak\n│   │   ├── leave.ts                  # getLeaveBalance, createLeaveRequest\n│   │   ├── swap.ts                   # createSwapRequest, respondToSwap\n│   │   ├── tasks.ts                  # getMyTasks, completeTaskItem\n│   │   ├── notifications.ts         # getNotifications, markAsRead\n│   │   ├── profile.ts               # getProfile, updateProfile\n│   │   ├── surveys.ts               # submitShiftSurvey\n│   │   ├── training.ts              # getAssignments, getGuideContent\n│   │   └── chat.ts                   # SSE stream handler for AI chat\n│   │\n│   ├── utils/\n│   │   ├── date.ts                   # date-fns helpers, timezone (Europe/Madrid)\n│   │   ├── format.ts                 # Currency, hours formatting\n│   │   ├── geolocation.ts           # Location permission, haversine distance\n│   │   ├── haptics.ts               # Haptic feedback wrappers\n│   │   └── network.ts               # NetInfo helpers, connectivity check\n│   │\n│   └── notifications/\n│       ├── register.ts              # Expo push token registration\n│       ├── handler.ts               # Foreground/background notification handler\n│       └── channels.ts             # Notification channel definitions (Android)\n│\n├── hooks/                            # Custom React hooks\n│   ├── use-auth.ts                   # Auth state from AuthProvider\n│   ├── use-my-shifts.ts              # TanStack Query: own shifts for date range\n│   ├── use-today-shift.ts            # TanStack Query: today's shift\n│   ├── use-clock-status.ts           # TanStack Query: current clock record\n│   ├── use-notifications.ts          # TanStack Query: notification list\n│   ├── use-leave-balance.ts          # TanStack Query: leave entitlements\n│   ├── use-my-tasks.ts               # TanStack Query: assigned tasks\n│   ├── use-profile.ts                # TanStack Query: own profile + employee\n│   ├── use-ai-chat.ts                # SSE streaming chat hook (mobile port)\n│   ├── use-geolocation.ts            # Location with permission handling\n│   ├── use-network.ts                # Online/offline detection\n│   └── use-realtime.ts               # Generic Supabase Realtime subscription\n│\n├── stores/                           # Zustand stores (client-only state)\n│   ├── app-store.ts                  # locale, theme, onboarding state\n│   ├── clock-store.ts                # Optimistic clock state during offline\n│   └── draft-store.ts               # Unsent form drafts (leave, swap, survey)\n│\n├── i18n/                             # Internationalization\n│   ├── config.ts                     # i18next init with languageDetector\n│   ├── en/                           # English translations\n│   │   ├── common.json\n│   │   ├── home.json\n│   │   ├── schedule.json\n│   │   ├── clock.json\n│   │   ├── chat.json\n│   │   ├── leave.json\n│   │   ├── tasks.json\n│   │   └── settings.json\n│   ├── nl/                           # Dutch translations (primary)\n│   ├── es/                           # Spanish translations\n│   └── de/                           # German translations\n│\n├── constants/\n│   ├── theme.ts                      # Colors (OKLch), spacing, typography\n│   ├── config.ts                     # Supabase URL, app version, feature flags\n│   ├── geofence.ts                  # Restaurant lat/lng, radius (200m)\n│   └── query-keys.ts               # TanStack Query key factory\n│\n├── types/\n│   ├── index.ts                      # Shared with web app (Profile, Shift, etc.)\n│   ├── navigation.ts                 # Expo Router typed routes\n│   └── database.ts                   # Auto-generated Supabase types (shared)\n│\n├── assets/\n│   ├── images/                       # App icons, splash, illustrations\n│   ├── fonts/                        # Custom fonts (if any)\n│   └── animations/                   # Lottie files (clock animation, success)\n│\n├── app.json                          # Expo config\n├── eas.json                          # EAS Build config (dev, preview, production)\n├── tailwind.config.ts                # NativeWind Tailwind config\n├── tsconfig.json                     # TypeScript strict mode\n├── babel.config.js                   # Babel for NativeWind\n├── metro.config.js                   # Metro bundler config\n├── .env.example                      # Environment variable template\n└── CLAUDE.md                         # AI assistant instructions for this repo\n```\n\n### Key Design Decisions for Structure\n\n**Shared types with the web app.** The `types/index.ts` file should be a direct copy (or symlinked) from the web app at `/Users/lr0y/Movies/claude-quickstarts-main/grandcafe-cheers-platform/app/grandcafe-cheers-app/src/types/index.ts`. The same TypeScript interfaces (`Profile`, `Employee`, `Shift`, `ClockInOut`, `LeaveRequest`, `StaffTask`, etc.) are used without modification. Similarly, `types/database.ts` is generated from the same Supabase instance via `supabase gen types typescript`.\n\n**API layer pattern.** Each file in `lib/api/` contains pure functions that call Supabase directly (no Next.js API route proxying for reads). Write operations that require server-side logic (e.g., clock-in with geolocation validation, survey submission) call the existing Next.js API routes at the web app's deployed URL. This avoids duplicating business logic while keeping reads fast.\n\n**Translation namespace alignment.** The i18n namespaces intentionally differ from the web app's 19 namespaces. The mobile app uses only 8 namespaces scoped to its features. However, translation keys for shared concepts (roles, statuses, errors) are kept identical to the web app's `common.json` so that translators work from a single source of truth.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Navigation Architecture\n\n### 3.1 Route Map\n\n```\n/                                 → Redirect based on auth state\n├── (auth)/\n│   ├── login                     → Email/password sign-in\n│   └── forgot-password           → Reset password via email\n│\n├── (tabs)/\n│   ├── (home)/\n│   │   ├── index                 → Today's shift, alerts, quick actions\n│   │   ├── notifications         → All notifications (paginated)\n│   │   └── notification/[id]     → Single notification detail\n│   │\n│   ├── (schedule)/\n│   │   ├── index                 → Week view calendar (own shifts)\n│   │   ├── shift/[id]            → Shift detail: times, team, notes\n│   │   ├── availability          → Mark availability per date\n│   │   ├── swap-requests         → My swap requests (incoming + outgoing)\n│   │   └── swap-request/[id]     → Accept/reject swap\n│   │\n│   ├── clock                     → Clock in/out + break toggle\n│   │\n│   ├── (chat)/\n│   │   ├── index                 → Conversation list\n│   │   └── conversation/[id]     → Chat thread (SSE streaming)\n│   │\n│   └── (more)/\n│       ├── index                 → Menu grid\n│       ├── profile               → View/edit profile\n│       ├── leave                 → Leave balance + history\n│       ├── tasks                 → My tasks\n│       ├── task/[id]             → Task detail + checklist\n│       ├── training              → Training list\n│       ├── training/[code]       → Training viewer\n│       ├── hours-summary         → Monthly hours\n│       ├── documents             → Documents list\n│       ├── settings              → App settings\n│       └── about                 → Version + legal\n│\n├── (modals)/\n│   ├── leave-request             → Create leave request (modal)\n│   ├── swap-create               → Create swap request (modal)\n│   ├── shift-survey              → Post-shift survey (modal)\n│   └── task-complete             → Complete task with notes (modal)\n│\n└── +not-found                    → 404 fallback\n```\n\n### 3.2 Tab Bar Configuration\n\n```typescript\n// app/(tabs)/_layout.tsx\n\nimport { Tabs } from 'expo-router'\nimport { Home, Calendar, MessageCircle, MoreHorizontal } from 'lucide-react-native'\nimport { ClockTabIcon } from '@/components/clock/clock-tab-icon'\n\nexport default function TabLayout() {\n  return (\n    <Tabs\n      screenOptions={{\n        tabBarActiveTintColor: '#F97316',  // Cheers orange\n        tabBarInactiveTintColor: '#9CA3AF',\n        headerShown: false,\n      }}\n    >\n      <Tabs.Screen\n        name=\"(home)\"\n        options={{\n          title: t('tabs.home'),\n          tabBarIcon: ({ color, size }) => <Home color={color} size={size} />,\n        }}\n      />\n      <Tabs.Screen\n        name=\"(schedule)\"\n        options={{\n          title: t('tabs.schedule'),\n          tabBarIcon: ({ color, size }) => <Calendar color={color} size={size} />,\n        }}\n      />\n      <Tabs.Screen\n        name=\"clock\"\n        options={{\n          title: t('tabs.clock'),\n          tabBarIcon: ({ color, focused }) => (\n            <ClockTabIcon focused={focused} color={color} />\n          ),\n          // Prominent center button with custom styling\n          tabBarItemStyle: { marginTop: -10 },\n        }}\n      />\n      <Tabs.Screen\n        name=\"(chat)\"\n        options={{\n          title: t('tabs.chat'),\n          tabBarIcon: ({ color, size }) => <MessageCircle color={color} size={size} />,\n        }}\n      />\n      <Tabs.Screen\n        name=\"(more)\"\n        options={{\n          title: t('tabs.more'),\n          tabBarIcon: ({ color, size }) => <MoreHorizontal color={color} size={size} />,\n        }}\n      />\n    </Tabs>\n  )\n}\n```\n\n### 3.3 Auth Guard\n\n```typescript\n// app/(tabs)/_layout.tsx (auth guard portion)\n\nimport { Redirect } from 'expo-router'\nimport { useAuth } from '@/hooks/use-auth'\n\nexport default function TabLayout() {\n  const { session, isLoading } = useAuth()\n\n  if (isLoading) return <SplashScreen />\n  if (!session) return <Redirect href=\"/(auth)/login\" />\n\n  return <Tabs>...</Tabs>\n}\n```\n\nThe root `_layout.tsx` wraps everything in providers and does NOT perform auth checks -- that responsibility belongs to the `(tabs)/_layout.tsx` so that auth routes remain accessible.\n\n### 3.4 Deep Linking Schema\n\n```json\n// app.json (partial)\n{\n  \"expo\": {\n    \"scheme\": \"cheers\",\n    \"ios\": {\n      \"associatedDomains\": [\"applinks:grandcafe-cheers.app\"]\n    },\n    \"android\": {\n      \"intentFilters\": [{\n        \"action\": \"VIEW\",\n        \"autoVerify\": true,\n        \"data\": [{ \"scheme\": \"https\", \"host\": \"grandcafe-cheers.app\", \"pathPrefix\": \"/m\" }]\n      }]\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Deep link mapping (for push notifications):**\n\n| Push Notification Type | Deep Link | Screen |\n|---|---|---|\n| `shift_assigned` | `cheers://schedule/shift/{shift_id}` | Shift detail |\n| `shift_changed` | `cheers://schedule/shift/{shift_id}` | Shift detail |\n| `swap_requested` | `cheers://schedule/swap-request/{swap_id}` | Swap detail |\n| `swap_approved` | `cheers://schedule/swap-requests` | Swap list |\n| `swap_rejected` | `cheers://schedule/swap-requests` | Swap list |\n| `clock_reminder` | `cheers://clock` | Clock screen |\n| `schedule_published` | `cheers://schedule` | Schedule view |\n| `shift_feedback_received` | `cheers://more/hours-summary` | Hours summary |\n| `system` | `cheers://home/notifications` | Notifications |\n\n### 3.5 Modal Routes\n\nModals are defined in `app/(modals)/_layout.tsx` using `presentation: 'modal'` (iOS sheet) or `transparentModal` for Android bottom-sheet behavior:\n\n```typescript\n// app/(modals)/_layout.tsx\nimport { Stack } from 'expo-router'\n\nexport default function ModalLayout() {\n  return (\n    <Stack\n      screenOptions={{\n        presentation: 'modal',\n        headerShown: true,\n        gestureEnabled: true,\n      }}\n    />\n  )\n}\n```\n\nModals are triggered from anywhere via `router.push('/(modals)/leave-request')`.\n\n---\n\n## 4. Supabase Client Setup\n\n### 4.1 Client Initialization with SecureStore\n\n```typescript\n// lib/supabase/client.ts\n\nimport 'react-native-url-polyfill/auto'\nimport AsyncStorage from '@react-native-async-storage/async-storage'\nimport * as SecureStore from 'expo-secure-store'\nimport { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js'\nimport { SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_ANON_KEY } from '@/constants/config'\nimport type { Database } from '@/types/database'\n\n/**\n * Supabase auth storage adapter using SecureStore for tokens\n * and AsyncStorage for non-sensitive data.\n *\n * SecureStore has a 2048-byte limit per item on some platforms,\n * so we split the session if needed.\n */\nconst secureStoreAdapter = {\n  async getItem(key: string): Promise<string | null> {\n    try {\n      return await SecureStore.getItemAsync(key)\n    } catch {\n      // Fallback for keys that exceed SecureStore limits\n      return await AsyncStorage.getItem(key)\n    }\n  },\n  async setItem(key: string, value: string): Promise<void> {\n    try {\n      await SecureStore.setItemAsync(key, value)\n    } catch {\n      // Supabase session can exceed 2KB; fall back to AsyncStorage\n      await AsyncStorage.setItem(key, value)\n    }\n  },\n  async removeItem(key: string): Promise<void> {\n    try {\n      await SecureStore.deleteItemAsync(key)\n    } catch {\n      await AsyncStorage.removeItem(key)\n    }\n  },\n}\n\nexport const supabase = createClient<Database>(\n  SUPABASE_URL,\n  SUPABASE_ANON_KEY,\n  {\n    auth: {\n      storage: secureStoreAdapter,\n      autoRefreshToken: true,\n      persistSession: true,\n      detectSessionInUrl: false,  // No browser URL in React Native\n    },\n    realtime: {\n      params: {\n        eventsPerSecond: 10,\n      },\n    },\n  }\n)\n```\n\n**Critical:** The mobile app uses the **anon key** only. The service role key (`SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY`) is NEVER included in the mobile binary. All data access is governed by the existing RLS policies.\n\n### 4.2 Reusing Existing RLS Policies\n\nThe existing RLS policies (defined across 69 migrations, key files: `002_staff_rls_policies.sql`, `017_schedule_plans_leave.sql`, `023_kiosk_clock_system.sql`, etc.) already support the mobile app's access patterns because they are user-scoped:\n\n| Table | Staff (waiter/bar/kitchen/dj) Access | Manager+ Access |\n|---|---|---|\n| `profiles` | Own record | All records |\n| `employees` | Own record | All records |\n| `shifts` | Own shifts (via employee_id match) | All shifts |\n| `clock_in_out` | Own records | All records |\n| `clock_breaks` | Own breaks (via clock_record_id -> employee_id) | All breaks |\n| `availability` | Own availability | All availability |\n| `shift_swap_requests` | Requests involving self | All requests |\n| `leave_requests` | Own requests | All requests |\n| `leave_entitlements` | Own entitlements | All entitlements |\n| `notifications` | Own notifications (user_id = auth.uid()) | Own only |\n| `staff_tasks` | Assigned tasks | All tasks |\n| `shift_survey_responses` | Own surveys | All surveys |\n| `schedule_plans` | Published plans only | All plans |\n| `ai_conversations` | Own conversations | Own only |\n| `ai_conversation_messages` | Own messages | Own only |\n\nNo new RLS policies are required. The `auth.uid()` function works identically whether the JWT comes from a web session cookie or a mobile access token.\n\n### 4.3 API Call Patterns\n\n**Pattern A: Direct Supabase Query (reads, simple writes)**\n\nUse for any operation where the existing RLS policies provide correct authorization and no server-side business logic is needed:\n\n```typescript\n// lib/api/shifts.ts\n\nimport { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase/client'\nimport type { ShiftWithEmployee } from '@/types'\n\nexport async function getMyShifts(\n  startDate: string,\n  endDate: string\n): Promise<ShiftWithEmployee[]> {\n  const { data, error } = await supabase\n    .from('shifts')\n    .select(`\n      *,\n      employee:employees(\n        id,\n        profile:profiles(id, full_name, role)\n      )\n    `)\n    .gte('date', startDate)\n    .lte('date', endDate)\n    .order('date', { ascending: true })\n    .order('start_time', { ascending: true })\n\n  if (error) throw new Error(error.message)\n  return data as ShiftWithEmployee[]\n}\n```\n\nRLS on `shifts` already filters to own shifts for non-manager roles, so no employee_id filter is needed in the query.\n\n**Pattern B: Next.js API Route (writes with server-side logic)**\n\nUse when the operation involves business logic that runs server-side (geolocation validation, auto-linking to shift, grace period checks, audit logging):\n\n```typescript\n// lib/api/clock.ts\n\nimport { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase/client'\nimport { WEB_APP_URL } from '@/constants/config'\n\nexport async function clockIn(options: {\n  latitude?: number\n  longitude?: number\n}): Promise<ClockInResponse> {\n  // Get the current session token\n  const { data: { session } } = await supabase.auth.getSession()\n  if (!session) throw new Error('Not authenticated')\n\n  const response = await fetch(`${WEB_APP_URL}/api/staff/clock?action=in`, {\n    method: 'POST',\n    headers: {\n      'Content-Type': 'application/json',\n      'Authorization': `Bearer ${session.access_token}`,\n    },\n    body: JSON.stringify({\n      latitude: options.latitude,\n      longitude: options.longitude,\n    }),\n  })\n\n  if (!response.ok) {\n    const error = await response.json()\n    throw new Error(error.error || 'Clock-in failed')\n  }\n\n  return response.json()\n}\n```\n\n**When to use which pattern:**\n\n| Operation | Pattern | Reason |\n|---|---|---|\n| Read own shifts | Direct Supabase | RLS handles scoping |\n| Read notifications | Direct Supabase | RLS: user_id = auth.uid() |\n| Read leave balance | Direct Supabase | RLS handles scoping |\n| Clock in/out | Next.js API | Geolocation validation, shift auto-linking, audit log |\n| Start/end break | Next.js API | Active break checks, auto-close logic |\n| Submit leave request | Next.js API | Ownership validation, entitlement checks |\n| Submit swap request | Direct Supabase (INSERT) | RLS enforces requested_by = own employee_id |\n| Accept/reject swap | Direct Supabase (UPDATE) | RLS allows updates on own swap requests |\n| Mark notification read | Direct Supabase (UPDATE) | RLS: user_id = auth.uid() |\n| Submit shift survey | Next.js API | Anomaly detection, AI analysis trigger |\n| AI chat stream | Next.js API (SSE) | Tool execution, model routing, prompt caching |\n| Update own profile | Direct Supabase (UPDATE) | RLS allows own profile updates |\n| Complete task item | Direct Supabase (UPDATE) | RLS allows assigned task updates |\n\n### 4.4 Auth Flow (Next.js API Route Authentication)\n\nThe existing Next.js API routes use cookie-based auth (`@supabase/ssr`). The mobile app does not have cookies, so it passes the JWT in the `Authorization` header. The Next.js API routes need a small adjustment to also accept Bearer tokens:\n\n```typescript\n// Existing: src/lib/utils/auth.ts uses createClient() which reads cookies\n// For mobile support, the API routes should check Authorization header as fallback\n\n// Option: Add a lightweight middleware or modify requireAuth():\n// 1. Check cookie-based session first (web)\n// 2. If no cookie session, check Authorization: Bearer <token> header (mobile)\n// 3. Verify token with supabase.auth.getUser(token)\n```\n\n**Recommended approach:** Create a `createClientFromRequest(request: NextRequest)` helper that checks for the `Authorization` header and creates a Supabase client with the provided token. This is a single-file change to the web app and does not affect existing web functionality.\n\n### 4.5 Realtime Subscriptions\n\n```typescript\n// lib/supabase/realtime.ts\n\nimport { supabase } from './client'\nimport type { RealtimeChannel } from '@supabase/supabase-js'\n\n/**\n * Subscribe to real-time changes on tables published to supabase_realtime.\n * Published tables (from migrations):\n * - shifts (002)\n * - shift_swap_requests (002)\n * - clock_in_out (002)\n * - clock_breaks (023)\n * - notifications (003)\n */\nexport function subscribeToShiftChanges(\n  employeeId: string,\n  onShiftChange: (payload: unknown) => void\n): RealtimeChannel {\n  return supabase\n    .channel(`shifts:employee:${employeeId}`)\n    .on(\n      'postgres_changes',\n      {\n        event: '*',\n        schema: 'public',\n        table: 'shifts',\n        filter: `employee_id=eq.${employeeId}`,\n      },\n      onShiftChange\n    )\n    .subscribe()\n}\n\nexport function subscribeToNotifications(\n  userId: string,\n  onNotification: (payload: unknown) => void\n): RealtimeChannel {\n  return supabase\n    .channel(`notifications:user:${userId}`)\n    .on(\n      'postgres_changes',\n      {\n        event: 'INSERT',\n        schema: 'public',\n        table: 'notifications',\n        filter: `user_id=eq.${userId}`,\n      },\n      onNotification\n    )\n    .subscribe()\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. State Management Architecture\n\n### 5.1 Architecture Overview\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│                    React Components                      │\n├─────────────┬───────────────────────┬───────────────────┤\n│  Zustand    │   TanStack Query      │   Supabase        │\n│  Stores     │   (Server State)      │   Realtime        │\n│             │                       │                   │\n│  - locale   │  - shifts             │  - shift changes  │\n│  - theme    │  - profile            │  - notifications  │\n│  - selected │  - clock status       │  - clock updates  │\n│    date     │  - notifications      │  - swap requests  │\n│  - offline  │  - leave balance      │                   │\n│    queue    │  - tasks              │                   │\n│  - drafts   │  - conversations      │                   │\n│             │  - training           │                   │\n├─────────────┴───────────────────────┴───────────────────┤\n│                     MMKV Persistence                     │\n│  (Zustand persist middleware + TanStack Query persister) │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n### 5.2 Zustand Stores (Client State)\n\n```typescript\n// stores/app-store.ts\n\nimport { create } from 'zustand'\nimport { persist, createJSONStorage } from 'zustand/middleware'\nimport { mmkvStorage } from './mmkv-storage'\n\ninterface AppState {\n  // Preferences\n  readonly locale: 'en' | 'nl' | 'es' | 'de'\n  readonly theme: 'light' | 'dark' | 'system'\n  readonly hasCompletedOnboarding: boolean\n\n  // UI state\n  readonly selectedScheduleDate: string // YYYY-MM-DD\n  readonly lastViewedConversationId: string | null\n\n  // Actions (return new state, never mutate)\n  setLocale: (locale: AppState['locale']) => void\n  setTheme: (theme: AppState['theme']) => void\n  setOnboardingComplete: () => void\n  setSelectedDate: (date: string) => void\n  setLastConversation: (id: string | null) => void\n}\n\nexport const useAppStore = create<AppState>()(\n  persist(\n    (set) => ({\n      locale: 'nl',  // Default for Dutch staff\n      theme: 'system',\n      hasCompletedOnboarding: false,\n      selectedScheduleDate: new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10),\n      lastViewedConversationId: null,\n\n      setLocale: (locale) => set({ locale }),\n      setTheme: (theme) => set({ theme }),\n      setOnboardingComplete: () => set({ hasCompletedOnboarding: true }),\n      setSelectedDate: (date) => set({ selectedScheduleDate: date }),\n      setLastConversation: (id) => set({ lastViewedConversationId: id }),\n    }),\n    {\n      name: 'cheers-app-store',\n      storage: createJSONStorage(() => mmkvStorage),\n    }\n  )\n)\n```\n\n```typescript\n// stores/clock-store.ts\n\nimport { create } from 'zustand'\nimport { persist, createJSONStorage } from 'zustand/middleware'\nimport { mmkvStorage } from './mmkv-storage'\n\ninterface ClockState {\n  // Optimistic state while offline or waiting for server\n  readonly pendingClockIn: {\n    timestamp: string\n    latitude?: number\n    longitude?: number\n  } | null\n  readonly pendingClockOut: {\n    clockRecordId: string\n    timestamp: string\n  } | null\n\n  setPendingClockIn: (data: ClockState['pendingClockIn']) => void\n  setPendingClockOut: (data: ClockState['pendingClockOut']) => void\n  clearPending: () => void\n}\n\nexport const useClockStore = create<ClockState>()(\n  persist(\n    (set) => ({\n      pendingClockIn: null,\n      pendingClockOut: null,\n\n      setPendingClockIn: (data) => set({ pendingClockIn: data }),\n      setPendingClockOut: (data) => set({ pendingClockOut: data }),\n      clearPending: () => set({ pendingClockIn: null, pendingClockOut: null }),\n    }),\n    {\n      name: 'cheers-clock-store',\n      storage: createJSONStorage(() => mmkvStorage),\n    }\n  )\n)\n```\n\n```typescript\n// stores/draft-store.ts\n\nimport { create } from 'zustand'\nimport { persist, createJSONStorage } from 'zustand/middleware'\nimport { mmkvStorage } from './mmkv-storage'\n\ninterface DraftState {\n  readonly leaveRequestDraft: Partial<CreateLeaveRequestInput> | null\n  readonly swapRequestDraft: { shiftId: string; offeredTo: string; reason: string } | null\n  readonly surveyDraft: { clockRecordId: string; rating: number; feedback: string } | null\n\n  setLeaveRequestDraft: (draft: DraftState['leaveRequestDraft']) => void\n  setSwapRequestDraft: (draft: DraftState['swapRequestDraft']) => void\n  setSurveyDraft: (draft: DraftState['surveyDraft']) => void\n  clearDraft: (type: 'leave' | 'swap' | 'survey') => void\n}\n\nexport const useDraftStore = create<DraftState>()(\n  persist(\n    (set) => ({\n      leaveRequestDraft: null,\n      swapRequestDraft: null,\n      surveyDraft: null,\n\n      setLeaveRequestDraft: (draft) => set({ leaveRequestDraft: draft }),\n      setSwapRequestDraft: (draft) => set({ swapRequestDraft: draft }),\n      setSurveyDraft: (draft) => set({ surveyDraft: draft }),\n      clearDraft: (type) => {\n        switch (type) {\n          case 'leave': return set({ leaveRequestDraft: null })\n          case 'swap': return set({ swapRequestDraft: null })\n          case 'survey': return set({ surveyDraft: null })\n        }\n      },\n    }),\n    {\n      name: 'cheers-draft-store',\n      storage: createJSONStorage(() => mmkvStorage),\n    }\n  )\n)\n```\n\n### 5.3 TanStack Query (Server State)\n\n```typescript\n// constants/query-keys.ts\n\nexport const queryKeys = {\n  profile: () => ['profile'] as const,\n  shifts: {\n    all: () => ['shifts'] as const,\n    forRange: (start: string, end: string) => ['shifts', start, end] as const,\n    today: () => ['shifts', 'today'] as const,\n    byId: (id: string) => ['shifts', id] as const,\n  },\n  clock: {\n    status: () => ['clock', 'status'] as const,\n    history: (month: string) => ['clock', 'history', month] as const,\n  },\n  notifications: {\n    all: () => ['notifications'] as const,\n    unreadCount: () => ['notifications', 'unread-count'] as const,\n  },\n  leave: {\n    balance: (year: number) => ['leave', 'balance', year] as const,\n    requests: () => ['leave', 'requests'] as const,\n  },\n  tasks: {\n    mine: () => ['tasks', 'mine'] as const,\n    byId: (id: string) => ['tasks', id] as const,\n  },\n  swapRequests: {\n    all: () => ['swap-requests'] as const,\n    byId: (id: string) => ['swap-requests', id] as const,\n  },\n  training: {\n    assignments: () => ['training', 'assignments'] as const,\n    guide: (code: string) => ['training', 'guide', code] as const,\n  },\n  conversations: {\n    all: () => ['conversations'] as const,\n    messages: (id: string) => ['conversations', id, 'messages'] as const,\n  },\n} as const\n```\n\n**Example hook:**\n\n```typescript\n// hooks/use-my-shifts.ts\n\nimport { useQuery } from '@tanstack/react-query'\nimport { getMyShifts } from '@/lib/api/shifts'\nimport { queryKeys } from '@/constants/query-keys'\n\nexport function useMyShifts(startDate: string, endDate: string) {\n  return useQuery({\n    queryKey: queryKeys.shifts.forRange(startDate, endDate),\n    queryFn: () => getMyShifts(startDate, endDate),\n    staleTime: 5 * 60 * 1000,    // 5 min before refetch\n    gcTime: 30 * 60 * 1000,      // 30 min in cache\n    retry: 2,\n  })\n}\n```\n\n### 5.4 MMKV Persistence Layer\n\n```typescript\n// stores/mmkv-storage.ts\n\nimport { MMKV } from 'react-native-mmkv'\nimport { StateStorage } from 'zustand/middleware'\n\nexport const mmkv = new MMKV({ id: 'cheers-app-storage' })\n\n/**\n * MMKV adapter for Zustand persist middleware.\n * MMKV is synchronous and 30x faster than AsyncStorage.\n */\nexport const mmkvStorage: StateStorage = {\n  getItem: (name: string): string | null => {\n    return mmkv.getString(name) ?? null\n  },\n  setItem: (name: string, value: string): void => {\n    mmkv.set(name, value)\n  },\n  removeItem: (name: string): void => {\n    mmkv.delete(name)\n  },\n}\n```\n\nFor TanStack Query persistence (offline cache), use `@tanstack/query-async-storage-persister` with MMKV:\n\n```typescript\n// components/providers/query-provider.tsx\n\nimport { QueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query'\nimport { PersistQueryClientProvider } from '@tanstack/react-query-persist-client'\nimport { createSyncStoragePersister } from '@tanstack/query-sync-storage-persister'\nimport { mmkvStorage } from '@/stores/mmkv-storage'\n\nconst queryClient = new QueryClient({\n  defaultOptions: {\n    queries: {\n      staleTime: 2 * 60 * 1000,   // 2 min\n      gcTime: 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000, // 24 hours (for offline)\n      retry: 2,\n      refetchOnReconnect: true,\n    },\n    mutations: {\n      retry: 1,\n    },\n  },\n})\n\nconst persister = createSyncStoragePersister({\n  storage: mmkvStorage,\n  key: 'cheers-query-cache',\n  throttleTime: 1000,\n})\n\nexport function QueryProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {\n  return (\n    <PersistQueryClientProvider\n      client={queryClient}\n      persistOptions={{\n        persister,\n        maxAge: 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000, // Persist for 24 hours\n        dehydrateOptions: {\n          // Only persist successful queries\n          shouldDehydrateQuery: (query) => {\n            return query.state.status === 'success'\n          },\n        },\n      }}\n    >\n      {children}\n    </PersistQueryClientProvider>\n  )\n}\n```\n\n### 5.5 Cache Invalidation with Realtime\n\nSupabase Realtime events trigger TanStack Query cache invalidation:\n\n```typescript\n// components/providers/realtime-provider.tsx\n\nimport { useEffect } from 'react'\nimport { useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query'\nimport { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase/client'\nimport { useAuth } from '@/hooks/use-auth'\nimport { queryKeys } from '@/constants/query-keys'\n\nexport function RealtimeProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {\n  const queryClient = useQueryClient()\n  const { profile, employee } = useAuth()\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!profile || !employee) return\n\n    // Channel 1: Own shift changes\n    const shiftsChannel = supabase\n      .channel('my-shifts')\n      .on(\n        'postgres_changes',\n        {\n          event: '*',\n          schema: 'public',\n          table: 'shifts',\n          filter: `employee_id=eq.${employee.id}`,\n        },\n        () => {\n          queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.shifts.all() })\n          queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.shifts.today() })\n        }\n      )\n      .subscribe()\n\n    // Channel 2: New notifications\n    const notificationsChannel = supabase\n      .channel('my-notifications')\n      .on(\n        'postgres_changes',\n        {\n          event: 'INSERT',\n          schema: 'public',\n          table: 'notifications',\n          filter: `user_id=eq.${profile.id}`,\n        },\n        () => {\n          queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.notifications.all() })\n          queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.notifications.unreadCount() })\n        }\n      )\n      .subscribe()\n\n    // Channel 3: Swap request status changes\n    const swapsChannel = supabase\n      .channel('my-swaps')\n      .on(\n        'postgres_changes',\n        {\n          event: 'UPDATE',\n          schema: 'public',\n          table: 'shift_swap_requests',\n        },\n        () => {\n          queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.swapRequests.all() })\n        }\n      )\n      .subscribe()\n\n    // Channel 4: Clock record changes (for status indicator)\n    const clockChannel = supabase\n      .channel('my-clock')\n      .on(\n        'postgres_changes',\n        {\n          event: '*',\n          schema: 'public',\n          table: 'clock_in_out',\n          filter: `employee_id=eq.${employee.id}`,\n        },\n        () => {\n          queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.clock.status() })\n        }\n      )\n      .subscribe()\n\n    return () => {\n      supabase.removeChannel(shiftsChannel)\n      supabase.removeChannel(notificationsChannel)\n      supabase.removeChannel(swapsChannel)\n      supabase.removeChannel(clockChannel)\n    }\n  }, [profile?.id, employee?.id, queryClient])\n\n  return <>{children}</>\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. Offline Strategy\n\n### 6.1 Offline Capability Matrix\n\n| Feature | Offline Support | Strategy |\n|---|---|---|\n| **View schedule** | Full | Cached via TanStack Query + MMKV persister (24h) |\n| **View profile** | Full | Cached, rarely changes |\n| **View notifications** | Full (stale) | Cached list, no new ones until online |\n| **View leave balance** | Full (stale) | Cached |\n| **View tasks** | Full (stale) | Cached |\n| **Clock in/out** | Queued | Stored in clock-store, synced when online |\n| **Start/end break** | Queued | Stored in clock-store, synced when online |\n| **Submit leave request** | Queued | Stored in draft-store, synced when online |\n| **Submit swap request** | Queued | Stored in draft-store, synced when online |\n| **AI chat** | None | Requires server (SSE streaming) |\n| **Submit survey** | Queued | Stored in draft-store, synced when online |\n| **Update availability** | Queued | Stored, synced when online |\n\n### 6.2 Offline Queue Pattern\n\n```typescript\n// stores/offline-queue.ts\n\nimport { create } from 'zustand'\nimport { persist, createJSONStorage } from 'zustand/middleware'\nimport { mmkvStorage } from './mmkv-storage'\n\ninterface QueuedAction {\n  readonly id: string\n  readonly type: 'clock_in' | 'clock_out' | 'break_start' | 'break_end'\n         | 'leave_request' | 'swap_request' | 'survey' | 'availability'\n  readonly payload: Record<string, unknown>\n  readonly createdAt: string  // ISO timestamp\n  readonly retryCount: number\n}\n\ninterface OfflineQueueState {\n  readonly queue: readonly QueuedAction[]\n  readonly isSyncing: boolean\n\n  enqueue: (action: Omit<QueuedAction, 'id' | 'createdAt' | 'retryCount'>) => void\n  dequeue: (id: string) => void\n  markSyncing: (syncing: boolean) => void\n  incrementRetry: (id: string) => void\n}\n\nexport const useOfflineQueue = create<OfflineQueueState>()(\n  persist(\n    (set, get) => ({\n      queue: [],\n      isSyncing: false,\n\n      enqueue: (action) => {\n        const newAction: QueuedAction = {\n          ...action,\n          id: `${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2)}`,\n          createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),\n          retryCount: 0,\n        }\n        set({ queue: [...get().queue, newAction] })\n      },\n\n      dequeue: (id) => {\n        set({ queue: get().queue.filter((a) => a.id !== id) })\n      },\n\n      markSyncing: (syncing) => set({ isSyncing: syncing }),\n\n      incrementRetry: (id) => {\n        set({\n          queue: get().queue.map((a) =>\n            a.id === id ? { ...a, retryCount: a.retryCount + 1 } : a\n          ),\n        })\n      },\n    }),\n    {\n      name: 'cheers-offline-queue',\n      storage: createJSONStorage(() => mmkvStorage),\n    }\n  )\n)\n```\n\n### 6.3 Sync Manager\n\n```typescript\n// lib/utils/sync-manager.ts\n\nimport NetInfo from '@react-native-community/netinfo'\nimport { useOfflineQueue } from '@/stores/offline-queue'\nimport { clockIn, clockOut, startBreak, endBreak } from '@/lib/api/clock'\n\nconst MAX_RETRIES = 3\nconst STALE_THRESHOLD_MS = 4 * 60 * 60 * 1000 // 4 hours\n\n/**\n * Process the offline queue when connectivity is restored.\n * Called from the network status listener and on app foreground.\n *\n * Queue items are processed in FIFO order (critical for clock events).\n * Items older than 4 hours are discarded with a warning.\n */\nexport async function processOfflineQueue(): Promise<void> {\n  const state = useOfflineQueue.getState()\n  if (state.isSyncing || state.queue.length === 0) return\n\n  const networkState = await NetInfo.fetch()\n  if (!networkState.isConnected) return\n\n  state.markSyncing(true)\n\n  for (const action of state.queue) {\n    // Discard stale actions\n    const age = Date.now() - new Date(action.createdAt).getTime()\n    if (age > STALE_THRESHOLD_MS) {\n      state.dequeue(action.id)\n      console.warn(`Discarded stale offline action: ${action.type} (${action.id})`)\n      continue\n    }\n\n    if (action.retryCount >= MAX_RETRIES) {\n      state.dequeue(action.id)\n      console.error(`Max retries exceeded for: ${action.type} (${action.id})`)\n      continue\n    }\n\n    try {\n      await executeAction(action)\n      state.dequeue(action.id)\n    } catch (error) {\n      state.incrementRetry(action.id)\n      break // Stop processing on first failure (preserve order)\n    }\n  }\n\n  state.markSyncing(false)\n}\n\nasync function executeAction(action: QueuedAction): Promise<void> {\n  switch (action.type) {\n    case 'clock_in':\n      await clockIn(action.payload as { latitude?: number; longitude?: number })\n      break\n    case 'clock_out':\n      await clockOut(action.payload as { clock_record_id: string })\n      break\n    // ... other action types\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Security Considerations\n\n### 7.1 Token Storage\n\n| Secret | Storage | Rationale |\n|---|---|---|\n| Supabase access token (JWT) | `expo-secure-store` | Encrypted at rest via iOS Keychain / Android Keystore |\n| Supabase refresh token | `expo-secure-store` | Same -- must be protected to prevent session hijacking |\n| Supabase session blob (>2KB) | `expo-secure-store` with fallback to AsyncStorage | SecureStore has a 2048-byte limit; the session JSON can exceed this |\n| User preferences (locale, theme) | MMKV | Non-sensitive, fast access |\n| Offline queue | MMKV | Contains action payloads but no secrets |\n| Cached query data | MMKV | Non-sensitive copies of data already accessible via RLS |\n\n### 7.2 No Service Role Key\n\nThe `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` is **never** included in the mobile app binary, environment variables, or build configuration. All Supabase operations use the anon key with RLS enforcement. Operations requiring admin privileges (bypassing RLS) are handled by calling the Next.js API routes, which run on the server and have access to the service role key.\n\n### 7.3 Certificate Pinning\n\n**Recommendation: Do not implement certificate pinning for v1.**\n\nRationale:\n- Supabase is a managed service; pinning their certificate would break on certificate rotation (which Supabase controls, not us).\n- The attack surface (MITM on a restaurant staff app) is low.\n- Expo managed workflow does not natively support certificate pinning without ejecting or using a config plugin.\n- The risk/benefit tradeoff does not justify the maintenance burden for a 20-30 user app.\n\nIf pinning becomes necessary in the future, use `expo-certificate-pinning` or move to a bare workflow with `TrustKit` (iOS) / `OkHttp CertificatePinner` (Android).\n\n### 7.4 Biometric Unlock\n\n**Recommendation: Implement as an opt-in feature for v1.1.**\n\nFlow:\n1. User logs in with email/password (stores session in SecureStore).\n2. After successful login, prompt: \"Enable Face ID / fingerprint to unlock?\"\n3. If enabled, wrap the SecureStore access with `expo-local-authentication`:\n   - On app launch, require biometric before reading the session from SecureStore.\n   - On session expiry, fall back to email/password login.\n4. Store a boolean `biometricEnabled` in MMKV (non-sensitive preference).\n\n```typescript\n// lib/utils/biometric.ts\n\nimport * as LocalAuthentication from 'expo-local-authentication'\n\nexport async function authenticateWithBiometric(): Promise<boolean> {\n  const hasHardware = await LocalAuthentication.hasHardwareAsync()\n  if (!hasHardware) return false\n\n  const isEnrolled = await LocalAuthentication.isEnrolledAsync()\n  if (!isEnrolled) return false\n\n  const result = await LocalAuthentication.authenticateAsync({\n    promptMessage: 'Unlock GrandCafe Cheers',\n    cancelLabel: 'Use password',\n    disableDeviceFallback: false,\n  })\n\n  return result.success\n}\n```\n\n### 7.5 Geolocation Privacy\n\nThe clock-in endpoint at `/api/staff/clock?action=in` already accepts optional `latitude`/`longitude` parameters and validates them against the restaurant's geofence (39.5021, 2.7392, 200m radius) -- see the existing implementation. In the mobile app:\n\n- Request location permission only when the user taps \"Clock In\" (not on app launch).\n- Show a clear explanation of why location is needed (\"Verify you are at the restaurant\").\n- If permission is denied, allow clock-in without location but log the absence of geolocation data in the `metadata` JSONB column.\n- Never track location in the background.\n\n### 7.6 Session Management\n\n- Access tokens expire per Supabase default (1 hour).\n- `autoRefreshToken: true` in the client config handles transparent renewal.\n- On `SIGNED_OUT` or `TOKEN_REFRESHED` auth events, update the stored session.\n- On `401` responses from Next.js API routes, attempt one token refresh before showing the login screen.\n- On app backgrounding for more than 30 minutes, refresh the token on foreground resume.\n\n### 7.7 Input Validation\n\nAll user inputs are validated before submission using Zod schemas (matching the existing web app patterns). The mobile app reuses the same Zod schemas defined in the web app's API routes for consistency:\n\n- Leave request: `z.object({ employee_id: z.string().uuid(), leave_type: z.enum([...]), start_date: z.string().regex(/^\\d{4}-\\d{2}-\\d{2}$/), ... })`\n- Clock in: `z.object({ latitude: z.number().min(-90).max(90).optional(), longitude: z.number().min(-180).max(180).optional() })`\n- Swap request: `z.object({ shift_id: z.string().uuid(), offered_to: z.string().uuid(), reason: z.string().optional() })`\n\n---\n\n## 8. Data Flow Diagrams\n\n### 8.1 Clock In/Out Flow\n\n```\n┌──────────┐     ┌──────────────┐     ┌────────────────┐     ┌──────────┐\n│  User     │     │  Mobile App  │     │  Next.js API   │     │ Supabase │\n│  taps     │────>│  Clock       │────>│  /api/staff/   │────>│ clock_   │\n│  \"Clock   │     │  Screen      │     │  clock?action  │     │ in_out   │\n│   In\"     │     │              │     │  =in           │     │ table    │\n└──────────┘     │              │     │                │     │          │\n                  │ 1. Request   │     │ 2. requireAuth │     │          │\n                  │    location  │     │ 3. Find shift  │     │          │\n                  │    permission│     │ 4. Grace check │     │          │\n                  │ 2. Get GPS   │     │ 5. Geofence    │     │          │\n                  │ 3. POST with │     │    validate    │     │          │\n                  │    lat/lng   │     │ 6. INSERT      │────>│          │\n                  │              │<────│ 7. Return      │     │          │\n                  │ 4. Update UI │     │    record      │     │          │\n                  │ 5. Start     │     │                │     │          │\n                  │    timer     │     └────────────────┘     │          │\n                  │              │                             │          │\n                  │ [OFFLINE]    │                             │          │\n                  │ Store in     │                             │          │\n                  │ offline queue│                             │          │\n                  │ Sync on      │                             │          │\n                  │ reconnect    │                             │          │\n                  └──────────────┘                             └──────────┘\n```\n\n### 8.2 Schedule View Flow\n\n```\n┌──────────┐     ┌──────────────┐     ┌──────────┐\n│  User     │     │  Mobile App  │     │ Supabase │\n│  opens    │────>│  Schedule    │     │          │\n│  Schedule │     │  Screen      │     │          │\n│  tab      │     │              │     │          │\n└──────────┘     │ 1. Check     │     │          │\n                  │    MMKV cache│     │          │\n                  │ 2. Show      │     │          │\n                  │    cached    │     │          │\n                  │    data      │     │          │\n                  │ 3. TanStack  │     │          │\n                  │    Query     │────>│ shifts   │\n                  │    fetches   │     │ table    │\n                  │    fresh     │     │ (RLS:    │\n                  │    data      │<────│  own     │\n                  │ 4. Update UI │     │  shifts) │\n                  │              │     │          │\n                  │ [REALTIME]   │     │          │\n                  │ Subscribe to │<═══>│ realtime │\n                  │ shift changes│     │ channel  │\n                  │ Invalidate   │     │          │\n                  │ query cache  │     │          │\n                  └──────────────┘     └──────────┘\n```\n\n### 8.3 AI Chat Flow\n\n```\n┌──────────┐     ┌──────────────┐     ┌────────────────┐     ┌──────────┐\n│  User     │     │  Mobile App  │     │  Next.js API   │     │ Claude   │\n│  sends    │────>│  Chat        │────>│  /api/ai/chat/ │────>│ API      │\n│  message  │     │  Screen      │     │  stream (SSE)  │     │          │\n└──────────┘     │              │     │                │     │          │\n                  │ 1. Add user  │     │ 2. Auth check  │     │          │\n                  │    message   │     │ 3. Load context│     │          │\n                  │    to UI     │     │ 4. Model route │     │          │\n                  │              │     │ 5. Stream      │<────│          │\n                  │ 6. Parse SSE │<────│    response    │     │          │\n                  │    events    │     │                │     │          │\n                  │ 7. Update    │     │ [Tool calls]   │     │          │\n                  │    streaming │     │ 8. Execute     │     │          │\n                  │    text      │     │    tools       │     │          │\n                  │              │<────│ 9. Tool results│     │          │\n                  │ 10. Show     │     │                │     │          │\n                  │    final     │     │ [Write tools]  │     │          │\n                  │    message   │     │ Create pending │     │          │\n                  │              │<────│ action (5min)  │     │          │\n                  │ 11. Show     │     │                │     │          │\n                  │    confirm/  │     │                │     │          │\n                  │    reject    │────>│ Confirm action │     │          │\n                  └──────────────┘     └────────────────┘     └──────────┘\n```\n\n---\n\n## 9. Key Design Decisions (ADRs)\n\n### ADR-001: Direct Supabase vs. Next.js API Proxy\n\n**Context:** The mobile app needs to read and write data. The web app has 90+ API routes on Next.js. Should the mobile app call the Next.js routes or query Supabase directly?\n\n**Decision:** Hybrid approach. Reads go directly to Supabase. Writes with server-side business logic go through Next.js API routes.\n\n**Consequences:**\n- (+) Reads are faster (no extra network hop through Next.js)\n- (+) RLS is enforced at the database level regardless of client\n- (+) No need to duplicate the existing API routes\n- (+) Business logic (geofence checks, grace period validation, AI chat) stays in one place\n- (-) Two different API calling patterns in the mobile codebase\n- (-) Next.js API routes need a small modification to accept Bearer tokens (currently cookie-only)\n- (-) Mobile app has a dependency on the web app's deployment URL\n\n**Alternatives Considered:**\n- All traffic through Next.js API: Adds latency to reads, couples mobile to web app availability for viewing data\n- All direct Supabase: Would require duplicating server-side validation logic in the mobile app, exposing business rules to the client\n\n### ADR-002: Expo Managed Workflow\n\n**Context:** Should the mobile app use Expo managed workflow or bare workflow?\n\n**Decision:** Managed workflow with Expo SDK 53, using EAS Build for native builds.\n\n**Consequences:**\n- (+) Faster development: OTA updates, no native code maintenance\n- (+) Expo Router provides file-based routing consistent with Next.js conventions\n- (+) Config plugins handle most native module needs (notifications, secure store, location)\n- (+) Smaller team can maintain the app without iOS/Android native expertise\n- (-) Cannot use libraries that require custom native modules without config plugins\n- (-) Certificate pinning requires ejecting or a third-party config plugin\n\n### ADR-003: MMKV over AsyncStorage\n\n**Context:** Need persistent storage for Zustand state and TanStack Query cache.\n\n**Decision:** Use `react-native-mmkv` for all persistence (Zustand stores, TanStack Query persister).\n\n**Consequences:**\n- (+) 30x faster than AsyncStorage (synchronous reads/writes)\n- (+) Zustand persist middleware works synchronously (no hydration flash)\n- (+) Efficient for the offline queue and form drafts\n- (+) Small binary size addition (~100KB)\n- (-) Requires Expo config plugin (`react-native-mmkv` is a native module)\n- (-) No encryption by default (but data stored is non-sensitive; tokens use SecureStore)\n\n### ADR-004: i18next over next-intl\n\n**Context:** The web app uses `next-intl`. Should the mobile app use the same library?\n\n**Decision:** Use `i18next` + `react-i18next` instead.\n\n**Consequences:**\n- (+) `i18next` is framework-agnostic and works natively in React Native\n- (+) Large ecosystem: language detection, pluralization, interpolation\n- (+) Translation JSON format is compatible (can share translation files)\n- (-) Different library from the web app (but same JSON structure)\n- (-) Need to maintain separate i18n initialization code\n\n**Alternatives Considered:**\n- `next-intl`: Designed for Next.js, relies on server components and middleware that do not exist in React Native\n- `expo-localization` + `i18n-js`: Simpler but lacks the plugin ecosystem of i18next\n\n### ADR-005: NativeWind over Tamagui/Gluestack\n\n**Context:** The web app uses Tailwind CSS. Which styling solution for React Native?\n\n**Decision:** NativeWind v4 (Tailwind CSS for React Native).\n\n**Consequences:**\n- (+) Same Tailwind utility classes as the web app\n- (+) Designers and developers share the same mental model\n- (+) Dark mode support via CSS variables, consistent with the web app's OKLch color system\n- (+) Smaller learning curve for the team already using Tailwind\n- (-) NativeWind v4 is still maturing; some CSS features do not translate to native\n- (-) Performance overhead of the className transform at build time\n\n### ADR-006: Push Notification Strategy\n\n**Context:** The existing system uses Web Push (VAPID keys) and stores subscriptions in `push_subscriptions` with `endpoint`, `p256dh_key`, and `auth_key` fields. React Native does not support Web Push.\n\n**Decision:** Use Expo Notifications (which wraps APNs and FCM) and store Expo push tokens in a new `device_tokens` table or extend `push_subscriptions` with a `platform` column.\n\n**Consequences:**\n- (+) Native push notifications with reliable delivery\n- (+) Expo handles token management, background delivery, and notification categories\n- (+) Can use the existing notification triggers (DB functions create `notifications` rows) as the source of truth, then fan out to Expo push\n- (-) Requires a new server-side process to watch for new `notifications` rows and send Expo push messages\n- (-) Need to add a migration for mobile push tokens (separate from web push subscriptions)\n\n**Implementation path:**\n1. Add a `device_push_tokens` table: `id`, `user_id`, `expo_push_token`, `platform` (ios/android), `active`, `created_at`\n2. Mobile app registers token on login and updates on each app launch\n3. Add an Edge Function or scheduled job that watches `notifications` INSERTs (via Realtime or pg_notify) and sends Expo push via `expo-server-sdk`\n4. Alternatively, modify the existing `create_notification()` DB function to call an HTTP Edge Function that sends push\n\n---\n\n## Appendix A: Provider Nesting Order\n\n```typescript\n// app/_layout.tsx\n\nexport default function RootLayout() {\n  return (\n    <GestureHandlerRootView style={{ flex: 1 }}>\n      <ThemeProvider>\n        <I18nProvider>\n          <AuthProvider>\n            <QueryProvider>\n              <RealtimeProvider>\n                <NotificationProvider>\n                  <Slot />\n                </NotificationProvider>\n              </RealtimeProvider>\n            </QueryProvider>\n          </AuthProvider>\n        </I18nProvider>\n      </ThemeProvider>\n    </GestureHandlerRootView>\n  )\n}\n```\n\nOrder rationale:\n1. **GestureHandlerRootView** -- Required by React Navigation (Expo Router) at the outermost level\n2. **ThemeProvider** -- Must wrap everything that uses NativeWind colors\n3. **I18nProvider** -- i18next must be available before any `t()` calls\n4. **AuthProvider** -- Supabase session management, must wrap QueryProvider so queries can access the session\n5. **QueryProvider** -- TanStack Query client with MMKV persistence\n6. **RealtimeProvider** -- Needs both auth (user ID) and query client (for invalidation)\n7. **NotificationProvider** -- Needs auth (to register push token) and query client (to refetch on notification)\n\n## Appendix B: Required Backend Changes\n\nTo support the mobile app, the existing web app needs these minimal changes:\n\n1. **Auth header support in API routes.** Modify `requireAuth()` in `/Users/lr0y/Movies/claude-quickstarts-main/grandcafe-cheers-platform/app/grandcafe-cheers-app/src/lib/utils/auth.ts` to also check for `Authorization: Bearer <token>` when no cookie session is found. Approximately 30 lines of code.\n\n2. **Mobile push token table.** New migration to create `device_push_tokens` with RLS (users can manage their own tokens, admin can read all).\n\n3. **Push notification sender.** A Supabase Edge Function or Next.js cron that watches for new `notifications` rows and sends to both web push (existing `push_subscriptions`) and mobile push (new `device_push_tokens` via Expo Push API).\n\n4. **CORS configuration.** If the Next.js API routes are called from a different origin (the mobile app's fetch calls), ensure CORS headers allow the mobile app's requests. Since mobile fetch requests do not have an `Origin` header, this is typically not an issue, but verify in testing.\n\n## Appendix C: File Size Targets\n\n| Directory | Target Lines per File | Rationale |\n|---|---|---|\n| `app/` route files | 50-150 | Route files should be thin, delegating to components |\n| `components/ui/` | 50-200 | Primitive components, highly reusable |\n| `components/{feature}/` | 100-300 | Feature-specific, self-contained |\n| `lib/api/` | 30-80 | Thin API wrappers, one function per export |\n| `hooks/` | 20-80 | Single-purpose hooks |\n| `stores/` | 40-100 | Zustand stores with clear boundaries |\n| `lib/utils/` | 30-150 | Pure utility functions |\n\nMaximum file size: 400 lines. If any file exceeds this, extract into sub-modules.\n\n---\n\n**Relevant source files analyzed for this architecture:**\n\n-
