# PART 2: SCREEN SPECIFICATIONS

# GrandCafe Cheers -- React Native Employee App: Screen Specification Document\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Global Design System](#1-global-design-system)\n2. [Authentication & Onboarding](#2-authentication--onboarding)\n3. [Tab 1 -- Home](#3-tab-1----home)\n4. [Tab 2 -- Schedule](#4-tab-2----schedule)\n5. [Tab 3 -- Clock](#5-tab-3----clock)\n6. [Tab 4 -- Chat](#6-tab-4----chat)\n7. [Tab 5 -- More](#7-tab-5----more)\n8. [Push Notification Routing](#8-push-notification-routing)\n9. [Global Error & Offline States](#9-global-error--offline-states)\n\n---\n\n## 1. Global Design System\n\n### 1.1 Navigation Architecture\n\n**Router:** Expo Router v3 with file-based routing.\n\n```\napp/\n  _layout.tsx                    # Root layout: auth gate, splash screen\n  (auth)/\n    login.tsx                    # Login screen\n    onboarding.tsx               # First-launch onboarding\n  (tabs)/\n    _layout.tsx                  # Bottom tab bar (5 tabs)\n    index.tsx                    # Tab 1: Home\n    schedule/\n      _layout.tsx                # Stack navigator for schedule\n      index.tsx                  # Calendar + shift list\n      [shiftId].tsx              # Shift detail modal\n      swap-request.tsx           # Swap request flow\n    clock/\n      _layout.tsx                # Stack navigator for clock\n      index.tsx                  # Clock in/out main screen\n      history.tsx                # Clock history\n      survey.tsx                 # Post-shift survey (modal)\n    chat/\n      _layout.tsx                # Stack navigator for chat\n      index.tsx                  # Announcements + team feed\n    more/\n      _layout.tsx                # Stack navigator for more\n      index.tsx                  # Section list\n      profile.tsx                # Profile edit\n      availability.tsx           # Set availability\n      leave-requests.tsx         # Leave request list + create\n      documents.tsx              # Employment documents\n      training/\n        index.tsx                # Training courses list\n        [guideCode].tsx          # Course study view\n        test.tsx                 # Training test modal\n        certificates.tsx         # My certificates\n      tasks.tsx                  # My tasks view\n      settings.tsx               # App settings\n      info-guide.tsx             # Read-only business reference\n```\n\n### 1.2 Tab Bar Configuration\n\n| Tab | Label | Icon (inactive) | Icon (active) | Badge |\n|-----|-------|-----------------|---------------|-------|\n| Home | Home | `House` outline | `House` filled | Unread notification dot (red, 8px) |\n| Schedule | Schedule | `CalendarDays` outline | `CalendarDays` filled | None |\n| Clock | Clock | `Clock` outline | `Clock` filled | \"Working\" pulse dot (green) when clocked in |\n| Chat | Chat | `MessageCircle` outline | `MessageCircle` filled | Unread count badge (max \"99+\") |\n| More | More | `Menu` outline | `Menu` filled | Red dot if pending training |\n\n**Tab bar height:** 56pt (iOS), 64dp (Android) + safe area insets.\n**Tab bar style:** Solid background matching theme (no blur on Android), 1px top border.\n\n### 1.3 Theming\n\nThe app inherits the web platform's OKLch color system but uses React Native's `useColorScheme()` + system preference. No manual theme toggle (follows device setting).\n\n- **Primary:** Cheers brand orange `#F97316`\n- **Background (light):** `#FFFFFF`, (dark): `#0A0A0A`\n- **Card (light):** `#F9FAFB`, (dark): `#1A1A1A`\n- **Muted text (light):** `#6B7280`, (dark): `#9CA3AF`\n- **Destructive:** `#EF4444`\n- **Success:** `#22C55E`\n\n### 1.4 Typography\n\n- **Font family:** System default (SF Pro on iOS, Roboto on Android)\n- **Heading 1:** 28pt semibold (screen titles)\n- **Heading 2:** 20pt semibold (section headers)\n- **Body:** 16pt regular\n- **Caption:** 13pt regular, muted color\n- **Mono:** System mono (for timers, clock displays)\n\n### 1.5 Spacing System\n\n4pt base grid: `4, 8, 12, 16, 20, 24, 32, 40, 48`.\nScreen horizontal padding: 16pt. Card internal padding: 16pt. Card border radius: 12pt.\n\n### 1.6 Common Components\n\n- **Pull-to-refresh:** Available on all scrollable screens. Uses native `RefreshControl`.\n- **Skeleton loaders:** Gray shimmer rectangles matching content layout, shown during initial data fetch.\n- **Toast notifications:** Bottom-of-screen toast, auto-dismiss after 3s. Swipeable to dismiss.\n- **Haptic feedback:** Light haptic on button press, medium on clock in/out, success on completed actions.\n- **Offline banner:** Persistent yellow banner at top of screen when connectivity lost: \"No internet connection. Data may be outdated.\"\n\n### 1.7 Internationalization\n\n4 locales: `en`, `nl`, `es`, `de`. Uses `expo-localization` + `i18n-js` or `react-intl`. Language determined by user profile `language` field (from Supabase `profiles.language`), not device locale. Changeable in Settings.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Authentication & Onboarding\n\n### 2.1 Splash Screen\n\n**Route:** Handled by Expo's `expo-splash-screen` + root `_layout.tsx` auth gate.\n\n**Wireframe:**\n- Full-screen brand orange background (`#F97316`)\n- Centered Cheers logo (`/icons/logoheader.png`) at 120x120pt\n- Subtle scale-up animation (0.9 -> 1.0 over 400ms with spring easing)\n- No text\n\n**Logic:**\n1. Check SecureStore for stored session tokens\n2. If valid session: navigate to `(tabs)` \n3. If no session or expired: navigate to `(auth)/login`\n4. If first launch ever (AsyncStorage flag `hasOnboarded` is false): navigate to `(auth)/onboarding`\n\n**Duration:** Maximum 2 seconds before fallback navigation.\n\n---\n\n### 2.2 Onboarding Screen\n\n**Route:** `(auth)/onboarding`\n\n**Wireframe:**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n| [Status Bar]                              |\n|                                           |\n|        [Cheers Logo - 80x80]             |\n|                                           |\n|     Welcome to Cheers Staff App          |\n|     [Subtitle text - 2 lines]            |\n|                                           |\n| +----- Step 1: Language ---------+       |\n| |  Select your preferred language |       |\n| |                                 |       |\n| |  [EN]  [NL]  [ES]  [DE]       |       |\n| |   ^^selected                   |       |\n| +---------------------------------+       |\n|                                           |\n| +----- Step 2: Notifications ----+       |\n| |  [Bell icon - 48pt]            |       |\n| |                                 |       |\n| |  Enable push notifications     |       |\n| |  to receive shift reminders,   |       |\n| |  schedule updates, and more.   |       |\n| |                                 |       |\n| |  [Enable Notifications]  (CTA) |       |\n| |  [Maybe Later]   (text link)   |       |\n| +---------------------------------+       |\n|                                           |\n|          [Get Started]  (CTA)            |\n|                                           |\n| [Progress dots: o  o]                    |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Layout:**\n- Paged horizontal `ScrollView` or `PagerView` with 2 steps\n- Bottom progress dots (2 dots, active = filled primary, inactive = gray)\n- \"Get Started\" button appears on final page\n\n**Step 1 -- Language Selection:**\n- 4 horizontal language chips: `EN` English, `NL` Nederlands, `ES` Espanol, `DE` Deutsch\n- Default pre-selected based on `expo-localization.locale` (best match)\n- Selecting a chip highlights it with primary border + filled background\n- Selection is persisted to `AsyncStorage` temporarily (applied after login via profile update)\n\n**Step 2 -- Notification Permission:**\n- Large bell icon centered\n- Descriptive text explaining what notifications they will receive\n- Primary CTA: \"Enable Notifications\" -- triggers `expo-notifications.requestPermissionsAsync()`\n- Secondary text link: \"Maybe Later\" -- skips permission\n- On iOS, this triggers the system permission dialog\n- On Android 13+, triggers runtime permission request\n\n**Interactions:**\n- Horizontal swipe between pages\n- Tap language chip to select\n- Tap \"Enable Notifications\" to request permission\n- Tap \"Get Started\" to set `hasOnboarded = true` and navigate to login\n\n**Animations:**\n- Pages slide horizontally with spring physics\n- Language chips scale up on selection (1.0 -> 1.05, 200ms)\n- Progress dots animate width change (dot -> pill shape for active, 300ms)\n\n**Data sources:** None (purely local).\n\n**Empty states:** N/A.\n\n**Error states:** If notification permission denied, show subtle info text \"You can enable notifications later in Settings\" and continue.\n\n---\n\n### 2.3 Login Screen\n\n**Route:** `(auth)/login`\n\n**Wireframe:**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n| [Status Bar]                              |\n|                                           |\n|        [Cheers Logo - 80x80]             |\n|                                           |\n|        Cheers Staff                       |\n|     Sign in to your account              |\n|                                           |\n| +--- Login Card (elevated) ------+       |\n| |                                 |       |\n| |  Email                         |       |\n| |  [________________________]    |       |\n| |                                 |       |\n| |  Password                      |       |\n| |  [________________] [eye]      |       |\n| |                                 |       |\n| |  [x] Remember me              |       |\n| |                                 |       |\n| |  [error message area]         |       |\n| |                                 |       |\n| |  [      Sign In       ]  (CTA)|       |\n| |                                 |       |\n| +---------------------------------+       |\n|                                           |\n| +--- Language Selector -----------+       |\n| |  [EN]  [NL]  [ES]  [DE]       |       |\n| +---------------------------------+       |\n|                                           |\n|   GrandCafe Cheers                        |\n|   Carrer de la Sirena 2, El Arenal       |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Layout:**\n- Vertically centered on screen with `KeyboardAvoidingView`\n- Logo at top, login card center, language selector below card, address at bottom\n- Card has elevation/shadow on iOS, elevation on Android\n- 16pt horizontal margin\n\n**Components:**\n- **Email field:** `TextInput` with `keyboardType=\"email-address\"`, `autoCapitalize=\"none\"`, `autoComplete=\"email\"`, `textContentType=\"emailAddress\"`\n- **Password field:** `TextInput` with `secureTextEntry` toggle via eye icon button. `textContentType=\"password\"`, `autoComplete=\"password\"`\n- **Remember me:** Checkbox (stores session refresh token in `expo-secure-store` vs ephemeral)\n- **Error area:** Red background pill with error text. Hidden when no error. Appears with slide-down animation.\n- **Sign In button:** Full-width primary button. Shows spinner during loading. Disabled during loading.\n- **Language selector:** 4 horizontal chips below the card. Changes the UI language immediately (updates i18n context). Applied to profile after successful login.\n\n**Data sources:**\n- `POST /api/auth/login` -- Supabase `auth.signInWithPassword(email, password)`\n- Response: `SignInResponse` with `access_token`, `refresh_token`, `profile`\n\n**Interactions:**\n- Tap \"Sign In\" -- validate email format + password min length (6 chars) client-side, then call API\n- Tap eye icon -- toggle password visibility\n- Tap language chip -- change UI locale immediately\n- Tap \"Remember me\" -- toggles persistent vs session-only token storage\n- Keyboard \"Done\" on password field -- submits form\n\n**Empty states:** N/A (always shows form).\n\n**Error states:**\n- Invalid credentials: \"Invalid email or password. Please try again.\" (red error box)\n- Network error: \"Unable to connect. Check your internet connection.\"\n- Too many attempts: \"Too many login attempts. Please wait a moment.\"\n- All errors auto-dismiss after 5s or on next input change\n\n**Animations:**\n- Logo fades in + slides down (300ms) on mount\n- Card fades in + slides up (400ms, 100ms delay) on mount\n- Error box slides down from top of card with spring physics\n- Sign In button shows center spinner replacing text during loading\n- Successful login: card scales down (1.0 -> 0.95) + fades out before navigation (250ms)\n\n**Post-login flow:**\n1. Store tokens in `expo-secure-store` (if remember me) or memory\n2. Update profile language if changed during login\n3. Register device push token with server (see Section 8)\n4. Navigate to `(tabs)` with `router.replace()`\n\n---\n\n## 3. Tab 1 -- Home\n\n### 3.1 Home Dashboard\n\n**Route:** `(tabs)/index`\n\n**Wireframe:**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n| [Status Bar]                              |\n| Good morning, Maria        [Bell(3)] [Av]|\n|                                           |\n| +--- Next Shift Card ----------------+   |\n| |  TODAY                              |   |\n| |  Morning Shift  10:00 - 17:00      |   |\n| |  Starts in 2h 15m                  |   |\n| |  [Clock In ->]     (if within 30m) |   |\n| +-------------------------------------+   |\n|                                           |\n| +--- Weekly Hours ----------+  +--- W --+|\n| |  This Week      32.5h     |  | 24C   ||\n| |  [==========----] 81%     |  | Sunny ||\n| |  Target: 40h              |  | Wind  ||\n| +----------------------------+  +-------+|\n|                                           |\n| +--- Announcements ---------------------+|\n| |  [Pin] Schedule Week 12 Published     ||\n| |  2 hours ago                           ||\n| |                                        ||\n| |  [Pin] New cocktail training available ||\n| |  Yesterday                             ||\n| |                                        ||\n| |  [See all announcements ->]            ||\n| +----------------------------------------+|\n|                                           |\n| +--- My Tasks Today --------------------+|\n| |  [ ] Clean terrace chairs    [Medium] ||\n| |  [ ] Restock napkins         [Low]    ||\n| |  [View all tasks ->]                  ||\n| +----------------------------------------+|\n|                                           |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Layout:**\n- `ScrollView` with `RefreshControl`\n- Greeting header: left-aligned \"Good morning/afternoon/evening, {first_name}\". Right side: notification bell + avatar (32pt circle)\n- Next Shift card: full-width, prominent card with brand accent left border (4pt)\n- Two half-width cards row: Weekly Hours (left, 60%) + Weather (right, 40%)\n- Announcements card: full-width, shows last 3\n- My Tasks Today card: full-width, shows up to 3 tasks for today\n\n**Components:**\n\n**Greeting header:**\n- Dynamic time-based greeting using Europe/Madrid timezone\n- Notification bell: `Bell` icon with red badge showing unread count (matches web's `NotificationBell` component)\n- Tapping bell navigates to notification list sheet\n- Avatar: 32pt circle with user photo or initials fallback\n\n**Next Shift card:**\n- Shows the employee's next upcoming shift from `staff_shifts` table\n- States:\n  - **Upcoming today:** Orange left border. Shows shift type badge (Morning/Afternoon/Night/Split with color coding from `SHIFT_TYPE_CONFIG`), time range, countdown (\"Starts in Xh Ym\"). If within 30 minutes of start and not clocked in, shows \"Clock In\" button that navigates to Clock tab.\n  - **Currently working:** Green left border. Shift type + time range + \"Working for Xh Ym\" live counter. Shows \"View Clock\" link.\n  - **Next shift is tomorrow or later:** Gray left border. Shows date + shift type + time range.\n  - **No upcoming shifts:** Dashed border card. \"No upcoming shifts scheduled. Enjoy your time off!\"\n\n**Weekly Hours card:**\n- Circle or bar progress showing `weekMinutes / (weeklyHoursTarget * 60)` percentage\n- Large bold text: \"32.5h\"\n- Small text: \"Target: 40h\"\n- Color: green if under target, amber if 80-100%, red if over\n\n**Weather card:**\n- Current temperature in Celsius for El Arenal, Mallorca\n- Weather icon (sun, cloud, rain etc.)\n- Wind speed in km/h (relevant for beachfront)\n- Data from weather API (or cached)\n\n**Announcements card:**\n- List of most recent 3 announcements from `notifications` table where `type = 'system'` or `type = 'schedule_published'`\n- Each row: pin icon (if pinned), title text, relative time\n- \"See all announcements\" link at bottom navigates to Chat tab\n\n**My Tasks Today card:**\n- List of up to 3 tasks assigned to employee for today from `planned_tasks` table\n- Each row: checkbox (tappable to mark complete), title, priority badge\n- \"View all tasks\" link navigates to More > Tasks\n\n**Data sources:**\n- `GET /api/staff/shifts?employee_id={id}&start_date={today}&end_date={+7days}` -- next shift\n- `GET /api/staff/clock?employee_id={id}` -- current clock status\n- `GET /api/notifications` -- announcements\n- `GET /api/staff/task-plans?week={currentWeek}` -- today's tasks\n- `GET /api/staff/clock?employee_id={id}` -- week hours from clock records\n- Weather: External API or cached endpoint\n\n**Interactions:**\n- Pull-to-refresh: reloads all data sources\n- Tap Next Shift card: navigates to Schedule tab, scrolls to that day\n- Tap \"Clock In\" button: navigates to Clock tab\n- Tap notification bell: opens notification sheet (see 3.2)\n- Tap avatar: navigates to More > Profile\n- Tap announcement row: navigates to Chat tab\n- Tap task checkbox: toggles task completion with haptic feedback\n- Tap \"View all tasks\": navigates to More > Tasks\n\n**Empty states:**\n- No shifts: \"No upcoming shifts scheduled\" with calendar icon\n- No announcements: \"No announcements yet\" with megaphone icon\n- No tasks: \"No tasks for today\" with checkmark icon\n- All sections can be empty independently\n\n**Error states:**\n- Network error on any card: card shows \"Tap to retry\" with retry icon\n- Auth expired: redirect to login screen\n\n**Animations:**\n- Cards fade in staggered (100ms delay each) on mount\n- Next shift countdown updates every second (text only, no layout shift)\n- Task checkbox: checkmark draws in with stroke animation (200ms)\n- Pull-to-refresh: spinner rotates with native behavior\n\n---\n\n### 3.2 Notification Sheet\n\n**Route:** Modal sheet overlay on Home (not a separate route, triggered by bell tap)\n\n**Wireframe:**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n|  [Drag handle]                            |\n|  Notifications           [Mark all read] |\n|                                           |\n|  TODAY                                    |\n|  +--------------------------------------+|\n|  | [Cal] Schedule Week 13 Published     ||\n|  |       Your shifts have been updated  ||\n|  |       2 hours ago                    ||\n|  +--------------------------------------+|\n|  | [Clock] Shift reminder               ||\n|  |       Morning shift starts in 1h    ||\n|  |       3 hours ago                    ||\n|  +--------------------------------------+|\n|                                           |\n|  YESTERDAY                                |\n|  +--------------------------------------+|\n|  | [Users] Shift swap request           ||\n|  |       Carlos wants to swap Tue AM   ||\n|  |       Yesterday at 14:30            ||\n|  +--------------------------------------+|\n|                                           |\n|  EARLIER                                  |\n|  ...                                      |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Layout:**\n- Bottom sheet with drag handle, snaps to 50% and 90% height\n- Grouped by date: \"Today\", \"Yesterday\", \"This Week\", \"Earlier\"\n- Each notification row matches web's `NotificationItem` pattern\n- Swipe-left on row reveals \"Delete\" action\n\n**Components:**\n- Icon circle (40pt) with type-specific icon (same mapping as web `iconMap`)\n- Title (bold if unread), body text, relative timestamp\n- Unread indicator: 8pt blue dot on right\n- Swipe-to-delete: red background reveals behind row\n\n**Data sources:**\n- `GET /api/notifications` -- all notifications for user\n- `PATCH /api/notifications` -- mark as read\n- `DELETE /api/notifications` -- delete\n\n**Notification types and icons** (from web codebase):\n| Type | Icon | Description |\n|------|------|-------------|\n| `schedule_published` | Calendar | Weekly schedule published |\n| `shift_assigned` | CalendarCheck | New shift assigned |\n| `shift_changed` | Calendar | Shift modified |\n| `shift_reminder` | Clock | Upcoming shift reminder |\n| `swap_requested` | Users | Someone requests a swap |\n| `swap_approved` | CalendarCheck | Swap request approved |\n| `swap_rejected` | CalendarX | Swap request rejected |\n| `clock_reminder` | Clock | Forgot to clock out |\n| `reservation_new` | CalendarPlus | New reservation (waiter only) |\n| `reservation_cancelled` | CalendarX | Reservation cancelled |\n| `system` | Bell | General announcement |\n\n**Interactions:**\n- Tap notification: mark as read + navigate to `action_url` target screen (see Section 8)\n- Tap \"Mark all read\": marks all as read\n- Swipe left: reveals delete button\n- Pull down on sheet: dismiss\n\n**Empty states:** Centered bell icon + \"No notifications yet\" + \"You'll see shift reminders and updates here\"\n\n**Animations:**\n- Sheet slides up with spring physics\n- Unread dot fades out when marked as read (300ms)\n- Swipe-to-delete: row slides left, delete button revealed\n\n---\n\n## 4. Tab 2 -- Schedule\n\n### 4.1 Schedule Main Screen\n\n**Route:** `(tabs)/schedule/index`\n\n**Wireframe:**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n| [Status Bar]                              |\n| My Schedule                               |\n|                                           |\n| [< prev]  Week of 24 Mar 2026  [next >] |\n|           [Today]                         |\n|                                           |\n| +--- Calendar Strip (horizontal) ----+   |\n| | Mon  Tue  Wed  Thu  Fri  Sat  Sun  |   |\n| | 24   25   26   27   28   29   30   |   |\n| |  .    .   [*]   .    .   .    .    |   |\n| +-------------------------------------+   |\n| (* = today, highlighted. Dots = has shift)|\n|                                           |\n| +--- Monday 24 Mar ------- [Morning] -+  |\n| |  10:00 - 17:00                       |  |\n| |  Break: 30 min                       |  |\n| |  Zone: Terrace                       |  |\n| +--------------------------------------+  |\n|                                           |\n| +--- Tuesday 25 Mar ------ [Afternoon]+  |\n| |  17:00 - 00:00                       |  |\n| |  Break: 30 min                       |  |\n| +--------------------------------------+  |\n|                                           |\n| +--- Wednesday 26 Mar ---- [Day Off] -+  |\n| |  No shift scheduled                  |  |\n| +--------------------------------------+  |\n|                                           |\n| ... (remaining days)                      |\n|                                           |\n| +--- Week Summary ----------------------+|\n| |  Total Hours: 32.5h  |  Days Off: 2  ||\n| +----------------------------------------+|\n|                                           |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Layout:**\n- `ScrollView` with `RefreshControl`\n- Fixed header: \"My Schedule\" title\n- Week navigation: left/right chevrons + centered week label + \"Today\" button\n- Calendar strip: horizontal day indicators, today highlighted with primary circle, dots under days with shifts\n- Shift day cards: vertical list, one card per day (Mon-Sun), matching web's `ShiftDayCard` pattern\n- Week summary card at bottom\n\n**Components:**\n\n**Week navigation bar:**\n- Left chevron: previous week\n- Right chevron: next week  \n- \"Today\" button: jumps to current week\n- Center label: \"Week of {dd MMM yyyy}\" format\n\n**Calendar strip:**\n- 7 columns, fixed width\n- Day abbreviation (Mon/Tue/etc.) on top, date number below\n- Today: date number in filled primary circle\n- Days with shifts: small dot below date (color matches shift type)\n- Days off: no dot\n- Tapping a day scrolls the list to that day's card\n\n**Shift day cards** (replicates web `ShiftDayCard`):\n- Header: \"{Day name} {date}\" left-aligned, shift type badge right-aligned\n- Shift type badge colors from `SHIFT_TYPE_CONFIG`:\n  - Morning (M): amber background\n  - Afternoon (T): orange background\n  - Night (N): blue background\n  - Split (P): emerald background\n  - Day Off (D): gray/muted\n- Body: Start time - End time in bold\n- For split shifts: second time range below\n- Break duration shown\n- Zone assignment if applicable\n- Notes if any (from `shift.notes`)\n- Tapping card opens shift detail modal\n\n**Week summary card:**\n- Two-column layout: \"Total Hours: {X}h\" | \"Days Off: {X}\"\n- Hours calculated from `SHIFT_TYPE_CONFIG` hours values\n\n**Data sources:**\n- `GET /api/staff/shifts?employee_id={id}&start_date={weekStart}&end_date={weekEnd}` -- week's shifts\n- Employee ID resolved from `profiles.id` -> `employees.profile_id` mapping (stored locally after login)\n\n**Interactions:**\n- Swipe left/right on calendar strip: navigate weeks\n- Tap day in calendar strip: scroll to that day's card\n- Tap prev/next chevrons: navigate weeks\n- Tap \"Today\": jump to current week\n- Tap shift card: open shift detail modal (see 4.2)\n- Pull-to-refresh: reload shifts\n- Long press shift card: show \"Request Swap\" option\n\n**Empty states:**\n- No shifts for entire week: large calendar icon + \"No shifts this week\" + \"Your schedule will appear here when published\"\n- Individual day without shift: card shows \"No shift scheduled\" with dashed border\n\n**Error states:**\n- Network error: \"Unable to load schedule. Pull down to retry.\"\n- Stale data indicator: if data older than 5 minutes and offline, show small \"Last updated: X min ago\" text\n\n**Animations:**\n- Week transition: cards cross-fade when navigating weeks (200ms)\n- Calendar strip day selection: circle scales up under finger on press\n- Scroll-to-day: smooth scroll with deceleration\n\n---\n\n### 4.2 Shift Detail Modal\n\n**Route:** `(tabs)/schedule/[shiftId]` (presented as modal)\n\n**Wireframe:**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n|  [X Close]        Shift Details          |\n|                                           |\n| +--- Header Card ---+                    |\n| |  [Morning icon]   |                    |\n| |  Morning Shift     |                    |\n| |  Monday, 24 Mar    |                    |\n| +--------------------+                    |\n|                                           |\n|  SCHEDULE                                 |\n|  Start        10:00                       |\n|  End          17:00                       |\n|  Break        30 minutes                  |\n|  Total        6.5 hours                   |\n|                                           |\n|  (For split shifts:)                      |\n|  Block 1      10:00 - 14:00              |\n|  Block 2      18:00 - 22:00              |\n|  Total        8.0 hours                   |\n|                                           |\n|  ZONE ASSIGNMENT                          |\n|  Terrace (Section A)                      |\n|                                           |\n|  NOTES                                    |\n|  \"VIP group arriving at 12:00\"           |\n|                                           |\n|  STATUS                                   |\n|  [Scheduled] badge                        |\n|                                           |\n| +----------------------------------------+|\n| | [Request Shift Swap]  (outline button) ||\n| +----------------------------------------+|\n|                                           |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Layout:**\n- Modal presentation (slide up from bottom on iOS, bottom sheet on Android)\n- Close button top-left\n- Scroll view content\n- Action button pinned at bottom\n\n**Components:**\n- Shift type icon + colored header card\n- Key-value detail rows with label-value alignment\n- Notes section (only shown if `shift.notes` is not null)\n- Status badge: \"Scheduled\" (default), \"In Progress\" (green), \"Completed\" (gray), \"Cancelled\" (red strikethrough)\n- \"Request Shift Swap\" button (navigates to swap request flow)\n\n**Data sources:**\n- Shift data passed via navigation params or fetched from `GET /api/staff/shifts/{id}`\n- Zone assignment from `zone_assignments` table (joined)\n\n**Interactions:**\n- Tap X: dismiss modal\n- Swipe down: dismiss modal\n- Tap \"Request Shift Swap\": navigate to swap request flow (4.3)\n\n**Empty states:** N/A (always has shift data if opened).\n\n**Error states:**\n- Shift not found: \"This shift is no longer available\" with back button\n\n**Animations:**\n- Modal slides up with spring physics\n- Dismiss: slides down\n\n---\n\n### 4.3 Swap Request Flow\n\n**Route:** `(tabs)/schedule/swap-request` (modal stack)\n\n**Wireframe (Step 1 -- Select Colleague):**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n| [< Back]     Swap Shift                  |\n|                                           |\n|  You want to swap:                        |\n|  +--- Your Shift Card --------+          |\n|  |  Mon 24 Mar - Morning      |          |\n|  |  10:00 - 17:00              |          |\n|  +-----------------------------+          |\n|                                           |\n|  Select a colleague to swap with:         |\n|                                           |\n|  [Search colleagues...]                  |\n|                                           |\n|  +--- Carlos Rodriguez --------+         |\n|  | [Avatar] Waiter              |         |\n|  |  Available                   |         |\n|  +------------------------------+         |\n|                                           |\n|  +--- Ana Martinez -------------+         |\n|  | [Avatar] Waiter              |         |\n|  |  Available                   |         |\n|  +------------------------------+         |\n|                                           |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Wireframe (Step 2 -- Confirm):**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n| [< Back]     Confirm Swap                |\n|                                           |\n|  Your Shift:                              |\n|  Mon 24 Mar - Morning 10:00-17:00        |\n|                                           |\n|  Swap with:                               |\n|  [Avatar] Carlos Rodriguez               |\n|                                           |\n|  Reason (optional):                       |\n|  [___________________________________]   |\n|  [___________________________________]   |\n|                                           |\n|  [     Send Swap Request     ]   (CTA)   |\n|                                           |\n|  Note: Your colleague and manager         |\n|  will need to approve this swap.          |\n|                                           |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Data sources:**\n- `GET /api/staff/employees` -- list of colleagues (same role or compatible)\n- `POST /api/staff/swap-requests` -- create swap request with `{ shift_id, offered_to, reason }`\n\n**Interactions:**\n- Tap colleague row: select and advance to step 2\n- Tap \"Send Swap Request\": POST request, show success toast, navigate back\n- Search field: filter colleagues by name\n\n**Empty states:**\n- No colleagues available: \"No colleagues available for swap at this time\"\n\n**Error states:**\n- Cannot swap own shift: \"You can only swap your own shifts\" (should not happen in normal flow)\n- API error: \"Unable to send swap request. Please try again.\"\n\n**Animations:**\n- Step transition: horizontal slide (step 1 slides left, step 2 slides in from right)\n- Success: checkmark animation + auto-dismiss after 2s\n\n---\n\n## 5. Tab 3 -- Clock\n\n### 5.1 Clock Main Screen\n\n**Route:** `(tabs)/clock/index`\n\n**Wireframe (Not Clocked In):**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n| [Status Bar]                              |\n| Time Clock                [History]      |\n|                                           |\n|              14:32:05                     |\n|         Monday, 24 March 2026            |\n|                                           |\n| +--- Today's Shift --+                   |\n| |  Morning Shift      |                   |\n| |  10:00 - 17:00      |                   |\n| +---------------------+                   |\n|                                           |\n|         Not clocked in                    |\n|                                           |\n|      +--------------------+               |\n|      |                    |               |\n|      |    CLOCK IN        |               |\n|      |    [large circle   |               |\n|      |     button]        |               |\n|      |                    |               |\n|      +--------------------+               |\n|                                           |\n|  [Location pin] Within restaurant area   |\n|           or                              |\n|  [Warning] Outside restaurant (342m)     |\n|                                           |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Wireframe (Clocked In):**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n| [Status Bar]                              |\n| Time Clock                [History]      |\n|                                           |\n|              14:32:05                     |\n|         Monday, 24 March 2026            |\n|                                           |\n| +--- Working ---- [Active badge] ------+ |\n| |  Clocked in at: 10:02                 | |\n| |  Duration: 04:30:05   (live counter)  | |\n| |  Started 4 hours ago                  | |\n| +---------------------------------------+ |\n|                                           |\n| [!] 6h+ without break — Spanish law     |\n|     requires 15 min break (ET Art. 34.4) |\n|                                           |\n|  [Start Break]      [End Break]          |\n|   (outline)          (disabled/orange)   |\n|                                           |\n|      +--------------------+               |\n|      |                    |               |\n|      |    CLOCK OUT       |               |\n|      |    [large circle   |               |\n|      |     button - red]  |               |\n|      |                    |               |\n|      +--------------------+               |\n|                                           |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Layout:**\n- No scroll needed (fits in viewport)\n- Large centered clock display (48pt mono font)\n- Date below clock (16pt)\n- Today's shift info card (if scheduled)\n- Status area: changes between \"Not clocked in\" and working info\n- Large circular action button (120pt diameter) centered\n- Break buttons (two half-width buttons) above main button\n- Geofence status at bottom\n- \"History\" text button in header\n\n**Components:**\n\n**Live clock display:**\n- `HH:MM:SS` format, updates every second via `setInterval`\n- 48pt monospace font, primary color when working, muted when not\n- Full date below in caption text\n\n**Today's shift card:**\n- Compact card showing scheduled shift type + time range\n- Only shown if employee has a shift today\n- If no shift today, hidden entirely\n\n**Geofence status indicator:**\n- Uses `expo-location` to get current position\n- Calculates distance from restaurant coordinates (lat: 39.5021, lng: 2.7392, radius: 200m)\n- Green pin + \"Within restaurant area\" if within 200m\n- Amber warning + \"Outside restaurant area ({X}m away)\" if outside\n- If location permission denied: \"Location unavailable\" with info icon\n\n**Clock In button (not clocked in state):**\n- 120pt circle, primary color fill, white \"CLOCK IN\" text + play icon\n- Disabled state with spinner during API call\n- Haptic feedback (medium impact) on press\n- On press: requests geolocation, then calls `POST /api/staff/clock?action=in`\n\n**Working state info:**\n- \"Active\" badge (green)\n- Clocked in time: \"10:02\"\n- Live duration counter: \"04:30:05\" updating every second\n- Relative time: \"Started 4 hours ago\"\n\n**6-hour break reminder** (from web's `SIX_HOURS_MS` constant):\n- Shown when `elapsed >= 6 hours` and not on break\n- Amber/destructive alert card\n- Text: \"You have worked 6+ hours without a break. Spanish law (ET Art. 34.4) requires a minimum 15-minute break.\"\n\n**Break buttons:**\n- \"Start Break\" (outline): enabled when clocked in and not on break\n- \"End Break\" (orange outline): enabled only when on break\n- When on break: shows orange \"On Break\" badge in header\n\n**Clock Out button (clocked in state):**\n- 120pt circle, destructive red fill, white \"CLOCK OUT\" text + stop icon\n- On press: calls `POST /api/staff/clock?action=out`, receives `ClockOutSummary`\n- After clock out: navigates to post-shift survey (5.2)\n\n**Data sources:**\n- `GET /api/staff/clock?employee_id={id}` -- current clock status (active record check)\n- `GET /api/staff/shifts?employee_id={id}&start_date={today}&end_date={today}` -- today's shift\n- `POST /api/staff/clock?action=in` -- clock in (sends `{ latitude, longitude }`)\n- `POST /api/staff/clock?action=out` -- clock out (sends `{ clock_record_id }`)\n- `POST /api/staff/clock/break` -- start/end break (sends `{ clock_record_id, action: 'start'|'end' }`)\n\n**Interactions:**\n- Tap Clock In: geolocation capture -> API call -> transition to working state\n- Tap Clock Out: API call -> receive summary -> navigate to survey\n- Tap Start Break: start break, button disables, End Break enables\n- Tap End Break: end break, swap button states\n- Tap \"History\": navigate to clock history screen (5.3)\n- Pull-to-refresh: re-fetch clock status\n\n**Empty states:**\n- No scheduled shift today: shift card hidden, only clock buttons shown\n\n**Error states:**\n- Geolocation denied: \"Location permission required for clock-in. Enable in device settings.\" with button to open settings\n- Already clocked in (on another device): \"You are already clocked in. Clock out first.\"\n- API error: toast with \"Unable to clock in/out. Please try again.\"\n- Outside geofence: clock-in still allowed but warning stored. Server response includes `geolocation_warning`.\n- Clock-in warnings from server (early/late for shift): shown as amber toast\n\n**Animations:**\n- Clock In/Out button: pulsing glow animation when ready to press\n- Press: button scales down to 0.9, then back to 1.0 with haptic\n- State transition (not clocked in -> working): card cross-fade (300ms)\n- Duration counter: numbers change without layout shift (monospace ensures fixed width)\n- Break alert slides in from top (300ms spring)\n\n---\n\n### 5.2 Post-Shift Survey (Modal)\n\n**Route:** `(tabs)/clock/survey` (presented as modal after clock out)\n\nThis replicates the web's `PostShiftSurvey` component with its multi-step flow.\n\n**Wireframe (Step 1 -- Anomaly Detection):**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n|  [Drag handle]                            |\n|  Post-Shift Feedback                      |\n|  Optional - help us improve               |\n|                                           |\n| [!] You worked 35 minutes longer than    |\n|     your scheduled shift.                 |\n|                                           |\n|  Why did this happen?                     |\n|  +--- [High demand]          -------+    |\n|  +--- [Understaffed]         -------+    |\n|  +--- [Equipment issue]     -------+    |\n|  +--- [Personal decision]   -------+    |\n|  +--- [Other]                -------+    |\n|                                           |\n|  [Skip]              [Next ->]           |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Wireframe (Step 2 -- Emoji Rating):**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n|  Post-Shift Feedback                      |\n|                                           |\n|  How was your shift today?                |\n|                                           |\n|   [angry] [sad] [meh] [happy] [great]    |\n|                                           |\n|  [Skip]              [Next ->]           |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Wireframe (Step 3 -- Optional Comment):**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n|  Post-Shift Feedback                      |\n|                                           |\n|  Anything else you'd like to share?       |\n|  [___________________________________]   |\n|  [___________________________________]   |\n|  [___________________________________]   |\n|                          487 chars left   |\n|                                           |\n|  [Skip]              [Submit]            |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Logic flow** (matches web `PostShiftSurvey`):\n1. If `ClockOutSummary` has anomaly (overtime >15min, undertime >15min, or break variance >15min from `calculateShiftVariance()`): show Step 1 (Anomaly)\n2. If no anomaly: skip directly to Step 2 (Rating)\n3. Step 2: Emoji rating (5 emojis: angry, sad, neutral, happy, great)\n4. Step 3: Optional text feedback (max 500 chars)\n5. Submit: `POST /api/staff/surveys`\n6. Done: checkmark animation, auto-dismiss after 3s\n\n**Data sources:**\n- `ClockOutSummary` passed from clock-out response\n- `POST /api/staff/surveys` -- submit survey data\n\n**Interactions:**\n- Tap anomaly reason: select (highlight)\n- Tap emoji: select with scale animation\n- Tap Skip at any step: dismiss modal\n- Tap Submit: post data, show success\n- Swipe down: dismiss (same as skip)\n\n**Animations:**\n- Step transitions: horizontal slide\n- Emoji selection: scale up 1.0 -> 1.15 with ring highlight\n- Success checkmark: draws in with stroke animation\n- Auto-dismiss: fade out after 3s\n\n---\n\n### 5.3 Clock History Screen\n\n**Route:** `(tabs)/clock/history`\n\n**Wireframe:**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n| [< Back]     Clock History               |\n|                                           |\n|  Total Worked: 127.5h                    |\n|                                           |\n| +--- Mar 24 (Today) ---- [Active] -----+|\n| |  Clock In:   10:02                     ||\n| |  Clock Out:  —                         ||\n| |  Break:      —                         ||\n| |  Duration:   Working...                ||\n| +----------------------------------------+|\n|                                           |\n| +--- Mar 23 (Sunday) --- [Completed] --+|\n| |  Clock In:   17:05                     ||\n| |  Clock Out:  00:12                     ||\n| |  Break:      15m                       ||\n| |  Duration:   6h 52m                    ||\n| +----------------------------------------+|\n|                                           |\n| +--- Mar 22 (Saturday) - [Completed] --+|\n| |  Clock In:   10:01                     ||\n| |  Clock Out:  17:08                     ||\n| |  Break:      32m                       ||\n| |  Duration:   6h 35m                    ||\n| +----------------------------------------+|\n|                                           |\n| ... (scrollable, last 30 records)         |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Layout:**\n- Stack screen with back button\n- Total worked hours summary at top\n- `FlatList` of clock records, ordered by most recent first\n- Each record is a card with 4 rows: clock in, clock out, break, duration\n\n**Components:**\n- Total worked header: large bold text showing sum of all completed records\n- Record cards matching web's `ClockHistory` table but in card format for mobile\n- Status badge: \"Active\" (green) for open records, \"Completed\" (gray) for closed\n- Break display: total break minutes, or \"Active\" badge if break in progress\n\n**Data sources:**\n- `GET /api/staff/clock?employee_id={id}` -- all clock records (limited to last 30)\n\n**Interactions:**\n- Pull-to-refresh\n- Scroll to load more (pagination if implemented)\n- Tap record: expand to show break details (if multiple breaks)\n\n**Empty states:** Clock icon + \"No clock records yet\" + \"Your time entries will appear here\"\n\n**Animations:**\n- Cards fade in staggered on load\n\n---\n\n## 6. Tab 4 -- Chat\n\n### 6.1 Chat Main Screen\n\n**Route:** `(tabs)/chat/index`\n\n**Wireframe:**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n| [Status Bar]                              |\n| Chat                                      |\n|                                           |\n| +--- Segment Control --------+           |\n| | [Announcements] | [Team]   |           |\n| +-----------------------------+           |\n|                                           |\n| === ANNOUNCEMENTS VIEW ===               |\n|                                           |\n| +--- Pinned --------------------------+ |\n| | [Pin] New summer cocktail menu       | |\n| |   Published by Manager Maria         | |\n| |   March 20 at 14:30                  | |\n| +--------------------------------------+ |\n|                                           |\n| +--- Mar 23 --------------------------+ |\n| | [Cal] Schedule Week 13 published     | |\n| |   Your shifts: Mon(M), Tue(T),      | |\n| |   Thu(M), Fri(T), Sat(N)            | |\n| |   2 hours ago                         | |\n| +--------------------------------------+ |\n|                                           |\n| +--- Mar 22 --------------------------+ |\n| | [Alert] Stock alert: Heineken low    | |\n| |   Current: 2 kegs (below minimum)   | |\n| |   Yesterday at 09:15                 | |\n| +--------------------------------------+ |\n|                                           |\n| ... (scrollable feed)                     |\n|                                           |\n| === TEAM VIEW (future) ===               |\n| [Coming soon illustration]                |\n| Team chat is coming in a future update.   |\n|                                           |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Layout:**\n- Segmented control at top: \"Announcements\" (active by default) | \"Team\" (future, disabled/grayed)\n- Announcements tab: `FlatList` of notification items, pinned items at top\n- Team tab: placeholder illustration with \"Coming soon\" message\n\n**Components:**\n\n**Announcements feed:**\n- Pulls from `notifications` table, filtered to types relevant to announcements\n- Pinned items (from `data.pinned = true` if available, else most important) grouped at top with pin icon\n- Regular items sorted by `created_at` descending\n- Each card: icon, title (bold), body, sender name, timestamp\n- Role-based filtering:\n  - **waiter:** sees schedule, shift, reservation, and system notifications\n  - **bar:** sees schedule, shift, stock alerts, events, system\n  - **kitchen:** sees schedule, shift, stock alerts, menu updates, system\n  - **dj:** sees schedule, shift, events, system\n\n**Team placeholder:**\n- Centered illustration (chat bubbles graphic)\n- \"Team Chat\" heading\n- \"Coming in a future update. For now, use your team's WhatsApp group.\"\n- Link to open WhatsApp (deep link to WhatsApp group if configured)\n\n**Data sources:**\n- `GET /api/notifications` -- all notifications for current user\n- Realtime subscription via Supabase `postgres_changes` on `notifications` table (matching web hook)\n\n**Interactions:**\n- Pull-to-refresh: reload notifications\n- Tap announcement: mark as read, navigate to relevant screen based on `action_url`\n- Segment control: switch between Announcements and Team\n- Swipe left on announcement: \"Mark as read\" or \"Delete\" actions\n\n**Empty states:**\n- No announcements: megaphone icon + \"No announcements yet\" + \"Important updates from your team will appear here\"\n\n**Error states:**\n- Network error: \"Unable to load announcements. Pull down to retry.\"\n- Realtime subscription failure: falls back to manual refresh\n\n**Animations:**\n- New announcement appears at top with slide-down animation\n- Segment control: underline slides between tabs\n- Unread indicator dot pulses once then stays solid\n\n---\n\n## 7. Tab 5 -- More\n\n### 7.1 More Menu Screen\n\n**Route:** `(tabs)/more/index`\n\n**Wireframe:**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n| [Status Bar]                              |\n| More                                      |\n|                                           |\n| +--- Profile Header ---------+           |\n| | [Avatar 64pt]  Maria Lopez |           |\n| | \"Settings\"\n- Each row: icon, label, optional badge/count, chevron\n- App version at bottom center\n\n**Components:**\n\n**Profile header card:**\n- 64pt avatar circle (photo or initials with role-based background color)\n- Full name in bold\n- Role badge (colored per `roleColors` from web settings page)\n- \"Edit\" link navigates to Profile screen\n\n**Menu rows:**\n- `Availability`: calendar icon, navigates to availability screen\n- `Leave Requests`: calendar-off icon, badge with pending count, navigates to leave requests\n- `My Tasks`: clipboard icon, badge with today's task count, navigates to tasks\n- `Documents`: file-text icon, navigates to documents\n- `Training`: graduation cap icon, red dot (*) if pending/overdue training, navigates to training\n- `Info Guide`: book icon, navigates to read-only business reference\n- `Settings`: gear icon, navigates to settings\n- `Log Out`: log-out icon (red text), confirmation dialog before logout\n\n**Conditional rows by role** (from web sidebar analysis):\n- **waiter only:** No additional rows (reservations/floor plan are management features, not shown in employee app)\n- **bar only:** No additional rows (stock is management, events are view-only via announcements)\n- **kitchen only:** No additional rows\n- **dj only:** No additional rows\n\n**Data sources:**\n- Profile data from auth context (locally cached)\n- `GET /api/staff/leave?employee_id={id}&status=pending` -- pending leave count\n- `GET /api/staff/task-plans?week={current}` -- today's task count\n- Training assignments from `GET /api/staff/training/assignments` -- overdue check\n\n**Interactions:**\n- Tap any row: navigate to respective screen\n- Tap \"Edit\" or profile card: navigate to profile edit\n- Tap \"Log Out\": show confirmation dialog (\"Are you sure you want to log out?\"), then clear tokens + navigate to login\n\n**Animations:**\n- Rows highlight on press with subtle background color change\n- Profile avatar has subtle shadow/elevation\n\n---\n\n### 7.2 Profile Edit Screen\n\n**Route:** `(tabs)/more/profile`\n\n**Wireframe:**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n| [< Back]      Edit Profile      [Save]  |\n|                                           |\n|           [Avatar 96pt]                   |\n|           [Change Photo]                  |\n|                                           |\n|  Full Name                                |\n|  [Maria Lopez___________________]        |\n|                                           |\n|  Phone                                    |\n|  [+34 612 345 678_______________]        |\n|  Used for emergency contact only          |\n|                                           |\n|  Language                                 |\n|  [English                        v]      |\n|  Changes the app language                 |\n|                                           |\n|  ---- Emergency Contact ----              |\n| [+34 698 765 432_______________]        |\n|  Required by Spanish labor law            |\n|                                           |\n|  [error/success message area]            |\n|                                           |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Layout:**\n- Stack screen with back button + \"Save\" button in header\n- `KeyboardAvoidingView` + `ScrollView`\n- Avatar at top with \"Change Photo\" button\n- Form fields matching web's `ProfileForm`: full_name, phone, language, emergency_contact, emergency_phone\n\n**Components:**\n- **Avatar upload:** Tap to Please try again.\"\n- Image upload failed: toast \"Unable to upload photo. Try a smaller image.\"\n\n**Animations:**\n- Success banner slides in from top (300ms)\n- Save button transitions between text/spinner smoothly\n\n---\n\n### 7.3 Availability Screen\n\n**Route:** Shows current status, toggle buttons, reason field.\n- Only future dates are tappable. Past dates are grayed out.\n\n**Data sources:**\n- `GET /api/staff/availability?employee_id={id}&start_date={monthStart}&end_date={monthEnd}` -- existing records\n- `POST /api/staff/availability` -- yet\" + \"Your employment documents will appear here once uploaded by your manager.\"\n\n**Error states:**\n- Load failed: FileX icon + \"Failed to load documents\"\n- Download failed: toast \"Unable /api/staff/training/guide-content/{guideCode}` -- full course content (sections, checklists, glossary)\n- `POST /api/staff/training/records` -- record section viewed\n\n**Interactions:**\n- Tap section: expand/collapse accordion\n- Viewing a section marks it as viewed (POST record)\n- \"Take Test\" button enabled when all sections viewed\n- Tap \"Take Test\": navigate to test screen\n\n---\n\n#### 7.6.3 Training Test\n\n**Route:** `(tabs)/more/training/test` (modal)\n\n**Wireframe:**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n| [X Close]     Test: Food Safety          |\n|                                           |\n|  Question 3 of 10                         |\n|  [===-------]                             |\n|                                           |\n|  What temperature should cold foods       |\n|  be stored below?                         |\n|                                           |\n|  ( ) 10C                                 |\n|  (o) 5C                                  |\n|  ( ) 8C                                  |\n|  ( ) 0C                                  |\n|                                           |\n|  [< Previous]         [Next >]           |\n|                                           |\n|  --- or on final question ---             |\n|  [< Previous]         [Submit Test]      |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Data sources:**\n- `GET /api/staff/training/tests/{guideCode}` -- test questions\n- `POST /api/staff/training/tests/{guideCode}/submit` -- submit answers\n\n**Interactions:**\n- Tap answer option: select (radio behavior)\n- Navigate between questions\n- Submit: shows score result, pass/fail, explanation for wrong answers\n- Pass: creates certificate record, confetti animation\n\n---\n\n#### 7.6.4 Certificates Screen\n\n**Route:** `(tabs)/more/training/certificates`\n\n**Wireframe:**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n| [< Back]     My Certificates             |\n|                                           |\n| +--- Certificate Card ------------------+|\n| |  [Award icon]                          ||\n| |  Food Safety & Hygiene                ||\n| |  Score: 90%  |  Passed: 15 Mar 2026   ||\n| |  [Download PDF]  [Share]               ||\n| +----------------------------------------+|\n| ...                                       |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Data sources:**\n- Training records with `action = 'test_passed'`\n- `GET /api/staff/training/certificate/{guideCode}` -- download PDF\n\n**Interactions:**\n- Tap \"Download PDF\": download and open with `expo-sharing`\n- Tap \"Share\": system share sheet\n\n---\n\n### 7.7 My Tasks Screen\n\n**Route:** `(tabs)/more/tasks`\n\nReplicates the employee view of web's tasks (filtered to \"My Tasks\" only).\n\n**Wireframe:**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n| [< Back]     My Tasks                    |\n|                                           |\n| +--- Week Navigation --------+           |\n| | [<]  Week of 24 Mar  [>]  [Today]     |\n| +-----------------------------+           |\n|                                           |\n| MONDAY 24 MAR Zone: Terrace                         ||\n| +----------------------------------------+|\n|                                           |\n| TUESDAY 25 MAR                            |\n| +--- Stock check --- [High] ------------+|\n| |  [x] Count napkins inventory           ||\n| |  [ ] Report low items to manager       ||\n| +----------------------------------------+|\n|                                           |\n| No tasks for remaining days               |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Layout:**\n- Stack screen with back button\n- Week navigation (prev/next/today)\n- Tasks grouped by day, matching web's `MyWeekTasks` component\n- Each task card shows checklist items if applicable\n\n**Data sources:**\n- `GET /api/staff/task-plans?week={weekStart}` -- weekly task plan\n- Filtered to only tasks assigned to current employee\n\n**Interactions:**\n- Tap checkbox: toggle task item completion\n- Week navigation: load new week's tasks\n- Pull-to-refresh\n\n**Empty states:** ListTodo icon + \"No tasks this week\"\n\n---\n\n### 7.8 Settings Screen\n\n**Route:** `(tabs)/more/settings`\n\n**Wireframe:**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n| [< Back]     Settings                    |\n|                                           |\n|  NOTIFICATIONS                            |\n|  +--------------------------------------+|\n|  | Shift Reminders          [toggle ON] ||\n|  | Schedule Changes         [toggle ON] ||\n|  | Leave   [toggle OFF]||\n|  | New Reservations         [toggle ON] ||\n|  | Cancelled Reservations   [toggle ON] ||\n|  | Birthday Alerts          [toggle OFF]||\n|  +--------------------------------------+|\n|                                           |\n|  ABOUT                                    |\n|  +--------------------------------------+|\n|  | App Version              v2.1.0     ||\n|  | Terms of Service                 [>]||\n|  | Privacy Policy                   [>]||\n|  +--------------------------------------+|\n|                                           |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Layout:**\n- Stack screen with back button\n- Grouped list: \"Notifications\" section with 10 toggle switches, \"About\" section\n- Notification toggles match web's 10 notification types from `NOTIFICATION_TYPES` constant\n- Note: The web has 2 channels (in_app, email). Mobile only shows push toggle (combining in_app + push). Email preferences are not shown in mobile app.\n\n**Components:**\n- Toggle switches per notification type\n- Each toggle has label and description\n- Toggling immediately saves via API\n\n**Data sources:**\n- `GET /api/settings/notifications` -- current preferences\n- `PATCH /api/settings/notifications` -- update preference\n\n**Interactions:**\n- Toggle switch: immediate save, subtle haptic\n- Tap \"Terms of Service\": open in-app browser\n- Tap \"Privacy Policy\": open in-app browser\n\n---\n\n### 7.9 Info Guide Screen\n\n**Route:** `(tabs)/more/info-guide`\n\n**Wireframe:**\n```\n+------------------------------------------+\n| [< Back]     Business Reference          |\n|                                           |\n| +--- Search --------+                    |\n| | [Search guides...] |                    |\n| +--------------------+                    |\n|                                           |\n|  MENU & OFFERINGS                         |\n|  +--------------------------------------+|\n|  | Happy Hour times and pricing         ||\n|  | Daily specials schedule              ||\n|  | Allergen information reference       ||\n|  +--------------------------------------+|\n|                                           |\n|  OPERATIONS                               |\n|  +--------------------------------------+|\n|  | Opening hours by season              ||\n|  | Emergency procedures                 ||\n|  | Contact numbers (suppliers, etc.)    ||\n|  +--------------------------------------+|\n|                                           |\n|  POLICIES                                 |\n|  +--------------------------------------+|\n|  | Dress code                           ||\n|  | Tips policy                          ||\n|  | Phone usage policy                   ||\n|  +--------------------------------------+|\n|                                           |\n+------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n**Layout:**\n- Stack screen with back button\n- Search bar at top\n- Categorized list of reference articles\n- Tap article: expand accordion or navigate to detail view\n\n**Data sources:**\n- Static content embedded in app (no API, no AI)\n- Content curated by management, bundled in app update\n\n**Interactions:**\n- Search: filter articles by keyword\n- Tap article: expand or navigate to full content\n- Pull-to-refresh: N/A (static content)\n\n**Empty states:** N/A (always has content).\n\n---\n\n## 8. Push Notification Routing\n\n### 8.1 Push Token Registration\n\nOn successful login:\n1. Request push notification permission via `expo-notifications`\n2. Get Expo push token or APNs/FCM token\n3. Register with server: `POST /api/notifications/register-device` with `{ token, platform, device_id }`\n4. Store token locally to detect changes\n\nOn logout: unregister token.\n\n### 8.2 Notification Tap -> Screen Routing\n\nWhen user taps a push notification, the app should navigate to the appropriate screen based on the notification `type` field:\n\n| Notification Type | Deep Link Route | Screen |\n|---|---|---|\n| `schedule_published` | `/(tabs)/schedule` | Schedule tab, current week |\n| `shift_assigned` | `/(tabs)/schedule` | Schedule tab, scroll to shift date |\n| `shift_changed` | `/(tabs)/schedule` | Schedule tab, scroll to changed shift |\n| `shift_reminder` | `/(tabs)/clock` | Clock tab (ready to clock in) |\n| `swap_requested` | `/(tabs)/schedule/swap-request?id={swap_id}` | Swap request detail |\n| `swap_approved` | `/(tabs)/schedule` | Schedule tab |\n| `swap_rejected` | `/(tabs)/schedule` | Schedule tab |\n| `clock_reminder` | `/(tabs)/clock` | Clock tab |\n| `task_assigned` | `/(tabs)/more/tasks` | My Tasks |\n| `training_due` | `/(tabs)/more/training` | Training list |\n| `leave_approved` | `/(tabs)/more/leave-requests` | Leave requests |\n| `leave_rejected` | `/(tabs)/more/leave-requests` | Leave requests |\n| `stock_alert` | `/(tabs)/chat` | Chat (announcements feed) |\n| `reservation_new` | `/(tabs)/chat` | Chat (announcements feed) |\n| `reservation_cancelled` | `/(tabs)/chat` | Chat (announcements feed) |\n| `birthday_alert` | `/(tabs)` | Home |\n| `system` | `/(tabs)/chat` | Chat (announcements feed) |\n\n### 8.3 Foreground Notification Handling\n\nWhen app is in foreground:\n- Show in-app notification banner (slide down from top, auto-dismiss 5s)\n- Banner shows icon, title, body\n- Tap banner: navigate to appropriate screen\n- Swipe up: dismiss\n\n### 8.4 Background Notification Handling\n\n- Badge count updated on app icon\n- When app opens from background: check for missed notifications, show unread count on Home tab bell\n\n---\n\n## 9. Global Error & Offline States\n\n### 9.1 Network Connectivity\n\n**Detection:** Use `@react-native-community/netinfo` to monitor connectivity.\n\n**Offline banner:**\n- Persistent yellow banner at top of screen (below status bar)\n- Text: \"No internet connection\" with Wi-Fi-off icon\n- Shown on all screens when offline\n- Auto-dismisses when connection restored (with green \"Back online\" flash for 2s)\n\n**Behavior when offline:**\n- All screens show cached data if available\n- Action buttons (clock in/out, submit requests) are disabled with tooltip \"Requires internet connection\"\n- Pull-to-refresh shows error: \"Unable to refresh. Check your connection.\"\n\n### 9.2 Auth Session Expiry\n\n**Detection:** Any API response returning 401.\n\n**Behavior:**\n1. Show alert: \"Session Expired. Please log in again.\"\n2. Clear stored tokens\n3. Navigate to login screen with `router.replace('/(auth)/login')`\n4. Preserve last-used email in the login form\n\n### 9.3 Server Errors (5xx)\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Show toast: \"Something went wrong. Please try again.\"\n- Log error details to console (or crash reporting service)\n- If repeated failures (3+ in 30 seconds): show full-screen error with \"Retry\" button\n\n### 9.4 App Update Required\n\n**Detection:** Server response header `X-Min-App-Version` comparison.\n\n**Behavior:**\n- If current app version < min required: show blocking modal\n- \"Update Required. A new version is available. Please update to continue.\"\n- Single button: \"Update Now\" (opens App Store / Play Store)\n\n---\n\n## Appendix A: Key File References from Codebase\n\nThe following web codebase files informed
