Global Design System\n\n### 1.1 Navigation Structure\n\n```\n(auth)\n  _layout.tsx          -- Stack navigator, no tabs visible\n  login.tsx\n  onboarding.tsx\n\n(tabs)\n  _layout.tsx          -- Bottom tab bar with 5 tabs\n  (home)\n    index.tsx\n  (schedule)\n    index.tsx\n    [shiftId].tsx\n    swap-request.tsx\n  (clock)\n    index.tsx\n    history.tsx\n    survey.tsx\n  (chat)\n    index.tsx\n    [channelId].tsx\n  (more)\n    index.tsx\n    profile.tsx\n    availability.tsx\n    leave-requests.tsx\n    leave-request-new.tsx\n    documents.tsx\n    training/index.tsx\n    training/[guideCode].tsx\n    training/test/[guideCode].tsx\n    settings.tsx\n    settings/notifications.tsx\n    info-guide.tsx\n```\n\n### 1.2 Color Tokens (from existing OKLch system)\n\n| Token | Usage |\n|---|---|\n| `primary` | Buttons, active tab icon, accent borders |\n| `success` (green) | Clocked in badge, completed states |\n| `destructive` (red) | Errors, urgent badges, clock out button |\n| `amber-500` | Morning shift badge, break reminder |\n| `orange-500` | Afternoon shift badge, on-break badge |\n| `blue-500` | Night shift badge, weekly hours icon |\n| `emerald-500` | Split shift badge |\n| `muted-foreground` | Secondary text, placeholders |\n\n### 1.3 Shift Type Color Mapping (from `SHIFT_TYPE_CONFIG`)\n\n| Shift | Code | Background | Text |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| Morning | M | `amber-500/15` | `amber-700` |\n| Afternoon | T | `orange-500/15` | `orange-700` |\n| Night | N | `blue-500/15` | `blue-700` |\n| Split | P | `emerald-500/15` | `emerald-700` |\n| Day Off | D | `muted/50` | `muted-foreground` |\n\n### 1.4 Typography Scale\n\n- **Large title**: 28pt bold (screen headers)\n- **Title**: 20pt semibold (card headers)\n- **Headline**: 17pt semibold (section headers)\n- **Body**: 15pt regular (content)\n- **Subhead**: 13pt regular (secondary content)\n- **Caption**: 11pt regular (timestamps, metadata)\n- **Mono**: Monospace family for clock displays and time values\n\n### 1.5 Spacing System\n\n- Screen horizontal padding: 16pt\n- Card internal padding: 16pt\n- Section gap: 24pt\n- Card gap: 12pt\n- Inline element gap: 8pt\n- Minimum touch target: 44x44pt\n\n### 1.6 Global Error Handling\n\nAll screens share a common error treatment:\n\n- **Network offline**: Full-width banner at top of screen, amber background, icon + \"No connection -- showing cached data\" text. Banner is sticky and dismisses automatically when connectivity returns.\n- **Auth expired (401)**: Redirect to `/(auth)/login` with a toast \"Session expired, please log in again.\" Clear stored tokens.\n- **Server error (500)**: Inline error card replacing content area with retry button. Message: \"Something went wrong. Tap to retry.\"\n- **Validation error (400)**: Inline field-level error messages in red below the offending input.\n\n### 1.7 Global Animations\n\n- **Screen transitions**: Expo Router default stack push (right-to-left slide, 300ms ease-in-out). Tab switches use cross-fade (200ms).\n- **Pull-to-refresh**: Native platform indicator (iOS spinner / Android circular).\n- **List items appearing**: Staggered fade-in + translateY(8px) over 150ms, 30ms delay per item, max 10 items animated.\n- **Button press**: Scale down to 0.97 on press, spring back on release (150ms).\n- **Badge count change**: Scale pulse (1.0 to 1.2 to 1.0, 200ms) when unread count changes.\n- **Clock timer**: No animation -- the timer text updates every second with direct value replacement (no transitions to avoid jank).\n\n---\n\n## 2. Authentication & Onboarding\n\n### 2.1 Login Screen\n\n**Screen name**: Login\n**Route**: `/(auth)/login`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- Status bar: light content\n- Full-screen gradient background (`from-secondary via-background to-muted`, matching web)\n- Vertically centered content container, max-width 340pt, horizontal padding 24pt\n- **Logo block** (top): `logoheader.png` image, 64x64pt, centered. Below: \"GrandCafe Cheers\" in 24pt bold. Below: \"Management Platform\" in 13pt muted-foreground.\n- **Gap**: 32pt\n- **Language selector row**: 4 flag buttons (EN, NL, ES, DE) in a horizontal row, 44x44pt each, rounded-full. Selected flag has `primary` ring-2 border. Flags are emoji: GB, NL, ES, DE. Tapping changes the app locale immediately (stored in AsyncStorage under `locale` key, sent as `Accept-Language` header on all API calls).\n- **Gap**: 24pt\n- **Email input**: Full width, rounded-lg border, 48pt height, placeholder \"email@example.com\", keyboard type `email-address`, autocomplete `email`, auto-capitalize off.\n- **Gap**: 12pt\n- **Password input**: Full width, rounded-lg border, 48pt height, placeholder \"Password\", secure text entry, show/hide toggle eye icon on right side. Autocomplete `current-password`.\n- **Gap**: 12pt\n- **Remember me row**: Horizontal layout. Left: toggle switch (default ON). Right: \"Remember me\" in 13pt body text. When ON, stores Supabase refresh token in SecureStore. When OFF, stores only in memory (clears on app kill).\n- **Gap**: 16pt\n- **Sign In button**: Full width, 48pt height, `primary` background, \"Sign In\" in 15pt bold white. Disabled state at 50% opacity when loading.\n- **Loading state**: Button text replaced with spinner + \"Signing in...\" when request is in flight.\n- **Error state**: Below button, rounded-md card with `destructive/15` background, error message in 13pt `destructive` text. Appears with fade-in 200ms. Dismisses on next tap of Sign In.\n- **Gap**: 32pt\n- **Footer**: \"Carrer de Cartago 22, El Arenal, Mallorca\" in 11pt muted-foreground, centered. Below: \"@cheersmallorca\" in 11pt muted-foreground.\n\n**Data sources**:\n- `POST /api/auth/login` (Supabase `signInWithPassword`)\n- Response returns: `session.access_token`, `session.refresh_token`, profile object with `role`, `language`, `full_name`, `avatar_url`, `id`\n- On success, the app fetches the employee record: `GET /api/staff/employees?profile_id={user.id}` to get `employee_id` (needed for all subsequent API calls)\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Tap flag: Changes locale, persists to AsyncStorage, re-renders all text\n- Tap email field: Keyboard appears, email type\n- Tap password field: Keyboard appears, secure\n- Tap eye icon: Toggles secure text entry\n- Tap \"Remember me\" toggle: Toggles refresh token persistence\n- Tap \"Sign In\": Validates inputs (email format, password min 6 chars), submits login request\n- Keyboard \"Done\" on password field: Submits form\n\n**Empty states**: N/A (this is the initial screen)\n\n**Error states**:\n- Invalid credentials: \"Invalid email or password\" error card\n- Network error: \"Unable to connect. Check your internet connection.\" error card\n- Account disabled: \"Your account has been deactivated. Contact your manager.\" error card\n\n**Animations**:\n- Logo: Fade in + scale from 0.9 to 1.0 on mount (400ms ease-out)\n- Form fields: Staggered slide-up from 16pt below (200ms each, 100ms delay)\n- Error card: Fade-in + slide-down from 8pt above (200ms)\n- On successful login: Entire screen fades out (200ms) before navigating to onboarding or home\n\n---\n\n### 2.2 Onboarding Screen (First Launch Only)\n\n**Screen name**: Onboarding\n**Route**: `/(auth)/onboarding`\n\n**Shown when**: `AsyncStorage.getItem('onboarding_complete')` returns null. After completion, sets `onboarding_complete = true`.\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- Horizontal pager (3 steps), dots indicator at bottom, \"Skip\" text button top-right\n\n**Step 1 -- Welcome**:\n- Full-screen centered content\n- Large GrandCafe Cheers logo (96pt)\n- \"Welcome, {full_name}!\" in 28pt bold\n- \"Your role: {role}\" in badge format (role-colored)\n- \"Let's get you set up\" in 15pt muted-foreground\n- \"Next\" button, full width, primary\n\n**Step 2 -- Language Confirmation**:\n- \"Preferred Language\" in 20pt semibold\n- 4 language cards (stacked vertically, 64pt height each):\n  - Flag emoji (24pt) + language name in native script + language name in English (13pt muted)\n  - Selected card has primary border + checkmark\n- Current language (from profile) pre-selected\n- \"Next\" button\n\n**Step 3 -- Notification Permission**:\n- Bell icon (48pt, primary color)\n- \"Stay Updated\" in 20pt semibold\n- \"Get notified about schedule changes, new tasks, and shift reminders\" in 15pt muted-foreground, centered, max 280pt width\n- \"Enable Notifications\" button, full width, primary\n- \"Maybe Later\" text button below, muted-foreground\n- Tapping \"Enable\" triggers `Notifications.requestPermissionsAsync()` and, if granted, registers the Expo push token via `POST /api/notifications/subscribe`\n- \"Maybe Later\" skips and proceeds\n\nAfter step 3, navigates to `/(tabs)/(home)`.\n\n**Data sources**:\n- `PATCH /api/settings/profile` -- to update language if changed\n- `POST /api/notifications/subscribe` -- to register push token\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Swipe left/right between steps\n- Tap \"Skip\" top-right: Marks onboarding complete, goes to home\n- Tap language card: Selects language\n- Tap \"Enable Notifications\": Requests OS permission\n- Tap \"Maybe Later\": Skips notification setup\n\n**Empty states**: N/A\n\n**Error states**:\n- Permission denied: Show toast \"You can enable notifications later in Settings\"\n- API failure on language update: Silent retry once, then proceed anyway\n\n**Animations**:\n- Page transitions: Horizontal slide (native pager)\n- Dot indicator: Animated dot width change (active dot 24pt wide, inactive 8pt, spring animation 200ms)\n- Bell icon on step 3: Gentle shake animation (rotate -5deg to 5deg, 3 cycles, 600ms) on mount\n\n---\n\n## 3. Tab 1 -- Home\n\n### 3.1 Home Dashboard\n\n**Screen name**: Home\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(home)/index`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- **Safe area top padding**\n- **Header row**: Left: \"Hello, {first_name}\" in 28pt bold (first name extracted from `full_name`). Right: notification bell icon (24pt) with red unread count badge (if > 0). Tapping bell navigates to a notification list modal.\n- **Gap**: 8pt\n- **Date subtitle**: Today's date formatted as \"Friday, 14 March 2026\" in 13pt muted-foreground\n- **Gap**: 20pt\n\n**Section 1 -- Next Shift Card** (prominent, full width):\n- Card with rounded-xl corners, subtle shadow\n- If shift exists today or upcoming:\n  - Top line: \"{shift_type} Shift\" in shift-type-colored badge (e.g., \"Morning\" in amber badge)\n  - Title: Day name + date (e.g., \"Today\" or \"Tomorrow\" or \"Monday, 16 Mar\") in 17pt semibold\n  - Time: \"{start_time} - {end_time}\" in 20pt bold mono\n  - Split shift: Second line \"{second_start_time} - {second_end_time}\" in 13pt mono muted-foreground\n  - Break info: \"30 min break\" in 13pt muted-foreground\n  - Bottom: Countdown text \"Starts in 2h 34m\" or \"In progress\" (green badge) if currently within shift window\n- If no upcoming shifts this week:\n  - Empty illustration (calendar icon 48pt, muted at 30% opacity)\n  - \"No upcoming shifts\" in 15pt muted-foreground\n  - \"Check back later\" in 13pt muted-foreground\n\n**Section 2 -- Quick Actions Row** (horizontal scroll, 4 items):\n- Horizontally scrollable row of 4 square cards (80x80pt each, 8pt gap):\n  1. **Clock In/Out**: Clock icon + \"Clock\" text. Green dot if currently clocked in. Navigates to `/(tabs)/(clock)`.\n  2. **My Tasks**: Checklist icon + \"Tasks\" text + count badge of pending tasks. Navigates to `/(tabs)/(schedule)` with tasks tab selected.\n  3. **Swap Shift**: Arrows-swap icon + \"Swap\" text. Navigates to `/(tabs)/(schedule)/swap-request`.\n  4. **Leave**: Calendar-off icon + \"Leave\" text. Navigates to `/(tabs)/(more)/leave-requests`.\n\n**Section 3 -- Weekly Hours Summary** (compact card):\n- Card with two columns:\n  - Left column: \"This Week\" label in 11pt muted-foreground. Below: \"{hours}h {minutes}m\" in 20pt bold.\n  - Right column: \"This Month\" label in 11pt muted-foreground. Below: \"{hours}h {minutes}m\" in 20pt bold.\n- Calculated from `GET /api/staff/clock?employee_id={id}` records, identical logic to `MyHoursSummary` component (deducts break minutes for net hours).\n\n**Section 4 -- Announcements Preview** (max 2 items):\n- Section header: \"Announcements\" in 17pt semibold. Right: \"See All\" text link navigating to `/(tabs)/(chat)`.\n- List of up to 2 most recent announcement notifications (type = `system` or `schedule_published`):\n  - Each item: Icon circle (40pt) + title (15pt semibold) + body (13pt muted, single line truncated) + relative time (\"2h ago\" in 11pt muted)\n- Empty state: \"No recent announcements\" in 13pt muted-foreground\n\n**Section 5 -- Weather Widget** (compact, bottom of scroll):\n- Card with: Sun/cloud icon (24pt) + temperature (\"24C\") in 17pt bold + \"El Arenal, Mallorca\" in 11pt muted + short description (\"Sunny\") in 13pt\n- Data from a weather API call or cached value\n- If weather data unavailable: Card hidden entirely (not an error)\n\n**Data sources**:\n- `GET /api/staff/shifts?employee_id={id}&start_date={today}&end_date={today+7}` -- next shift\n- `GET /api/staff/clock?employee_id={id}` -- hours summary, active clock status\n- `GET /api/notifications?limit=5` -- announcements\n- `GET /api/staff/tasks?assigned_to={id}&status=pending` -- pending task count\n- Weather: `https://api.open-meteo.com/v1/forecast?latitude=39.5021&longitude=2.7392&current=temperature_2m,weather_code` (free, no key needed)\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Pull-to-refresh: Refetches all data sources in parallel\n- Tap next shift card: Navigates to `/(tabs)/(schedule)/[shiftId]`\n- Tap quick action cards: Navigate as described above\n- Tap notification bell: Opens notification list as a bottom sheet modal\n- Tap announcement item: Navigates to `/(tabs)/(chat)` and scrolls to that message\n- Tap \"See All\" on announcements: Navigates to `/(tabs)/(chat)`\n\n**Empty states**:\n- No shift: Described above (calendar icon + text)\n- No hours: Shows \"0h 0m\" for both week and month\n- No announcements: \"No recent announcements\" text\n- No tasks: Tasks quick action shows no badge\n\n**Error states**:\n- All sections load independently. If one fails, it shows a small inline retry. Other sections still render.\n- Full offline: Shows cached data with amber \"Offline\" banner at top\n\n**Animations**:\n- Cards: Staggered fade-in on mount (150ms each, 50ms delay)\n- Pull-to-refresh: Native platform spinner\n- Quick action tap: Scale press feedback (0.97)\n- Hours numbers: Count-up animation from 0 to final value over 400ms on first load\n\n---\n\n### 3.2 Notification List Modal\n\n**Screen name**: Notifications\n**Route**: Modal overlay (presented from Home)\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- Bottom sheet modal, 75% screen height, drag handle at top\n- **Header**: \"Notifications\" in 20pt semibold. Right: \"Mark All Read\" text button (primary color). Only shown when unreadCount > 0.\n- **List**: Scrollable FlatList of notification items\n  - Each item matches web `NotificationItem` layout:\n    - Left: Icon circle (40pt, colored by type -- same `iconMap` as web)\n    - Center: Title (15pt, semibold if unread) + body (13pt muted, max 2 lines) + relative time (11pt muted)\n    - Right: Blue unread dot (8pt circle) if unread\n  - Swipe left to reveal delete button (red background, trash icon)\n- **Empty state**: Bell icon (48pt, 30% opacity) + \"You're all caught up\" in 15pt muted-foreground\n\n**Data sources**:\n- `GET /api/notifications` -- all notifications for user\n- `PATCH /api/notifications` -- mark as read\n- `DELETE /api/notifications` -- delete notifications\n- Supabase realtime subscription on `notifications` table (same as web `useNotifications` hook)\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Tap notification: Marks as read, navigates to `action_url` if present (deep link within app)\n- Swipe left on notification: Reveals delete button\n- Tap \"Mark All Read\": Marks all unread as read\n- Pull-to-refresh: Refetches notification list\n- Drag sheet down: Dismisses modal\n\n**Animations**:\n- Sheet: Slides up from bottom (300ms spring)\n- Dismiss: Slides down (200ms ease-out)\n- Swipe-to-delete: Row slides left, delete button revealed underneath\n- Unread dot disappear: Fade out 200ms when marked read\n\n---\n\n## 4. Tab 2 -- Schedule\n\n### 4.1 Schedule Main Screen\n\n**Screen name**: My Schedule\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(schedule)/index`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- **Header**: \"Schedule\" in 28pt bold, left-aligned\n- **Calendar Strip** (horizontal, 56pt height):\n  - Horizontally scrollable row of 7 day cells for the current week\n  - Each cell: 48pt wide, contains:\n    - Day abbreviation (Mon, Tue...) in 11pt muted-foreground\n    - Day number in 15pt semibold\n    - Colored dot below (4pt circle) indicating shift type color, or no dot for day off\n  - Today's cell has `primary` circle background behind the day number (like iOS Calendar)\n  - Tapping a day scrolls the shift list to that day's content\n- **Week navigation row** (below strip):\n  - Left chevron + right chevron buttons (44x44pt touch targets)\n  - Center: \"Week of 10 Mar 2026\" in 13pt semibold\n  - \"Today\" pill button on right, navigates back to current week\n- **Gap**: 16pt\n\n**Segmented control** (below navigation, full width):\n- Two segments: \"Shifts\" (default) | \"Tasks\"\n- Standard iOS/Android segmented control style, 36pt height\n\n**When \"Shifts\" segment is selected**:\n- Vertical list of 7 day cards (matching web `ShiftDayCard` component):\n  - Each card: Full width, rounded-lg border\n    - Header row: Day name + date (left), day number (right, bold)\n    - Today's card: `primary` ring-2 border\n    - Content:\n      - If shift exists: Shift type badge (colored) + \"{start_time} - {end_time}\" in 15pt mono bold + split shift second time line if applicable\n      - If no shift: Dash badge + \"Day off\" in 13pt muted-foreground\n  - Tapping a shift card opens the shift detail modal (`/(tabs)/(schedule)/[shiftId]`)\n- **Bottom summary card**: \"Total Hours: {hours}h\" in 15pt, right-aligned bold value\n\n**When \"Tasks\" segment is selected**:\n- Matches web `MyWeekTasks` component behavior\n- Tasks grouped by day (only days with tasks shown)\n- Each day header: Day name + date in 13pt semibold muted\n- Each task card: Title (15pt) + section badge (if any) + priority badge (colored) + status badge\n- Empty state: ListTodo icon (48pt, 30% opacity) + \"No tasks this week\" in 15pt muted-foreground\n\n**Data sources**:\n- `GET /api/staff/shifts?employee_id={id}&start_date={weekStart}&end_date={weekEnd}` -- shifts for current week\n- `GET /api/staff/task-plans?week={weekStartDate}` -- planned tasks for current week\n- Shift type colors and hours from `SHIFT_TYPE_CONFIG` constant\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Swipe calendar strip horizontally: Scrolls through days (visual only, no week change)\n- Tap left/right chevron: Changes week (-7/+7 days), refetches data\n- Tap \"Today\": Resets to current week\n- Tap day cell in strip: Scrolls shift list to that day\n- Tap shift card: Opens shift detail modal\n- Tap task card: (future) Opens task detail\n- Tap segment control: Switches between Shifts and Tasks views\n- Pull-to-refresh: Refetches shifts and tasks\n\n**Empty states**:\n- No shifts this week: \"No shifts scheduled this week\" with calendar icon\n- No tasks this week: \"No tasks this week\" with checklist icon\n\n**Error states**:\n- Failed to load shifts: Error card with retry button in the shift list area\n- Failed to load tasks: Same treatment in tasks area\n\n**Animations**:\n- Week change: Shift list cross-fades (150ms)\n- Day cards: Fade-in stagger on load\n- Segment switch: Cross-fade between views (200ms)\n- Calendar strip scroll: Native scroll physics\n\n---\n\n### 4.2 Shift Detail Modal\n\n**Screen name**: Shift Detail\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(schedule)/[shiftId]`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- Full-screen modal (presented as stack push)\n- **Header**: Back arrow (left) + \"Shift Detail\" in 17pt semibold (center)\n- **Shift type hero**: Full-width colored banner (64pt height, shift type background color)\n  - Shift type label in 20pt bold (shift type text color) + date\n- **Details card**:\n  - Row: \"Time\" label + \"{start_time} - {end_time}\" value\n  - Row: \"Break\" label + \"{break_duration_minutes} min\" value\n  - Row: \"Total Hours\" label + \"{calculated_hours}h\" value\n  - Row: \"Status\" label + status badge (scheduled/in_progress/completed/cancelled)\n  - If split shift: Additional row \"Second Period\" + \"{second_start_time} - {second_end_time}\"\n  - If notes: \"Notes\" label + notes text\n- **Gap**: 24pt\n- **Actions section** (only for future shifts with status = 'scheduled'):\n  - \"Request Swap\" button, full width, outline variant. Navigates to swap request flow.\n  - (If current day) \"Go to Clock\" button, full width, primary variant. Navigates to clock tab.\n\n**Data sources**:\n- Shift data passed via navigation params (already loaded from list)\n- Fallback: `GET /api/staff/shifts/{id}` if deep-linked\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Tap back arrow: Dismisses modal\n- Swipe right from left edge: Dismisses modal (iOS gesture)\n- Tap \"Request Swap\": Navigates to `/(tabs)/(schedule)/swap-request` with `shiftId` param\n- Tap \"Go to Clock\": Switches to clock tab\n\n**Empty states**: N/A (always has shift data)\n\n**Error states**:\n- Shift not found (deep link to deleted shift): \"This shift no longer exists\" + back button\n\n**Animations**:\n- Modal: Slides up from bottom (stack push animation)\n- Colored banner: Fade-in 200ms\n\n---\n\n### 4.3 Swap Request Flow\n\n**Screen name**: Request Shift Swap\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(schedule)/swap-request`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- Full-screen (stack push)\n- **Header**: Back arrow + \"Swap Request\" in 17pt semibold\n- **Step 1 -- Select Shift** (if not pre-selected via param):\n  - List of upcoming shifts for the current user\n  - Each item: Date + shift type badge + time\n  - Tapping selects it (checkmark appears, primary ring)\n- **Step 2 -- Select Colleague**:\n  - \"Offer to\" label in 13pt muted\n  - List of employees with same role (fetched from employees endpoint, filtered by role match)\n  - Each item: Avatar circle (40pt, initials fallback) + name (15pt) + role badge (11pt)\n  - Search bar at top to filter by name\n  - Tapping selects colleague (checkmark, primary ring)\n- **Step 3 -- Add Reason** (optional):\n  - TextArea input, 4 lines, placeholder \"Why do you want to swap? (optional)\"\n  - Character counter \"0/200\" in 11pt muted-foreground, bottom-right\n- **Submit button**: Full width, primary, \"Send Swap Request\"\n  - Loading state: Spinner + \"Sending...\"\n  - Disabled until both shift and colleague selected\n- **Success state**: Replaces form with checkmark icon (48pt, green) + \"Swap request sent!\" + \"Waiting for {colleague_name} to respond\" in 13pt muted + \"Done\" button that navigates back\n\n**Data sources**:\n- `GET /api/staff/shifts?employee_id={id}&start_date={today}&status=scheduled` -- user's swappable shifts\n- `GET /api/staff/employees?employment_status=active` -- colleague list (filtered client-side by role)\n- `POST /api/staff/swap-requests` -- create swap request (body: `{ shift_id, offered_to, reason }`)\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Tap shift card: Selects shift\n- Tap employee card: Selects colleague\n- Type in search: Filters colleague list\n- Type in reason textarea: Updates reason text\n- Tap \"Send Swap Request\": Submits request\n- Tap \"Done\" on success: Navigates back to schedule\n\n**Empty states**:\n- No swappable shifts: \"No upcoming shifts to swap\" + back button\n- No eligible colleagues: \"No colleagues available\" text (unlikely but handled)\n\n**Error states**:\n- Cannot swap own shift: \"You can only swap your own shifts\" (should not occur, but API returns 403)\n- Colleague already offered: API error shown as toast\n- Network error: Error card with retry\n\n**Animations**:\n- Step transitions: Cross-fade (200ms)\n- Success: Checkmark scales up from 0 with spring animation (300ms)\n- Selected item: Border color transition (150ms)\n\n---\n\n## 5. Tab 3 -- Clock\n\n### 5.1 Clock Main Screen\n\n**Screen name**: Time Clock\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(clock)/index`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- **Header**: \"Time Clock\" in 28pt bold\n\n**Section 1 -- Current Time Display** (centered, prominent):\n- Current time in 48pt bold mono: \"14:32:07\" (updates every second)\n- Date below: \"Friday, 14 March 2026\" in 13pt muted-foreground\n- Geofence status indicator: Small dot (8pt) + text\n  - Green dot + \"At restaurant\" if within 200m of lat 39.5021, lng 2.7392\n  - Amber dot + \"Outside restaurant area\" if beyond 200m\n  - Gray dot + \"Location unavailable\" if permission denied\n\n**Section 2 -- Clock Status Card** (full width, prominent):\n\n**State A -- Not Clocked In**:\n- Dashed border card, centered content\n- Clock icon (32pt, muted at 50%)\n- \"Not clocked in\" in 15pt muted-foreground\n- **\"Clock In\" button**: Full width, 56pt height, `primary` background, large text\n  - On tap: Requests geolocation (high accuracy, 5s timeout), then calls `POST /api/staff/clock?action=in` with `{ latitude, longitude }`\n  - Loading state: Spinner + \"Clocking in...\"\n  - If geolocation denied: Proceeds without location, API may return `geolocation_warning`\n\n**State B -- Clocked In, Working**:\n- Solid border card, `success/5` background\n- Top right: \"Active\" green badge + clock-in time \"Clocked in at 09:15\" in 13pt muted\n- **Running timer**: \"05:17:23\" in 32pt bold mono, `success` color (updates every second)\n- Below timer: \"Started {relative_time}\" in 11pt muted (e.g., \"Started 5 hours ago\")\n- **Break buttons row** (2 columns, each 44pt height):\n  - \"Start Break\" button (outline, coffee icon) -- enabled\n  - \"End Break\" button (outline, coffee icon, orange text) -- disabled\n- **Mandatory break reminder** (conditional, from web `showBreakReminder`):\n  - If clocked in for 6+ hours without break: Amber alert banner\n  - Alert triangle icon + \"You have worked 6+ hours without a break. Spanish law (ET Art. 34.4) requires a minimum 15-minute break.\"\n- **\"Clock Out\" button**: Full width, 56pt height, `destructive` background\n  - On tap: Calls `POST /api/staff/clock?action=out` with `{ clock_record_id }`\n  - Returns `ClockOutSummary` and triggers post-shift survey\n\n**State C -- Clocked In, On Break**:\n- Same as State B but:\n  - \"On Break\" orange badge replaces \"Active\" badge\n  - Timer text in `orange-500` color\n  - \"Start Break\" button disabled\n  - \"End Break\" button enabled (orange border, orange text)\n  - Break started time shown: \"Break started at 12:30\" in 11pt orange\n\n**Section 3 -- Today's Scheduled Shift** (compact info card, below clock card):\n- If today has a scheduled shift:\n  - Row: Shift type badge + \"{start_time} - {end_time}\"\n  - If currently outside shift window but clocked in: \"Note: Outside scheduled hours\" in 11pt amber\n- If no shift today: \"No shift scheduled today\" in 13pt muted\n\n**Section 4 -- Quick History Link**:\n- \"View Clock History\" right-arrow link at bottom, navigates to `/(tabs)/(clock)/history`\n\n**Data sources**:\n- `GET /api/staff/clock?employee_id={id}` -- current clock status (find record without `clock_out_time`)\n- `POST /api/staff/clock?action=in` -- clock in\n- `POST /api/staff/clock?action=out` -- clock out\n- `POST /api/staff/clock/break` -- start/end break (body: `{ clock_record_id, action: 'start' | 'end' }`)\n- `GET /api/staff/shifts?employee_id={id}&date={today}` -- today's scheduled shift\n- `expo-location`: `Location.getCurrentPositionAsync({ accuracy: Location.Accuracy.High })`\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Tap \"Clock In\": Requests location, creates clock record\n- Tap \"Start Break\": Creates break record\n- Tap \"End Break\": Closes break record\n- Tap \"Clock Out\": Closes clock record, shows summary, triggers survey\n- Tap \"View Clock History\": Navigates to history screen\n- Pull-to-refresh: Refetches clock status\n\n**Empty states**:\n- Not clocked in: State A (described above)\n\n**Error states**:\n- Already clocked in: \"You are already clocked in\" toast (API returns 400)\n- Geolocation timeout: Proceed without location, show toast \"Could not determine location\"\n- Geofence violation: API returns `geolocation_warning` string, shown as amber toast with distance\n- Clock-in blocked (grace period validation from `validateClockInTiming`): API returns 403 with `shift_warning.message`, shown as error alert\n\n**Animations**:\n- Clock-in transition: State A card fades out, State B fades in (300ms cross-fade)\n- Timer update: Direct text replacement, no animation (avoids jank at 1Hz updates)\n- Clock Out button tap: Haptic feedback (medium impact)\n- Break reminder appearance: Slide down from above card (200ms)\n\n---\n\n### 5.2 Post-Shift Survey\n\n**Screen name**: Post-Shift Survey\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(clock)/survey` (or presented as modal from Clock screen)\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- Bottom sheet modal, auto-height (content-driven)\n- Presented immediately after successful clock-out\n- Matches web `PostShiftSurvey` component with 3-step flow\n\n**Step 1 -- Anomaly Detection** (conditional, only if shift variance detected):\n- Shown when `calculateShiftVariance()` returns `hasAnomaly: true`\n- Amber banner: Anomaly message (e.g., \"You worked 45 minutes longer than scheduled\")\n- List of 5 reason buttons (full width, outline, 44pt height each):\n  - \"High demand\"\n  - \"Understaffed\"\n  - \"Equipment issue\"\n  - \"Personal decision\"\n  - \"Other\" (reveals text input when selected)\n- If \"Other\" selected: TextArea (2 lines, max 500 chars)\n- Bottom row: \"Skip\" ghost button (left) + \"Next\" primary button (right, disabled until reason selected)\n- Auto-skipped if no anomaly detected\n\n**Step 2 -- Emoji Rating**:\n- \"How was your shift?\" in 15pt muted-foreground, centered\n- Row of 5 emoji buttons (each 56x56pt), horizontally centered:\n  - Emojis: \"Terrible\" \"Bad\" \"OK\" \"Good\" \"Great\" (matching `EMOJI_RATINGS = ['bad face', 'meh face', 'neutral', 'smile', 'grin']`)\n  - Selected emoji: Scale 1.15, `primary/15` background circle, ring-2 `primary/30`\n  - Unselected: Scale 1.0, transparent background\n- Bottom row: \"Skip\" + \"Next\" buttons\n\n**Step 3 -- Written Feedback**:\n- TextArea (4 lines, placeholder \"Any comments about your shift?\", max 500 chars)\n- Character counter \"500 chars remaining\" in 11pt muted, right-aligned\n- Bottom row: \"Skip\" + \"Submit\" buttons\n\n**Submitting state**: Centered spinner (32pt) replacing form content\n\n**Done state** (auto-dismisses after 3 seconds):\n- Green checkmark circle (48pt)\n- \"Thank you!\" in 17pt semibold\n- \"Your feedback helps us improve\" in 13pt muted\n\n**Error state**:\n- Red alert circle (48pt) + \"Could not save feedback\" in 13pt destructive\n- \"Skip\" + \"Retry\" buttons\n\n**Data sources**:\n- `POST /api/staff/surveys` -- submit survey (body: `{ clock_record_id, rating, feedback, anomaly_type, anomaly_reason, anomaly_comment, worked_minutes, scheduled_minutes, variance_minutes, break_variance_minutes }`)\n- `ClockOutSummary` object passed from clock-out response\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Tap emoji: Selects rating (1-5)\n- Tap reason button: Selects anomaly reason\n- Type feedback: Updates feedback text\n- Tap \"Skip\": Dismisses survey without saving (at any step)\n- Tap \"Submit\": Submits all collected data\n- Tap \"Retry\": Re-attempts submission\n\n**Animations**:\n- Sheet slides up (300ms spring)\n- Step transitions: Cross-fade (200ms)\n- Emoji selection: Scale spring animation (200ms)\n- Done checkmark: Scale from 0 with spring (300ms)\n- Auto-dismiss: Fade out (200ms) after 3s timer\n\n---\n\n### 5.3 Clock History\n\n**Screen name**: Clock History\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(clock)/history`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- Stack push from Clock screen\n- **Header**: Back arrow + \"Clock History\" in 17pt semibold. Right: Total hours \"47.2h\" in 17pt bold\n- **Summary row**: \"Last {n} records\" in 13pt muted-foreground\n\n**List** (FlatList, paginated):\n- Each row (matches web `ClockHistory` table row, but card layout for mobile):\n  - Card, full width, rounded-lg\n  - **Top row**: Date \"Mar 14, 2026\" (15pt semibold) + day name \"Friday\" (11pt muted)\n  - **Middle row** (3 columns):\n    - Clock In: clock icon (12pt) + \"09:15\" mono\n    - Clock Out: clock icon (12pt) + \"17:30\" mono (or dash if in progress)\n    - Duration: \"7h 45m\" in 15pt bold right-aligned\n  - **Bottom row**: Break info\n    - If breaks exist: coffee icon + \"{totalMinutes}m break\"\n    - If active break: Orange \"On Break\" badge\n    - If no breaks: Dash\n  - **Status badge**: Right-aligned, \"Active\" (green) or \"Completed\" (gray secondary)\n\n**Data sources**:\n- `GET /api/staff/clock?employee_id={id}&limit=50&offset={offset}` -- paginated clock records with breaks\n- Pagination: Load more on scroll (infinite scroll, 50 records per page)\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Scroll: Loads more records at end of list\n- Pull-to-refresh: Reloads from beginning\n- Tap back: Returns to Clock main screen\n\n**Empty states**:\n- No records: Clock icon (48pt, 30% opacity) + \"No clock records yet\" in 15pt muted\n\n**Error states**:\n- Failed to load: Error card with retry button\n\n**Animations**:\n- List items: Fade-in stagger on initial load\n- Load more: Subtle spinner at bottom of list\n\n---\n\n## 6. Tab 4 -- Chat\n\n### 6.1 Announcements & Team Chat\n\n**Screen name**: Chat\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(chat)/index`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- **Header**: \"Chat\" in 28pt bold\n\n**Segmented control** (full width, 36pt height):\n- Two segments: \"Announcements\" (default) | \"Team Chat\"\n\n**When \"Announcements\" selected**:\n- Chronological feed (newest first) of announcement-type notifications\n- Each announcement card:\n  - Icon circle (40pt, type-based icon from `iconMap`)\n  - Title in 15pt semibold\n  - Body in 13pt muted-foreground (full text, multi-line)\n  - Timestamp in 11pt muted-foreground (relative: \"2h ago\")\n  - If `action_url` present: Subtle right chevron indicating tappable\n- This feed combines notification types: `schedule_published`, `system`, and any broadcast-type messages\n- Empty state: Megaphone icon (48pt, 30% opacity) + \"No announcements\" + \"Check back later for updates from management\"\n\n**When \"Team Chat\" selected**:\n- **Phase 1 (MVP)**: Simple team-wide chat room\n  - Messages displayed in a standard chat bubble layout:\n    - Other users: Left-aligned, gray bubble, avatar circle (32pt) + name (11pt semibold) above bubble\n    - Current user: Right-aligned, primary-colored bubble, no avatar\n    - Message text in 15pt, timestamp in 11pt muted below bubble\n  - **Compose bar** at bottom (above keyboard):\n    - Text input (rounded-full, 40pt height, placeholder \"Type a message...\")\n    - Send button (primary circle, 36pt, arrow-up icon), disabled when input empty\n  - Messages loaded from a `team_messages` table or similar, with Supabase realtime subscription\n- **Phase 1 fallback** (if team chat table does not exist):\n  - \"Team Chat coming soon\" placeholder with chat bubbles illustration\n\n**Data sources**:\n- Announcements: `GET /api/notifications?limit=50` filtered client-side by announcement types\n- Team chat: Supabase realtime on `team_messages` table (future)\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Tap segment: Switches view\n- Tap announcement with `action_url`: Navigates to target screen\n- Pull-to-refresh: Reloads announcements or chat messages\n- Type message + tap send: Sends team chat message\n- Scroll up in chat: Loads older messages (infinite scroll)\n\n**Empty states**:\n- Announcements: As described above\n- Team chat: \"No messages yet. Say hello!\" with chat bubble icon\n\n**Error states**:\n- Failed to load announcements: Error card with retry\n- Failed to send message: Red exclamation on message bubble + \"Tap to retry\"\n\n**Animations**:\n- Segment switch: Cross-fade (200ms)\n- New announcement: Slide in from top (200ms)\n- New chat message received: Slide up from bottom (150ms)\n- Send message: Bubble appears with scale-up from 0.8 (100ms)\n\n---\n\n## 7. Tab 5 -- More\n\n### 7.1 More Menu\n\n**Screen name**: More\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(more)/index`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- **Header section**: \n  - Avatar circle (64pt, image from `avatar_url` or initials fallback in `primary/15` background)\n  - Full name in 20pt semibold\n  - Role badge (colored by role, e.g., \"Waiter\" in blue)\n  - Email in 13pt muted-foreground\n\n**Menu sections** (grouped list, iOS Settings style):\n\n**Section: \"My Account\"**:\n1. **Edit Profile** -- person icon + \"Profile\" + right chevron. Route: `/(tabs)/(more)/profile`\n2. **Availability** -- calendar-check icon + \"Availability\" + right chevron. Route: `/(tabs)/(more)/availability`\n3. **Leave Requests** -- calendar-off icon + \"Leave Requests\" + badge with pending count. Route: `/(tabs)/(more)/leave-requests`\n\n**Section: \"Work\"**:\n4. **Documents** -- file-text icon + \"Documents\" + right chevron. Route: `/(tabs)/(more)/documents`\n5. **Training** -- graduation-cap icon + \"Training & Guides\" + badge with overdue count (red) or pending count (amber). Route: `/(tabs)/(more)/training/index`\n\n**Section: \"App\"**:\n6. **Settings** -- settings icon + \"Settings\" + right chevron. Route: `/(tabs)/(more)/settings`\n7. **Info Guide** -- info icon + \"Restaurant Info\" + right chevron. Route: `/(tabs)/(more)/info-guide`\n\n**Section: \"Account\"**:\n8. **Log Out** -- log-out icon + \"Log Out\" in `destructive` color. No chevron.\n   - Tap triggers confirmation alert: \"Are you sure you want to log out?\"\n   - Confirm: Calls `supabase.auth.signOut()`, clears SecureStore tokens, navigates to `/(auth)/login`\n\n**Footer**: \"Version 1.0.0\" + \"GrandCafe Cheers\" in 11pt muted-foreground, centered\n\n**Data sources**:\n- Profile data from auth context (cached at login)\n- `GET /api/staff/leave?employee_id={id}&status=pending` -- pending leave count\n- `GET /api/staff/training/compliance` -- training compliance stats for badge counts\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Tap menu item: Navigates to respective screen\n- Tap avatar: Same as Edit Profile\n- Tap \"Log Out\": Shows confirmation alert\n- Pull-to-refresh: Refreshes badge counts\n\n**Empty states**: N/A (always shows menu items)\n\n**Error states**: Badge counts fail silently (show no badge)\n\n**Animations**:\n- Menu items: None (static list, instant render)\n- Avatar: Fade-in 200ms on image load\n\n---\n\n### 7.2 Edit Profile\n\n**Screen name**: Edit Profile\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(more)/profile`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- Stack push\n- **Header**: Back arrow + \"Edit Profile\" + \"Save\" text button (right, primary, disabled until changes made)\n\n**Avatar section** (centered):\n- Avatar circle (96pt)\n- \"Change Photo\" text button below\n- Tap opens action sheet: \"Take Photo\" | \"Choose from Library\" | \"Remove Photo\" | \"Cancel\"\n- Photo cropped to square, uploaded to Supabase Storage, URL saved to profile\n\n**Form fields** (scrollable):\n- **Full Name**: Text input, pre-filled from `profile.full_name`, required\n- **Phone**: Text input, phone keyboard type, pre-filled from `profile.phone`, optional\n- **Emergency Contact**: Text input, pre-filled from `profile.emergency_contact`, optional\n- **Emergency Phone**: Text input, phone keyboard type, pre-filled from `profile.emergency_phone`, optional\n- All inputs: Full width, rounded-lg border, 48pt height, label above in 13pt semibold\n\n**Read-only section** (\"Account Information\" header):\n- **Email**: Shown as read-only text (not editable by employee)\n- **Role**: Shown as badge\n- **Member since**: Formatted date from `profile.created_at`\n\n**Data sources**:\n- Profile data from auth context\n- `PATCH /api/settings/profile` (or Supabase direct update on `profiles` table) -- update profile fields\n- Supabase Storage -- avatar upload\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Edit text fields: Updates local form state\n- Tap \"Save\": Validates (full_name required), submits update, shows success toast \"Profile updated\"\n- Tap \"Change Photo\": Opens photo picker\n- Tap back: If unsaved changes, shows \"Discard changes?\" alert\n\n**Empty states**: N/A\n\n**Error states**:\n- Update failed: \"Could not save profile. Try again.\" error toast\n- Photo upload failed: \"Photo upload failed\" error toast, reverts to previous avatar\n\n**Animations**:\n- Save success: Brief green flash on Save button (200ms)\n- Avatar change: Cross-fade between old and new photo (300ms)\n\n---\n\n### 7.3 Availability\n\n**Screen name**: My Availability\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(more)/availability`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- Stack push\n- **Header**: Back arrow + \"Availability\"\n\n**Calendar view**: Month calendar grid (standard calendar component):\n- Days with availability set show colored indicators:\n  - Green circle: Available\n  - Red circle: Unavailable\n  - No circle: Not set (defaults to available)\n- Tapping a day opens a bottom sheet to set availability for that date\n\n**Bottom sheet** (on day tap):\n- Date shown as \"Monday, 17 March 2026\" in 15pt semibold\n- Toggle: \"Available\" (green) / \"Unavailable\" (red)\n- If unavailable: Reason text input (optional, 2 lines)\n- \"Save\" button, full width, primary\n\n**Data sources**:\n- `GET /api/staff/availability?employee_id={id}&start_date={monthStart}&end_date={monthEnd}` -- availability records\n- `POST /api/staff/availability` -- upsert availability (body: `{ employee_id, date, available, reason }`)\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Tap day on calendar: Opens availability sheet\n- Toggle available/unavailable: Updates toggle state\n- Tap \"Save\": Submits availability, refreshes calendar\n- Swipe month: Navigate between months\n- Pull-to-refresh: Reloads availability data\n\n**Empty states**:\n- No availability set for any day: Calendar shows no indicators + explanatory text below: \"Tap a day to set your availability\"\n\n**Error states**:\n- Save failed: \"Could not save availability\" error toast\n\n**Animations**:\n- Bottom sheet: Slides up (300ms spring)\n- Calendar indicator change: Fade transition (200ms)\n\n---\n\n### 7.4 Leave Requests\n\n**Screen name**: Leave Requests\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(more)/leave-requests`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- Stack push\n- **Header**: Back arrow + \"Leave Requests\" + \"+\" FAB or header button (navigates to new request)\n\n**Request list** (FlatList):\n- Each request card (matches web `MyLeaveRequests` component):\n  - Leave type label in 13pt semibold (e.g., \"Vacation\", \"Sick Leave\") -- localized via `leaveTypeLabel` map\n  - Date range: \"17 Mar 2026 to 21 Mar 2026\" in 13pt muted\n  - Duration: \"(5 days)\" in 13pt semibold\n  - Status badge: \"Pending\" (amber/secondary) | \"Approved\" (green/default) | \"Rejected\" (red/destructive)\n  - If reason exists: Reason text in 11pt muted, max 2 lines\n- Sorted by `created_at` descending\n\n**Empty state**: CalendarOff icon (48pt, 30% opacity) + \"No leave requests\" + \"Request time off\" button (outline)\n\n**Data sources**:\n- `GET /api/staff/leave?employee_id={id}` -- leave requests for employee\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Tap \"+\": Navigates to `/(tabs)/(more)/leave-request-new`\n- Pull-to-refresh: Reloads requests\n- Tap request card: (future) Shows detail/cancellation option\n\n**Error states**: Error card with retry\n\n**Animations**: List item fade-in stagger\n\n---\n\n### 7.5 New Leave Request\n\n**Screen name**: New Leave Request\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(more)/leave-request-new`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- Stack push\n- **Header**: Back arrow + \"New Request\"\n\n**Form fields**:\n- **Leave Type**: Dropdown/picker with 5 options:\n  - Vacation, Sick Leave, Personal Day, Maternity, Unpaid\n  - Default: Vacation\n- **Start Date**: Date picker, minimum = today\n- **End Date**: Date picker, minimum = start date\n- **Total Days**: Calculated automatically, shown as \"{n} day(s)\" in 13pt semibold (read-only)\n  - Calculation: `Math.max(1, differenceInCalendarDays(endDate, startDate) + 1)`\n- **Reason**: TextArea, 3 lines, optional\n- **Submit button**: Full width, primary, \"Submit Request\", disabled until start + end dates selected\n\n**Success**: Toast \"Leave request submitted\" + navigate back to leave request list\n\n**Data sources**:\n- `POST /api/staff/leave` -- create leave request (body: `{ employee_id, leave_type, start_date, end_date, total_days, reason }`)\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Select leave type: Opens native picker\n- Tap start/end date: Opens date picker\n- Type reason: Updates text\n- Tap \"Submit\": Validates and submits\n- Tap back with unsaved form: Shows \"Discard?\" alert\n\n**Error states**:\n- Validation: \"Start date must be before end date\" inline error\n- API error: \"Could not submit request\" error toast\n\n**Animations**:\n- Date picker: Native platform animation\n- Success: Navigate back with success toast\n\n---\n\n### 7.6 Documents\n\n**Screen name**: My Documents\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(more)/documents`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- Stack push\n- **Header**: Back arrow + \"Documents\"\n\n**Document list** (grouped by type):\n\n**Group headers** (one per document type):\n- \"Contracts\" | \"Payslips\" | \"ID Documents\" | \"Tax Forms\" | \"Other\"\n- Collapsed by default, tap header to expand/collapse\n\n**Document items** (within each group):\n- File icon (based on mime type: PDF icon for PDF, image icon for images)\n- File name in 15pt (truncated to 1 line)\n- Upload date in 11pt muted\n- File size in 11pt muted (if available)\n- Tap: Opens document in system viewer (Share sheet or in-app WebView for PDFs)\n\n**Data sources**:\n- `GET /api/staff/documents?employee_id={id}` -- employee documents\n- Document types: `contract`, `payslip`, `id_document`, `tax_form`, `other`\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Tap document: Opens in system viewer / share sheet\n- Tap group header: Expand/collapse\n- Pull-to-refresh: Reloads document list\n\n**Empty states**:\n- No documents: File icon (48pt, 30% opacity) + \"No documents yet\" + \"Your contracts and payslips will appear here\"\n\n**Error states**: Error card with retry\n\n**Animations**:\n- Group expand/collapse: Animated height with spring (200ms)\n- Document items within group: Fade-in stagger\n\n---\n\n### 7.7 Training & Guides\n\n**Screen name**: Training\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(more)/training/index`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- Stack push\n- **Header**: Back arrow + \"Training & Guides\"\n\n**Compliance stats card** (top):\n- 3-column summary:\n  - Completed: Green number / total (e.g., \"5/8\")\n  - Pending: Amber number\n  - Overdue: Red number\n- Progress bar below: `(completed / total) * 100`%\n\n**Category tabs** (horizontal scroll chips):\n- Chips for each `GuideCategory`: \"Food Safety\", \"Occupational Health\", \"Labor Regulations\", \"Role Specific\", \"Required Docs\", \"Environmental\"\n- \"All\" chip selected by default\n- Tapping filters the guide list\n\n**Guide list** (matches web `ResourceGuideList`):\n- Each guide card:\n  - Code badge (mono, outline) e.g., \"G-FS-001\"\n  - Status icon: Green checkmark (completed) | Amber clock (pending) | Red warning triangle (overdue) | nothing (not assigned)\n  - Title in 15pt semibold (from i18n `guides.{code}.title`)\n  - Description snippet in 13pt muted (1 line)\n  - Applicable role badges (colored chips, 10pt)\n  - Right chevron\n- Tapping navigates to `/(tabs)/(more)/training/[guideCode]`\n- List filtered by user's role (guides with `applicableRoles` containing user's role or empty `applicableRoles`)\n\n**Data sources**:\n- `GUIDES` constant (hardcoded guide metadata from `resource-guides.ts`)\n- `GET /api/staff/training/compliance` -- compliance stats\n- `GET /api/staff/training/records/{employeeId}` -- training completion status per guide\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Tap category chip: Filters list\n- Tap guide card: Navigates to guide study view\n- Pull-to-refresh: Reloads compliance stats and training records\n\n**Empty states**:\n- No guides for category: \"No guides in this category\" text\n- No training assigned: \"No training requirements for your role\"\n\n**Error states**: Error card with retry\n\n**Animations**:\n- Category chip selection: Background color transition (150ms)\n- Guide cards: Fade-in stagger\n\n---\n\n### 7.8 Guide Study View\n\n**Screen name**: Guide Study\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(more)/training/[guideCode]`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- Full-screen stack push\n- **Header**: Back arrow + guide code (e.g., \"G-FS-001\") + \"Study Material\" badge\n\n**Progress bar** (below header, sticky):\n- Thin bar (4pt height) showing section completion percentage\n- \"{n}%\" text right-aligned above bar\n\n**Section navigation chips** (horizontal scroll):\n- Numbered pills (1, 2, 3... n) for each section\n- Green background + checkmark for viewed sections\n- Primary background for current section\n- Muted background for unviewed\n\n**Current section content** (scrollable):\n- Section counter: \"Section 2 of 8\" in 13pt muted\n- Section heading in 20pt semibold\n- Section content in 15pt body, leading-relaxed, multi-line\n- Subsections: Indented with left border (2pt muted line), sub-heading 15pt semibold, sub-content 15pt body\n\n**Bottom action bar** (fixed):\n- Left: \"Previous\" button (disabled on first section)\n- Center: \"Mark as Read\" button (primary) or \"Completed\" green badge if already viewed\n- Right: \"Next\" button (disabled on last section)\n\n**All sections read CTA** (appears below content when all sections viewed):\n- Green bordered card with checkmark icon\n- \"All sections read!\" text\n- \"Take Test\" button (primary, navigates to test screen)\n\n**Data sources**:\n- `GET /api/staff/training/guide-content/{guideCode}?lang={locale}` -- full guide content (sections, subsections, key points)\n- `POST /api/staff/training/records` -- record section view action\n- Existing `useCourseProgress` and `useGuideContent` hook logic\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Tap section chip: Jumps to that section\n- Tap \"Mark as Read\": Records section view, updates progress\n- Tap \"Previous\"/\"Next\": Navigates between sections\n- Tap \"Take Test\": Navigates to `/(tabs)/(more)/training/test/[guideCode]`\n- Scroll: Reads content\n- Tap back: Returns to training list (progress persists)\n\n**Empty states**:\n- Guide content loading: Centered spinner\n- No content available: \"Content not available in your language\" + language fallback option\n\n**Error states**:\n- Failed to load content: Error card with retry\n- Failed to record progress: Silent retry, no user-facing error\n\n**Animations**:\n- 7.9 Training Test\n\n**Screen name**: Training Test\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(more)/training/test/[guideCode]`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- Full-screen stack push, no back gesture during test (confirmation required)\n- **Header**: \"Test: {guideCode}\" + question counter \"3/10\"\n\n**Question card** (one at a time):\n- Question text in 17pt semibold\n- Answer options: List of buttons (full width, 48pt height, outline variant)\n  - Tapping selects answer (primary border + fill)\n  - Only one answer selectable per question\n\n**Navigation** (bottom):\n- \"Previous\" (left) + \"Next\" or \"Submit\" (right, on last question)\n- Progress dots or bar showing question position\n\n**Results screen** (after submission):\n- Score circle: Large percentage display (e.g., \"85%\") in 48pt bold\n  - Green if >= passing score (from `training_materials.passing_score`)\n  - Red if < passing score\n- \"Passed!\" or \"Not Passed\" text\n- Summary: \"{correct}/{total} correct answers\"\n- If passed: \"Download Certificate\" button (outline) + \"Done\" button (primary)\n- If failed: \"You need {passing_score}% to pass. Review the material and try again.\" + \"Review Material\" button + \"Done\" button\n\n**Data sources**:\n- `GET /api/staff/training/tests/{guideCode}?lang={locale}` -- test questions with options\n- `POST /api/staff/training/tests/{guideCode}/submit` -- submit answers (body: `{ answers: Record<questionId, selectedIndex> }`)\n- `GET /api/staff/training/certificate/{guideCode}` -- download certificate PDF\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Tap answer option: Selects answer\n- Tap \"Next\": Moves to next question\n- Tap \"Previous\": Moves to previous question\n- Tap \"Submit\": Submits all answers, shows results\n- Tap \"Download Certificate\": Opens PDF in system viewer\n- Tap \"Done\": Returns to training list\n- Tap back (during test): \"Are you sure? Your progress will be lost.\" alert\n\n**Empty states**: N/A (always has questions)\n\n**Error states**:\n- No questions loaded: \"Test not available in your language\"\n- Submission failed: \"Could not submit test. Tap to retry.\" with retry button\n\n**Animations**:\n- Question transition: Horizontal slide (200ms)\n- Score reveal: Count-up animation from 0% to final score (800ms)\n- Pass/fail: Confetti particles for pass (subtle, 2 seconds) / shake animation for fail (300ms)\n\n---\n\n### 7.10 Settings\n\n**Screen name**: Settings\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(more)/settings`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- Stack push\n- **Header**: Back arrow + \"Settings\"\n\n**Settings groups** (iOS Settings style grouped list):\n\n**Group: \"Appearance\"**:\n- **Language**: Current language flag + name. Tap opens picker with 4 options (EN, NL, ES, DE). Changing language updates `profile.language` via API and reloads app locale.\n- **Dark Mode**: Three-way selector: \"Light\" | \"Dark\" | \"System\". Updates `profile.theme` and applies immediately.\n\n**Group: \"Notifications\"**:\n- **Push Notifications**: Toggle. Controls OS-level notification permission. If toggling ON and not yet granted, requests permission.\n- **Notification Preferences**: Right chevron. Navigates to `/(tabs)/(more)/settings/notifications`.\n\n**Group: \"About\"**:\n- **App Version**: Read-only, shows \"1.0.0 (build 1)\"\n- **Terms of Service**: Opens `/legal/terms` in in-app browser\n- **Privacy Policy**: Opens `/legal/privacy` in in-app browser\n\n**Data sources**:\n- Profile data from auth context (language, theme)\n- `PATCH /api/settings/profile` -- update language/theme\n- OS notification permission status via `expo-notifications`\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Tap language row: Opens picker\n- Tap dark mode option: Changes theme immediately\n- Toggle push notifications: Requests/revokes permission\n- Tap notification preferences: Navigates to detail screen\n- Tap terms/privacy: Opens in-app browser\n\n**Empty states**: N/A\n\n**Error states**:\n- Language update failed: \"Could not save preference\" toast\n- Permission request denied: \"Open Settings to enable notifications\" with \"Open Settings\" button\n\n**Animations**:\n- Theme change: Instant (no animation, full re-render)\n- Language change: Brief fade-out/fade-in of text content (200ms)\n\n---\n\n### 7.11 Notification Preferences\n\n**Screen name**: Notification Preferences\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(more)/settings/notifications`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- Stack push\n- **Header**: Back arrow + \"Notification Preferences\"\n\n**Table** (matches web `NotificationsSettingsPage`):\n- 10 notification types, each row:\n  - Left: Type name (15pt) + description (13pt muted, max 2 lines)\n  - Right: Two toggle switches labeled \"In-App\" and \"Push\" (replacing web \"Email\" with \"Push\" for mobile)\n- Types (from `NOTIFICATION_TYPES` constant):\n  1. Shift Reminder\n  2. Schedule Change\n  3. Leave Approved\n  4. Leave Rejected\n  5. Task Assigned\n  6. Training Due\n  7. Stock Alert (visible to bar/kitchen roles only)\n  8. New Reservation (visible to waiter role only)\n  9. Reservation Cancelled (visible to waiter role only)\n  10. Birthday Alert\n\n- Each toggle immediately saves on change (optimistic update with API call)\n- Saving indicator: Brief spinner replaces toggle during save (200ms)\n\n**Data sources**:\n- `GET /api/settings/notifications` -- current preferences\n- `PATCH /api/settings/notifications` -- update individual preference (body: `{ type, channel, enabled }`)\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Toggle switch: Immediately saves preference\n- Pull-to-refresh: Reloads preferences\n\n**Empty states**: N/A (always shows all types)\n\n**Error states**:\n- Save failed: Toggle reverts to previous state + \"Could not save\" toast\n\n**Animations**:\n- Toggle: Native switch animation\n- Save feedback: Brief spinner overlay on toggle (200ms)\n\n---\n\n### 7.12 Info Guide (Business Reference)\n\n**Screen name**: Restaurant Info\n**Route**: `/(tabs)/(more)/info-guide`\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- Stack push\n- **Header**: Back arrow + \"Restaurant Info\"\n\n**This replaces the AI assistant** with a read-only reference guide. Content is hardcoded/bundled (no API calls).\n\n**Sections** (collapsible accordion):\n\n1. **Contact & Location**:\n   - Address: Carrer de Cartago 22, El Arenal, 07600 Mallorca\n   - Phone: Restaurant phone number\n   - Email: Contact email\n   - Map thumbnail: Static map image centered on 39.5021, 2.7392 (tappable, opens in native Maps app)\n\n2. **Opening Hours**:\n   - Table of daily opening hours\n   - Seasonal notes (e.g., \"Extended hours Jun-Sep\")\n\n3. **WiFi & Access**:\n   - Staff WiFi network name + password\n   - POS system login info\n   - Emergency exits location\n\n4. **Emergency Procedures**:\n   - Fire evacuation route description\n   - First aid kit locations\n   - Emergency phone numbers (112, fire, police, ambulance)\n   - Manager on-duty contact protocol\n\n5. **House Rules**:\n   - Dress code\n   - Phone policy during shifts\n   - Break room location and rules\n   - Lost & found procedure\n\n6. **Menu Quick Reference**:\n   - Link to digital menu: Opens `/digital` in in-app browser\n   - Allergen information summary\n   - Most common customer questions + answers\n\n7. **Social Media**:\n   - Instagram: @cheersmallorca\n   - Facebook page link\n\n**Each section**: Collapsible with tap. Header shows section name + expand/collapse chevron.\n\n**Data sources**: Bundled static content (no API). Localized strings from i18n bundles.\n\n**User interactions**:\n- Tap section header: Expand/collapse with animated height change\n- Tap map: Opens native maps app with restaurant coordinates\n- Tap phone numbers: Opens phone dialer\n- Tap email: Opens email composer\n- Tap digital menu link: Opens in-app browser\n\n**Empty states**: N/A (static content)\n\n**Error states**: N/A (no network required)\n\n**Animations**:\n- Accordion expand/collapse: Height animation with spring (250ms)\n- Section content: Fade-in on expand (150ms)\n\n---\n\n## 8. Push Notification Routing\n\nWhen a user taps a push notification, the app should deep-link to the appropriate screen. The routing is determined by the `type` field on the notification and its `action_url`.\n\n| Notification Type | Target Screen | Route |\n|---|---|---|\n| `shift_reminder` | Schedule tab, today highlighted | `/(tabs)/(schedule)/index` |\n| `schedule_published` | Schedule tab | `/(tabs)/(schedule)/index` |\n| `shift_assigned` | Shift detail for the assigned shift | `/(tabs)/(schedule)/[shiftId]` (shiftId from `data.shift_id`) |\n| `shift_changed` | Shift detail for the changed shift | `/(tabs)/(schedule)/[shiftId]` |\n| `swap_requested` | Schedule tab (future: swap request detail) | `/(tabs)/(schedule)/index` |\n| `swap_approved` | Schedule tab | `/(tabs)/(schedule)/index` |\n| `swap_rejected` | Schedule tab | `/(tabs)/(schedule)/index` |\n| `leave_approved` | Leave requests list | `/(tabs)/(more)/leave-requests` |\n| `leave_rejected` | Leave requests list | `/(tabs)/(more)/leave-requests` |\n| `task_assigned` | Schedule tab, tasks segment | `/(tabs)/(schedule)/index` (with tasks segment auto-selected) |\n| `training_due` | Training list | `/(tabs)/(more)/training/index` |\n| `stock_alert` | Home (informational only) | `/(tabs)/(home)/index` |\n| `reservation_new` | Home (informational only) | `/(tabs)/(home)/index` |\n| `reservation_cancelled` | Home (informational only) | `/(tabs)/(home)/index` |\n| `clock_reminder` | Clock tab | `/(tabs)/(clock)/index` |\n| `system` | Chat announcements tab | `/(tabs)/(chat)/index` |\n| Unknown / no `action_url` | Home | `/(tabs)/(home)/index` |\n\n**Implementation notes**:\n- Use `expo-notifications` `addNotificationResponseReceivedListener` to handle taps\n- Parse `notification.request.content.data` for `type` and routing params\n- If app is cold-started from notification, use `Notifications.getLastNotificationResponseAsync()` on mount\n- When app is in foreground, display an in-app banner (not a system notification) for 4 seconds with tap-to-navigate behavior\n- Notification data object structure: `{ type: string, action_url: string | null, shift_id?: string, ... }`\n\n---\n\n## 9. Global Components\n\n### 9.1 Bottom Tab Bar\n\n**Wireframe description**:\n- 5 tabs, standard platform height (49pt iOS, 56pt Android + safe area)\n- Each tab: Icon (24pt) + label (10pt) below\n- Active tab: `primary` color icon + label\n- Inactive tab: `muted-foreground` icon + label\n- Clock tab (center): Slightly larger icon (28pt), no special styling\n\n| Position | Icon | Label | Badge |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| 1 | Home icon | Home | None |\n| 2 | Calendar icon | Schedule | None |\n| 3 | Clock icon | Clock | Green dot when clocked in |\n| 4 | MessageSquare icon | Chat | Red badge with unread count |\n| 5 | MoreHorizontal icon | More | Red dot if training overdue |\n\n**Clock tab green dot**: 8pt circle, positioned at top-right of clock icon, `success` color. Visible when user has an active clock record (no `clock_out_time`). Determined by cached clock status from initial fetch.\n\n**Chat tab badge**: Standard red notification badge with unread count number. Uses `unreadCount` from notification hook.\n\n**More tab dot**: Small 6pt red dot when there are overdue training items. No number.\n\n### 9.2 Offline Banner\n\n- Full-width bar at top of screen (below status bar, above header)\n- Amber background, 36pt height\n- Wi-Fi-off icon (16pt) + \"No connection -- showing cached data\" text (13pt)\n- Sticky: Stays visible across all tabs until connectivity returns\n- Uses `NetInfo` from `@react-native-community/netinfo`\n- On reconnection: Banner slides up and dismisses (200ms), stale data sections auto-refresh\n\n### 9.3 Toast Notifications\n\n- In-app toast for action feedback (success, error, info)\n- Appears 64pt below top safe area, centered horizontally\n- Rounded-lg, shadow, 48pt height, auto-dismiss after 3 seconds\n- Green left border for success, red for error, amber for warning\n- Icon (16pt) + message text (13pt)\n- Swipe up to dismiss early\n\n---\n\n## Appendix: API Endpoint Summary\n\nThe mobile app consumes the following existing API routes (all require authentication via Supabase session token in `Authorization: Bearer {token}` header):\n\n**Auth**:\n- `POST /auth/login` (Supabase `signInWithPassword`)\n- `POST /auth/logout` (Supabase `signOut`)\n\n**Staff/Clock**:\n- `GET /api/staff/clock?employee_id={id}` -- clock records\n- `POST /api/staff/clock?action=in` -- clock in (body: `{ latitude?, longitude? }`)\n- `POST /api/staff/clock?action=out` -- clock out (body: `{ clock_record_id }`)\n- `POST /api/staff/clock/break` -- start/end break (body: `{ clock_record_id, action }`)\n\n**Staff/Shifts**:\n- `GET /api/staff/shifts?employee_id={id}&start_date=X&end_date=Y` -- employee shifts\n\n**Staff/Swap**:\n- `GET /api/staff/swap-requests` -- list swap requests\n- `POST /api/staff/swap-requests` -- create swap request\n- `PATCH /api/staff/swap-requests?id={id}` -- accept/reject swap\n\n**Staff/Availability**:\n- `GET /api/staff/availability?employee_id={id}` -- availability records\n- `POST /api/staff/availability` -- set availability\n\n**Staff/Leave**:\n- `GET /api/staff/leave?employee_id={id}` -- leave requests\n- `POST /api/staff/leave` -- create leave request\n\n**Staff/Tasks**:\n- `GET /api/staff/tasks?assigned_to={id}` -- tasks\n- `GET /api/staff/task-plans?week={date}` -- weekly task plans\n\n**Staff/Documents**:\n- `GET /api/staff/documents?employee_id={id}` -- employee documents\n\n**Staff/Training**:\n- `GET /api/staff/training/guide-content/{guideCode}?lang={locale}` -- guide content\n- `GET /api/staff/training/tests/{guideCode}?lang={locale}` -- test questions\n- `POST /api/staff/training/tests/{guideCode}/submit` -- submit test\n- `GET /api/staff/training/records/{employeeId}` -- training records\n- `POST /api/staff/training/records` -- record training action\n- `GET /api/staff/training/compliance` -- compliance stats\n- `GET /api/staff/training/certificate/{guideCode}` -- certificate PDF\n\n**Staff/Surveys**:\n- `POST /api/staff/surveys` -- submit post-shift survey\n\n**Staff/Employees**:\n- `GET /api/staff/employees?profile_id={userId}` -- get employee record\n\n**Notifications**:\n- `GET /api/notifications` -- list notifications\n- `PATCH /api/notifications` -- mark as read\n- `DELETE /api/notifications` -- delete notifications\n- `POST /api/notifications/subscribe` -- register push token\n\n**Settings**:\n- `GET /api/settings/notifications` -- notification preferences\n- `PATCH /api/settings/notifications` -- update notification preference\n- `PATCH /api/settings/profile` -- update profile\n\n---\n\n## Appendix: Role-Based Visibility\n\nThe 4 employee roles see slightly different content:\n\n| Feature | Waiter | Bar | Kitchen | DJ |\n|---|---|---|---|---|\n| All Home sections | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |\n| Schedule (shifts + tasks) | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |\n| Clock in/out | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |\n| Announcements | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |\n| Leave requests | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |\n| Documents | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |\n| Training guides | Role-filtered | Role-filtered | Role-filtered | Role-filtered |\n| Notification: stock_alert | No | Yes | Yes | No |\n| Notification: reservation_new | Yes | No | No | No |\n| Notification: reservation_cancelled | Yes | No | No | No |\n| Notification pref: stock_alert row | Hidden | Visible | Visible | Hidden |\n| Notification pref: reservation rows | Visible | Hidden | Hidden | Hidden |\n\nThe guide list is filtered by `applicableRoles` from the `GUIDES` constant. Guides with empty `applicableRoles` array are shown to all roles. Guides with specific roles (e.g., `['kitchen', 'bar']`) are only shown to those roles.\n\n---\n\n**End of document.**

# PART 3: INFRASTRUCTURE (Push Notifications, i18n, Theming)

# GrandCafe Cheers -- React Native Employee App: Cross-Cutting Infrastructure Specification\n\n## Document Metadata\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| Version | 1.0 |\n| Based on web app commit | `0e4953e` (main) |\n| Target runtime | Expo SDK 53 (managed workflow) |\n| Backend | Supabase (PostgreSQL 17, existing instance) |\n| Users | 20-30 staff, 7 roles, 4 languages |\n| Timezone | Europe/Madrid |\n\n---\n\n## 1. Push Notification System\n\n### 1.1 Architecture Overview\n\nThe mobile app replaces the web app's Web Push (VAPID) mechanism with Expo Push Notifications. The web app already has a `notifications` table, a `push_subscriptions` table, a `notification_preferences` table, and DB triggers for shift/swap events (migration `003_notifications.sql` and `20260307180001_notification_preferences.sql`). The mobile system extends this infrastructure rather than replacing it.\n\n**Flow:**\n\n```\nDB Event (trigger/Edge Function)\n  -> Insert into `notifications` table\n  -> Supabase Edge Function reads `push_tokens` for user\n  -> Edge Function calls Expo Push API (https://exp.host/--/api/v2/push/send)\n  -> Expo routes to APNs / FCM\n  -> Device receives push\n  -> Tap opens deep link in app\n```\n\n### 1.2 Database Schema\n\n#### New table: `push_tokens`\n\nThis table is separate from the existing `push_subscriptions` (which stores Web Push VAPID endpoints). Native apps use Expo push tokens, which have a different shape.\n\n```sql\n-- Migration: XXX_push_tokens.sql\n\nCREATE TABLE push_tokens (\n  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n  user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES profiles(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n  expo_push_token TEXT NOT NULL,\n  device_id TEXT NOT NULL,             -- Expo Constants.installationId or Application.androidId / iOS identifierForVendor\n  platform TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (platform IN ('ios', 'android')),\n  app_version TEXT,                    -- e.g. '1.0.0'\n  locale TEXT DEFAULT 'nl',            -- user's device locale at registration time\n  active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,\n  last_used_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),\n  created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),\n  updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),\n  UNIQUE(user_id, device_id)\n);\n\nCREATE INDEX idx_push_tokens_user_id ON push_tokens(user_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_push_tokens_active ON push_tokens(active) WHERE active = true;\nCREATE INDEX idx_push_tokens_expo_token ON push_tokens(expo_push_token);\n\nALTER TABLE push_tokens ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;\n\n-- Users can read/manage their own tokens\nCREATE POLICY \"Users read own push tokens\"\n  ON push_tokens FOR SELECT USING (user_id = auth.uid());\nCREATE POLICY \"Users insert own push tokens\"\n  ON push_tokens FOR INSERT WITH CHECK (user_id = auth.uid());\nCREATE POLICY \"Users update own push tokens\"\n  ON push_tokens FOR UPDATE USING (user_id = auth.uid());\nCREATE POLICY \"Users delete own push tokens\"\n  ON push_tokens FOR DELETE USING (user_id = auth.uid());\n\n-- Auto-update updated_at\nCREATE TRIGGER push_tokens_updated_at\n  BEFORE UPDATE ON push_tokens\n  FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_push_subscriptions_updated_at();\n```\n\n#### Extend existing `notification_preferences` table\n\nThe existing table (`user_id`, `type`, `channel`, `enabled`) already supports per-type, per-channel preferences. Add the `push` channel alongside existing `in_app` and `email`. Add a `quiet_hours` table:\n\n```sql\n-- Migration: XXX_notification_quiet_hours.sql\n\nCREATE TABLE notification_quiet_hours (\n  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n  user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES profiles(id) ON DELETE CASCADE UNIQUE,\n  enabled BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,\n  start_time TIME NOT NULL DEFAULT '22:00',\n  end_time TIME NOT NULL DEFAULT '07:00',\n  timezone TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'Europe/Madrid',\n  created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),\n  updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()\n);\n\nALTER TABLE notification_quiet_hours ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;\n\nCREATE POLICY \"Users manage own quiet hours\"\n  ON notification_quiet_hours FOR ALL USING (user_id = auth.uid());\n```\n\n### 1.3 Notification Type Catalog (10 Types)\n\nEach notification type is defined with: title templates (4 languages), body template, deep link, priority, sound, and badge behavior.\n\n**Priority levels:**\n- `high` -- interrupts quiet hours, critical notification sound\n- `default` -- standard delivery, respects quiet hours\n- `low` -- silent delivery, badge increment only\n\n---\n\n#### Type 1: `shift_reminder`\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| Trigger | Cron Edge Function, 2 hours before shift start |\n| Priority | `high` |\n| Sound | `default` |\n| Badge | increment |\n| Deep link | `cheers://schedule/today` |\n\n**Title templates:**\n\n| Lang | Template |\n|------|----------|\n| NL | `Dienst herinnering` |\n| EN | `Shift reminder` |\n| ES | `Recordatorio de turno` |\n| DE | `Schicht-Erinnerung` |\n\n**Body templates:**\n\n| Lang | Template |\n|------|----------|\n| NL | `Je {{shift_type}} dienst begint om {{start_time}}` |\n| EN | `Your {{shift_type}} shift starts at {{start_time}}` |\n| ES | `Tu turno de {{shift_type}} comienza a las {{start_time}}` |\n| DE | `Deine {{shift_type}}-Schicht beginnt um {{start_time}}` |\n\n---\n\n#### Type 2: `schedule_published`\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| Trigger | DB trigger on `schedule_plans` status change to `published` |\n| Priority | `default` |\n| Sound | `default` |\n| Badge | increment |\n| Deep link | `cheers://schedule/week/{{week_start}}` |\n\n**Title templates:**\n\n| Lang | Template |\n|------|----------|\n| NL | `Nieuw rooster gepubliceerd` |\n| EN | `New schedule published` |\n| ES | `Nuevo horario publicado` |\n| DE | `Neuer Dienstplan veröffentlicht` |\n\n**Body templates:**\n\n| Lang | Template |\n|------|----------|\n| NL | `Het rooster voor week {{week_label}} is beschikbaar` |\n| EN | `The schedule for week {{week_label}} is now available` |\n| ES | `El horario de la semana {{week_label}} ya está disponible` |\n| DE | `Der Dienstplan für Woche {{week_label}} ist jetzt verfügbar` |\n\n---\n\n#### Type 3: `shift_change`\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| Trigger | DB trigger on `shifts` UPDATE where employee_id matches |\n| Priority | `high` |\n| Sound | `attention.wav` (custom) |\n| Badge | increment |\n| Deep link | `cheers://schedule/shift/{{shift_id}}` |\n\n**Title templates:**\n\n| Lang | Template |\n|------|----------|\n| NL | `Dienst gewijzigd` |\n| EN | `Shift changed` |\n| ES | `Turno modificado` |\n| DE | `Schicht geändert` |\n\n**Body templates:**\n\n| Lang | Template |\n|------|----------|\n| NL | `Je dienst op {{date}} is gewijzigd naar {{shift_type}} ({{start_time}}-{{end_time}})` |\n| EN | `Your shift on {{date}} has been changed to {{shift_type}} ({{start_time}}-{{end_time}})` |\n| ES | `Tu turno del {{date}} ha sido cambiado a {{shift_type}} ({{start_time}}-{{end_time}})` |\n| DE | `Deine Schicht am {{date}} wurde geändert zu {{shift_type}} ({{start_time}}-{{end_time}})` |\n\n---\n\n#### Type 4: `swap_request_received`\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| Trigger | DB trigger on `shift_swap_requests` INSERT |\n| Priority | `default` |\n| Sound | `default` |\n| Badge | increment |\n| Deep link | `cheers://schedule/swaps` |\n\n**Title templates:**\n\n| Lang | Template |\n|------|----------|\n| NL | `Dienstwissel verzoek` |\n| EN | `Shift swap request` |\n| ES | `Solicitud de cambio de turno` |\n| DE | `Schichttausch-Anfrage` |\n\n**Body templates:**\n\n| Lang | Template |\n|------|----------|\n| NL | `{{requester_name}} wil je {{shift_type}} dienst op {{date}} overnemen` |\n| EN | `{{requester_name}} wants to swap your {{shift_type}} shift on {{date}}` |\n| ES | `{{requester_name}} quiere intercambiar tu turno de {{shift_type}} del {{date}}` |\n| DE | `{{requester_name}} möchte deine {{shift_type}}-Schicht am {{date}} tauschen` |\n\n---\n\n#### Type 5: `swap_request_resolved`\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| Trigger | DB trigger on `shift_swap_requests` UPDATE where status changes |\n| Priority | `default` |\n| Sound | `default` |\n| Badge | increment |\n| Deep link | `cheers://schedule/swaps` |\n\n**Title templates (approved):**\n\n| Lang | Template |\n|------|----------|\n| NL | `Dienstwissel goedgekeurd` |\n| EN | `Shift swap approved` |\n| ES | `Cambio de turno aprobado` |\n| DE | `Schichttausch genehmigt` |\n\n**Title templates (rejected):**\n\n| Lang | Template |\n|------|----------|\n| NL | `Dienstwissel afgewezen` |\n| EN | `Shift swap rejected` |\n| ES | `Cambio de turno rechazado` |\n| DE | `Schichttausch abgelehnt` |\n\n**Body templates (approved):**\n\n| Lang | Template |\n|------|----------|\n| NL | `Je dienstwissel voor {{shift_type}} op {{date}} is goedgekeurd` |\n| EN | `Your swap request for {{shift_type}} on {{date}} has been approved` |\n| ES | `Tu solicitud de cambio de {{shift_type}} del {{date}} ha sido aprobada` |\n| DE | `Dein Tauschantrag für {{shift_type}} am {{date}} wurde genehmigt` |\n\n**Body templates (rejected):**\n\n| Lang | Template |\n|------|----------|\n| NL | `Je dienstwissel voor {{shift_type}} op {{date}} is afgewezen` |\n| EN | `Your swap request for {{shift_type}} on {{date}} has been rejected` |\n| ES | `Tu solicitud de cambio de {{shift_type}} del {{date}} ha sido rechazada` |\n| DE | `Dein Tauschantrag für {{shift_type}} am {{date}} wurde abgelehnt` |\n\n---\n\n#### Type 6: `leave_resolved`\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| Trigger | DB trigger on `leave_requests` UPDATE where status changes |\n| Priority | `default` |\n| Sound | `default` |\n| Badge | increment |\n| Deep link | `cheers://schedule/leave` |\n\n**Title templates (approved):**\n\n| Lang | Template |\n|------|----------|\n| NL | `Verlof goedgekeurd` |\n| EN | `Leave approved` |\n| ES | `Permiso aprobado` |\n| DE | `Urlaub genehmigt` |\n\n**Title templates (rejected):**\n\n| Lang | Template |\n|------|----------|\n| NL | `Verlof afgewezen` |\n| EN | `Leave
