`Clock-in missed` |\n| ES | `Fichaje perdido` |\n| DE | `Einstempeln verpasst` |\n\n**Body templates:**\n\n| Lang | Template |\n|------|----------|\n| NL | `Je {{shift_type}} dienst begon om {{start_time}}. Klok alsjeblieft in.` |\n| EN | `Your {{shift_type}} shift started at {{start_time}}. Please clock in.` |\n| ES | `Tu turno de {{shift_type}} comenzó a las {{start_time}}. Por favor, ficha.` |\n| DE | `Deine {{shift_type}}-Schicht begann um {{start_time}}. Bitte stempel ein.` |\n\n---\n\n#### Type 10: `document_uploaded`\n\n| Field | Value |\n|-------|-------|\n| Trigger | Edge Function called when admin uploads a document (contract, payslip, etc.) to an employee |\n| Priority | `low` |\n| Sound | none (silent) |\n| Badge | increment |\n| Deep link | `cheers://profile/documents` |\n\n**Title templates:**\n\n| Lang | Template |\n|------|----------|\n| NL | `Nieuw document beschikbaar` |\n| EN | `New document available` |\n| ES | `Nuevo documento disponible` |\n| DE | `Neues Dokument verfügbar` |\n\n**Body templates:**\n\n| Lang | Template |\n|------|----------|\n| NL | `{{document_type}} is geüpload naar je profiel` |\n| EN | `{{document_type}} has been uploaded to your profile` |\n| ES | `{{document_type}} ha sido subido a tu perfil` |\n| DE | `{{document_type}} wurde in dein Profil hochgeladen` |\n\n---\n\n### 1.4 Edge Function Patterns\n\n#### 1.4.1 Generic Push Sender\n\nFile: `supabase/functions/send-push-notification/index.ts`\n\nThis is the core Edge Function that all notification triggers call. It handles:\n- Looking up active push tokens for the target user\n- Resolving the user's preferred language from `profiles.language`\n- Checking quiet hours (if priority is not `high`)\n- Rendering title/body templates with variable interpolation\n- Calling the Expo Push API in batches (max 100 per request)\n- Handling ticket receipts and marking invalid tokens as `active = false`\n\n**Key logic (pseudocode):**\n\n```\nfunction handleNotification(userId, notificationType, templateVars, options):\n  1. Fetch user profile (language, id)\n  2. Fetch active push_tokens for user\n  3. If no tokens, return early (still insert into notifications table for in-app)\n  4. Check notification_preferences: is 'push' channel enabled for this type?\n     - If not enabled, return early\n  5. If priority != 'high':\n     - Fetch quiet_hours for user\n     - If current time (in user's timezone) is within quiet hours, defer:\n       queue for delivery at end of quiet period\n  6. Resolve title and body from NOTIFICATION_TEMPLATES[type][language]\n  7. Interpolate templateVars into title and body\n  8. Build Expo push messages:\n     {\n       to: token.expo_push_token,\n       title: resolvedTitle,\n       body: resolvedBody,\n       data: { type: notificationType, deepLink: options.deepLink, ...templateVars },\n       sound: options.sound || 'default',\n       priority: options.priority || 'default',\n       badge: options.badge  // managed via increment counter\n     }\n  9. POST to https://exp.host/--/api/v2/push/send (batch)\n  10. Process tickets: on DeviceNotRegistered errors, set token.active = false\n  11. Update push_tokens.last_used_at for successfully sent tokens\n```\n\n#### 1.4.2 DB Webhook Pattern (for trigger-based notifications)\n\nSupabase Database Webhooks call Edge Functions on INSERT/UPDATE. The existing `003_notifications.sql` already creates in-app notifications via triggers. The mobile system adds an Edge Function webhook that listens to the `notifications` table itself:\n\n**Pattern: Notifications table webhook**\n\n```\nTrigger: AFTER INSERT on notifications\n  -> Call Edge Function send-push-notification\n  -> Edge Function reads the new notification row\n  -> Resolves push tokens for the user_id\n  -> Sends push via Expo Push API\n```\n\nThis is the simplest pattern: the existing triggers already insert into `notifications`, so the push delivery is a separate concern that reads from the same table. This avoids duplicating trigger logic.\n\n#### 1.4.3 Cron-based Notifications\n\nFor `shift_reminder` and `clock_in_missed`, use Supabase `pg_cron` extension:\n\n```sql\n-- Run every 5 minutes, find shifts starting in 115-125 minutes\n-- (2 hours ahead, with 10-minute window to avoid missed runs)\nSELECT cron.schedule(\n  'shift-reminders',\n  '*/5 * * * *',\n  $$\n    SELECT net.http_post(\n      url := 'https://<project-ref>.supabase.co/functions/v1/shift-reminders',\n      headers := jsonb_build_object(\n        'Authorization', 'Bearer ' || current_setting('app.service_role_key'),\n        'Content-Type', 'application/json'\n      ),\n      body := '{}'::jsonb\n    );\n  $$\n);\n\n-- Run every 5 minutes, find shifts that started 10-15 minutes ago with no clock_in\nSELECT cron.schedule(\n  'clock-in-missed',\n  '*/5 * * * *',\n  $$\n    SELECT net.http_post(\n      url := 'https://<project-ref>.supabase.co/functions/v1/clock-in-missed',\n      headers := jsonb_build_object(\n        'Authorization', 'Bearer ' || current_setting('app.service_role_key'),\n        'Content-Type', 'application/json'\n      ),\n      body := '{}'::jsonb\n    );\n  $$\n);\n```\n\nThe Edge Functions query shifts joining clock_in_records to determine which users need reminders, then call the generic push sender.\n\n### 1.5 Client-Side Implementation\n\n#### Token Registration\n\nFile: `src/services/push-notifications.ts`\n\n```typescript\nimport * as Notifications from 'expo-notifications';\nimport * as Device from 'expo-device';\nimport { Platform } from 'react-native';\nimport { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase';\n\n// Configuration\nNotifications.setNotificationHandler({\n  handleNotification: async () => ({\n    shouldShowAlert: true,\n    shouldPlaySound: true,\n    shouldSetBadge: true,\n    priority: Notifications.AndroidNotificationPriority.HIGH,\n  }),\n});\n\nexport async function registerForPushNotifications(userId: string): Promise<string | null> {\n  if (!Device.isDevice) {\n    console.warn('Push notifications require a physical device');\n    return null;\n  }\n\n  const { status: existingStatus } = await Notifications.getPermissionsAsync();\n  let finalStatus = existingStatus;\n\n  if (existingStatus !== 'granted') {\n    const { status } = await Notifications.requestPermissionsAsync();\n    finalStatus = status;\n  }\n\n  if (finalStatus !== 'granted') {\n    return null;\n  }\n\n  // Android notification channel\n  if (Platform.OS === 'android') {\n    await Notifications.setNotificationChannelAsync('shift-alerts', {\n      name: 'Shift Alerts',\n      importance: Notifications.AndroidImportance.HIGH,\n      vibrationPattern: [0, 250, 250, 250],\n      lightColor: '#FF6B35', // cheers primary\n      sound: 'default',\n    });\n\n    await Notifications.setNotificationChannelAsync('general', {\n      name: 'General',\n      importance: Notifications.AndroidImportance.DEFAULT,\n      sound: 'default',\n    });\n\n    await Notifications.setNotificationChannelAsync('silent', {\n      name: 'Silent Updates',\n      importance: Notifications.AndroidImportance.LOW,\n      sound: null,\n    });\n  }\n\n  const tokenResponse = await Notifications.getExpoPushTokenAsync({\n    projectId: process.env.EXPO_PUBLIC_PROJECT_ID,\n  });\n\n  const expoPushToken = tokenResponse.data;\n\n  // Upsert token to database\n  const { error } = await supabase\n    .from('push_tokens')\n    .upsert(\n      {\n        user_id: userId,\n        expo_push_token: expoPushToken,\n        device_id: Device.modelId ?? 'unknown',\n        platform: Platform.OS,\n        app_version: '1.0.0',\n        active: true,\n        last_used_at: new Date().toISOString(),\n      },\n      { onConflict: 'user_id,device_id' }\n    );\n\n  if (error) {\n    console.error('Failed to register push token:', error);\n  }\n\n  return expoPushToken;\n}\n```\n\n#### Deep Link Handling\n\nFile: `src/services/deep-links.ts`\n\nMap notification `data.deepLink` to Expo Router paths:\n\n```typescript\nconst DEEP_LINK_MAP: Record<string, string> = {\n  'cheers://schedule/today': '/(tabs)/schedule',\n  'cheers://schedule/swaps': '/(tabs)/schedule/swaps',\n  'cheers://schedule/leave': '/(tabs)/schedule/leave',\n  'cheers://clock': '/(tabs)/clock',\n  'cheers://chat/announcements': '/(tabs)/chat',\n  'cheers://profile/documents': '/(tabs)/profile/documents',\n};\n\n// For parameterized links: cheers://schedule/week/2026-03-16\n// Parse prefix and extract params\nexport function resolveDeepLink(deepLink: string): string {\n  if (DEEP_LINK_MAP[deepLink]) {\n    return DEEP_LINK_MAP[deepLink];\n  }\n\n  // Pattern matching for parameterized routes\n  if (deepLink.startsWith('cheers://schedule/shift/')) {\n    const shiftId = deepLink.replace('cheers://schedule/shift/', '');\n    return `/(tabs)/schedule/shift/${shiftId}`;\n  }\n\n  if (deepLink.startsWith('cheers://tasks/')) {\n    const taskId = deepLink.replace('cheers://tasks/', '');\n    return `/(tabs)/tasks/${taskId}`;\n  }\n\n  if (deepLink.startsWith('cheers://schedule/week/')) {\n    const weekStart = deepLink.replace('cheers://schedule/week/', '');\n    return `/(tabs)/schedule?week=${weekStart}`;\n  }\n\n  return '/(tabs)/home';\n}\n```\n\n### 1.6 GDPR Compliance\n\n#### Opt-in Flow\n\n1. **First launch after login:** Show a permission prompt screen (not a system dialog yet).\n   - Explain what notifications the app will send and why.\n   - Show toggle switches for each notification category.\n   - \"Enable Notifications\" button triggers the OS permission dialog.\n   - \"Skip\" button lets the user proceed without push (in-app notifications still work).\n\n2. **Granular preferences:** Available in Profile > Notification Settings.\n   - Per-type toggles (all 10 types) with `push` channel.\n   - Quiet hours toggle with configurable start/end times (default: 22:00-07:00 Europe/Madrid).\n   - Uses the existing `notification_preferences` table with `channel = 'push'`.\n\n#### Preference Storage\n\nThe existing `notification_preferences` table structure (`user_id`, `type`, `channel`, `enabled`) is sufficient. For the mobile app, insert default rows on first login:\n\n```typescript\nconst DEFAULT_PREFERENCES = [\n  { type: 'shift_reminder', channel: 'push', enabled: true },\n  { type: 'schedule_published', channel: 'push', enabled: true },\n  { type: 'shift_change', channel: 'push', enabled: true },\n  { type: 'swap_request_received', channel: 'push', enabled: true },\n  { type: 'swap_request_resolved', channel: 'push', enabled: true },\n  { type: 'leave_resolved', channel: 'push', enabled: true },\n  { type: 'new_announcement', channel: 'push', enabled: true },\n  { type: 'task_assigned', channel: 'push', enabled: true },\n  { type: 'clock_in_missed', channel: 'push', enabled: true },\n  { type: 'document_uploaded', channel: 'push', enabled: true },\n];\n```\n\n#### Quiet Hours\n\n- Default: 22:00-07:00 Europe/Madrid\n- `high` priority notifications (shift_reminder, shift_change, clock_in_missed) bypass quiet hours\n- `default` and `low` priority notifications are queued and delivered at `end_time`\n- The Edge Function checks quiet hours server-side, not on the client\n\n#### Token Cleanup on Employee Departure\n\nWhen `employees.employment_status` changes to `terminated`:\n\n```sql\n-- Add to existing employee termination trigger or create new one:\nCREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION cleanup_push_tokens_on_termination()\nRETURNS TRIGGER AS $$\nBEGIN\n  IF NEW.employment_status = 'terminated' AND OLD.employment_status != 'terminated' THEN\n    UPDATE push_tokens\n    SET active = false, updated_at = NOW()\n    WHERE user_id = (SELECT profile_id FROM employees WHERE id = NEW.id);\n\n    -- Also delete notification preferences (GDPR: right to erasure)\n    DELETE FROM notification_preferences\n    WHERE user_id = (SELECT profile_id FROM employees WHERE id = NEW.id)\n    AND channel = 'push';\n  END IF;\n  RETURN NEW;\nEND;\n$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql SECURITY DEFINER;\n\nCREATE TRIGGER cleanup_push_on_termination\n  AFTER UPDATE ON employees\n  FOR EACH ROW\n  WHEN (NEW.employment_status = 'terminated')\n  EXECUTE FUNCTION cleanup_push_tokens_on_termination();\n```\n\nAdditionally, run a weekly cron job to prune tokens not used in 90 days:\n\n```sql\nSELECT cron.schedule(\n  'prune-stale-push-tokens',\n  '0 3 * * 0', -- Sundays at 3:00 AM\n  $$\n    DELETE FROM push_tokens\n    WHERE last_used_at < NOW() - INTERVAL '90 days';\n  $$\n);\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. Internationalization (i18n)\n\n### 2.1 Setup Architecture\n\n**Libraries:**\n- `expo-localization` -- device language detection\n- `i18next` + `react-i18next` -- translation runtime\n- `intl-pluralrules` -- polyfill for Android Hermes (Intl.PluralRules)\n- `date-fns` with locale imports (`nl`, `es`, `de`, `enGB`) -- date formatting\n- `react-native-intl-number-format` or built-in `Intl.NumberFormat` -- currency\n\n**Language resolution priority:**\n1. User preference stored in `profiles.language` (synced from backend)\n2. Device locale via `expo-localization`\n3. Fallback: `nl` (Dutch is primary for this team)\n\n### 2.2 Initialization\n\nFile: `src/i18n/index.ts`\n\n```typescript\nimport i18n from 'i18next';\nimport { initReactI18next } from 'react-i18next';\nimport { getLocales } from 'expo-localization';\nimport 'intl-pluralrules';\n\n// Import all namespaces for all languages (bundled at build time)\nimport nlCommon from './messages/nl/common.json';\nimport nlHome from './messages/nl/home.json';\nimport nlSchedule from './messages/nl/schedule.json';\nimport nlClock from './messages/nl/clock.json';\nimport nlChat from './messages/nl/chat.json';\nimport nlProfile from './messages/nl/profile.json';\nimport nlNotifications from './messages/nl/notifications.json';\n// ... repeat for en, es, de\n\nconst resources = {\n  nl: { common: nlCommon, home: nlHome, schedule: nlSchedule, clock: nlClock, chat: nlChat, profile: nlProfile, notifications: nlNotifications },\n  en: { common: enCommon, home: enHome, schedule: enSchedule, clock: enClock, chat: enChat, profile: enProfile, notifications: enNotifications },\n  es: { common: esCommon, home: esHome, schedule: esSchedule, clock: esClock, chat: esChat, profile: esProfile, notifications: esNotifications },\n  de: { common: deCommon, home: deHome, schedule: deSchedule, clock: deClock, chat: deChat, profile: deProfile, notifications: deNotifications },\n};\n\nconst deviceLocale = getLocales()[0]?.languageCode ?? 'nl';\nconst supportedLocales = ['nl', 'en', 'es', 'de'];\nconst detectedLocale = supportedLocales.includes(deviceLocale) ? deviceLocale : 'nl';\n\ni18n.use(initReactI18next).init({\n  resources,\n  lng: detectedLocale,      // will be overridden by user profile preference\n  fallbackLng: 'nl',\n  defaultNS: 'common',\n  ns: ['common', 'home', 'schedule', 'clock', 'chat', 'profile', 'notifications'],\n  interpolation: {\n    escapeValue: false,      // React Native handles escaping\n  },\n  compatibilityJSON: 'v4',  // Required for Hermes pluralization\n});\n\nexport default i18n;\n\n// Helper to change language when user profile loads\nexport function setAppLanguage(lang: 'nl' | 'en' | 'es' | 'de'): void {\n  if (i18n.language !== lang) {\n    i18n.changeLanguage(lang);\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### 2.3 Namespace Structure\n\nThe mobile app uses 7 namespaces. These are a subset and restructuring of the web app's ~14 namespaces, focused on the mobile-relevant features:\n\n| Namespace | Mobile Screens | Web App Source Namespaces |\n|-----------|---------------|--------------------------|\n| `common` | Shared buttons, labels, errors, roles, status, time | `common` (buttons, roles, status, errors, time, table) |\n| `home` | Dashboard/home screen | `common` (nav, shell), new mobile-specific |\n| `schedule` | Calendar, shifts, swaps, leave | `staff` (schedule section), `settings` (schedule settings) |\n| `clock` | Time tracking, clock in/out | `staff` (clock section), new |\n| `chat` | Team messaging, announcements | `common` (chat), new |\n| `profile` | Settings, personal info, documents | `settings` (form, appearance), `auth` |\n| `notifications` | Push notification content, preferences | `settings` (notifications), `common` (notificationPermission) |\n\n### 2.4 Translation Files\n\nBelow is the complete translation structure for all 4 languages across all 7 namespaces.\n\n#### 2.4.1 `common` namespace\n\n**NL (`src/i18n/messages/nl/common.json`):**\n```json\n{\n  \"buttons\": {\n enGB } from 'date-fns/locale';\nimport i18n from './index';\n\nconst DATE_LOCALES = {\n  nl,\n  en: enGB,\n  es,\n  de,\n} as const;\n\nfunction getDateLocale() {\n  return DATE_LOCALES[i18n.language as keyof typeof DATE_LOCALES] ?? nl;\n}\n\nexport function formatDate(date: Date | string, pattern: string = 'PPP'): string {\n  const d = typeof date === 'string' ? new Date(date) : date;\n  return format(d, pattern, { locale: getDateLocale() });\n}\n\nexport function formatTime(date: Date | string, pattern: string = 'HH:mm'): string {\n  const d = typeof date === 'string' ? new Date(date) : date;\n  return format(d, pattern, { locale: getDateLocale() });\n}\n\nexport function formatRelativeDate(date: Date | string): string {\n  const d = typeof date === 'string' ? new Date(date) : date;\n  return formatRelative(d, new Date(), { locale: getDateLocale() });\n}\n\nexport function formatTimeAgo(date: Date | string): string {\n  const d = typeof date === 'string' ? new Date(date) : date;\n  return formatDistance(d, new Date(), { addSuffix: true, locale: getDateLocale() });\n}\n\n// Shift time display: \"10:00 - 17:00\"\nexport function formatShiftTime(start: string, end: string): string {\n  return `${start.slice(0, 5)} - ${end.slice(0, 5)}`;\n}\n```\n\n### 2.6 Currency Formatting\n\nFile: `src/i18n/number-utils.ts`\n\n```typescript\nimport i18n from './index';\n\nconst LOCALE_MAP: Record<string, string> = {\n  nl: 'nl-NL',\n  en: 'en-GB',\n  es: 'es-ES',\n  de: 'de-DE',\n};\n\nexport function formatCurrency(amount: number): string {\n  const locale = LOCALE_MAP[i18n.language] ?? 'nl-NL';\n  return new Intl.NumberFormat(locale, {\n    style: 'currency',\n    currency: 'EUR',\n    minimumFractionDigits: 2,\n  }).format(amount);\n}\n\nexport function formatNumber(value: number, decimals: number = 0): string {\n  const locale = LOCALE_MAP[i18n.language] ?? 'nl-NL';\n  return new Intl.NumberFormat(locale, {\n    minimumFractionDigits: decimals,\n    maximumFractionDigits: decimals,\n  }).format(value);\n}\n\nexport function formatHours(hours: number): string {\n  return formatNumber(hours, 1);\n}\n```\n\n### 2.7 Syncing with Web App Translation Keys\n\n**Strategy:** The mobile app does NOT share files directly with the web app, because:\n1. The web app uses `next-intl` (flat key access), the mobile uses `i18next` (namespace access).\n2. The mobile app has different screens and fewer namespaces.\n3. Some keys are identical (roles, status, buttons) and should be kept in sync manually.\n\n**Sync process:**\n1. Shared keys (roles, status, button labels, error messages) are copied from the web app's `src/i18n/messages/{locale}/common.json` and kept alphabetically sorted in both projects.\n2. A CI check script compares shared key subsets between web and mobile repos, flagging drift.\n3. New keys added to the web app that affect mobile functionality are tracked in a `TRANSLATION_SYNC.md` file.\n\n**File for CI sync script** (`scripts/check-i18n-sync.ts`):\n\n```typescript\n// Compares common.buttons, common.roles, common.status, common.errors\n// between web app and mobile app JSON files.\n// Outputs diff report. Run in CI to detect drift.\n\nconst SHARED_NAMESPACES = ['buttons', 'roles', 'status', 'errors'];\n// Compare key presence and value for all 4 locales\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Theming System\n\n### 3.1 NativeWind Setup\n\nThe mobile app uses NativeWind v4 (Tailwind CSS for React Native) to maintain parity with the web app's Tailwind-based design system.\n\nFile: `tailwind.config.ts`\n\n```typescript\nimport type { Config } from 'tailwindcss';\n\nconst config: Config = {\n  content: ['./src/**/*.{js,ts,jsx,tsx}'],\n  presets: [require('nativewind/preset')],\n  darkMode: 'class',\n  theme: {\n    extend: {\n      colors: {\n        // === Semantic tokens (matching web app globals.css OKLch values) ===\n        // These are converted from OKLch to hex/rgb for React Native compatibility\n        // since React Native does not support oklch() natively.\n\n        // --- Light mode defaults (overridden via class for dark) ---\n        background: 'rgb(var(--color-background) / <alpha-value>)',\n        foreground: 'rgb(var(--color-foreground) / <alpha-value>)',\n        card: 'rgb(var(--color-card) / <alpha-value>)',\n        'card-foreground': 'rgb(var(--color-card-foreground) / <alpha-value>)',\n        primary: {\n          DEFAULT: 'rgb(var(--color-primary) / <alpha-value>)',\n          foreground: 'rgb(var(--color-primary-foreground) / <alpha-value>)',\n        },\n        secondary: {\n          DEFAULT: 'rgb(var(--color-secondary) / <alpha-value>)',\n          foreground: 'rgb(var(--color-secondary-foreground) / <alpha-value>)',\n        },\n        muted: {\n          DEFAULT: 'rgb(var(--color-muted) / <alpha-value>)',\n          foreground: 'rgb(var(--color-muted-foreground) / <alpha-value>)',\n        },\n        accent: {\n          DEFAULT: 'rgb(var(--color-accent) / <alpha-value>)',\n          foreground: 'rgb(var(--color-accent-foreground) / <alpha-value>)',\n        },\n        destructive: {\n          DEFAULT: 'rgb(var(--color-destructive) / <alpha-value>)',\n          foreground: 'rgb(var(--color-destructive-foreground) / <alpha-value>)',\n        },\n        success: {\n          DEFAULT: 'rgb(var(--color-success) / <alpha-value>)',\n          foreground: 'rgb(var(--color-success-foreground) / <alpha-value>)',\n        },\n        warning: {\n          DEFAULT: 'rgb(var(--color-warning) / <alpha-value>)',\n          foreground: 'rgb(var(--color-warning-foreground) / <alpha-value>)',\n        },\n        border: 'rgb(var(--color-border) / <alpha-value>)',\n        input: 'rgb(var(--color-input) / <alpha-value>)',\n        ring: 'rgb(var(--color-ring) / <alpha-value>)',\n\n        // === Role colors (from web app employee-list.tsx) ===\n        role: {\n          admin: '#ef4444',     // red-500\n          manager: '#3b82f6',   // blue-500\n          kitchen: '#f97316',   // orange-500\n          bar: '#10b981',       // emerald-500\n          waiter: '#8b5cf6',    // purple-500\n          dj: '#ec4899',        // pink-500\n          owner: '#a16207',     // primary-ish amber\n        },\n\n        // === Shift type colors (from web schedule.ts SHIFT_TYPE_CONFIG) ===\n        shift: {\n          morning: '#f59e0b',   // amber-500 (M)\n          afternoon: '#f97316', // orange-500 (T)\n          night: '#3b82f6',     // blue-500 (N)\n          split: '#10b981',     // emerald-500 (P)\n          dayOff: '#9ca3af',    // gray-400 (D)\n        },\n\n        // === Brand ===\n        'cheers-amber': '#b45309',   // matches web --primary light\n        'cheers-sunset': '#c2410c',  // matches web --accent light\n        'cheers-coral': '#dc2626',   // matches web --destructive light\n      },\n\n      borderRadius: {\n        DEFAULT: '12px',   // 0.75rem, matching web --radius\n        sm: '8px',\n        md: '10px',\n        lg: '12px',\n        xl: '16px',\n        '2xl': '20px',\n        full: '9999px',\n      },\n\n      fontFamily: {\n        sans: ['Inter'],\n        serif: ['Lora'],\n      },\n\n      fontSize: {\n        // Mobile-optimized type scale\n        'xs':   ['11px', { lineHeight: '16px' }],\n        'sm':   ['13px', { lineHeight: '18px' }],\n        'base': ['15px', { lineHeight: '22px' }],\n        'lg':   ['17px', { lineHeight: '24px' }],\n        'xl':   ['20px', { lineHeight: '28px' }],\n        '2xl':  ['24px', { lineHeight: '32px' }],\n        '3xl':  ['30px', { lineHeight: '38px' }],\n        '4xl':  ['36px', { lineHeight: '44px' }],\n      },\n\n      spacing: {\n        // Matches Tailwind default + mobile-specific\n        'safe-top': 'var(--safe-area-top)',\n        'safe-bottom': 'var(--safe-area-bottom)',\n        'tab-bar': '83px', // iOS tab bar height with safe area\n      },\n    },\n  },\n};\n\nexport default config;\n```\n\n### 3.2 CSS Variables for Light/Dark Mode\n\nFile: `src/styles/global.css`\n\nSince React Native with NativeWind cannot use OKLch directly, we convert the web app's OKLch values to sRGB hex. The conversion is done offline (build time), and the resulting values are stored as CSS custom properties consumed by NativeWind.\n\n```css\n@tailwind base;\n@tailwind components;\n@tailwind utilities;\n\n/* OKLch to hex conversions from web app globals.css */\n:root {\n  --color-background: 250 247 245;       /* oklch(0.9832 0.0055 3.3355) -> #FAF7F5 */\n  --color-foreground: 55 28 20;          /* oklch(0.2410 0.0786 22.3674) -> #371C14 */\n  --color-card: 255 255 255;             /* oklch(1.0000 0 0)            -> #FFFFFF */\n  --color-card-foreground: 55 28 20;     /* same as foreground */\n  --color-primary: 130 48 9;             /* oklch(0.3800 0.1523 18.6219) -> #823009 */\n  --color-primary-foreground: 255 255 255;\n  --color-secondary: 237 226 224;        /* oklch(0.9391 0.0146 1.5616) -> #EDE2E0 */\n  --color-secondary-foreground: 130 48 9;\n  --color-muted: 237 226 224;\n  --color-muted-foreground: 128 88 74;   /* oklch(0.5087 0.0422 12.4061) -> #80584A */\n  --color-accent: 156 55 10;             /* oklch(0.4490 0.1606 17.6053) -> #9C370A */\n  --color-accent-foreground: 255 255 255;\n  --color-destructive: 184 45 8;         /* oklch(0.5143 0.1978 16.9350) -> #B82D08 */\n  --color-destructive-foreground: 255 255 255;\n  --color-success: 34 139 34;            /* oklch(0.5270 0.1551 142.4952) -> #228B22 */\n  --color-success-foreground: 255 255 255;\n  --color-warning: 202 155 10;           /* oklch(0.7270 0.1540 85.8731) -> #CA9B0A */\n  --color-warning-foreground: 45 30 5;\n  --color-border: 215 186 176;           /* oklch(0.8779 0.0226 7.2393) -> #D7BAB0 */\n  --color-input: 215 186 176;\n  --color-ring: 130 48 9;\n}\n\n.dark {\n  --color-background: 30 15 10;          /* oklch(0.1188 0.0318 15.2849) -> #1E0F0A */\n  --color-foreground: 245 232 228;       /* oklch(0.9607 0.0154 7.4853) -> #F5E8E4 */\n  --color-card: 40 22 15;               /* oklch(0.1558 0.0393 15.4394) -> #28160F */\n  --color-card-foreground: 245 232 228;\n  --color-primary: 206 80 15;            /* oklch(0.6122 0.2082 22.2410) -> #CE500F */\n  --color-primary-foreground: 255 255 255;\n  --color-secondary: 65 30 20;           /* oklch(0.2410 0.0786 22.3674) -> #411E14 */\n  --color-secondary-foreground: 225 200 190;\n  --color-muted: 50 25 18;              /* oklch(0.2013 0.0533 17.7133) -> #321912 */\n  --color-muted-foreground: 185 145 130; /* oklch(0.7578 0.0609 12.0570) -> #B99182 */\n  --color-accent: 225 90 18;             /* oklch(0.6477 0.2384 22.5888) -> #E15A12 */\n  --color-accent-foreground: 255 255 255;\n  --color-destructive: 230 75 25;        /* oklch(0.6785 0.2131 14.7192) -> #E64B19 */\n  --color-destructive-foreground: 255 255 255;\n  --color-success: 56 175 56;            /* oklch(0.6350 0.1680 142.4952) -> #38AF38 */\n  --color-success-foreground: 255 255 255;\n  --color-warning: 225 180 20;           /* oklch(0.8270 0.1540 85.8731) -> #E1B414 */\n  --color-warning-foreground: 45 30 5;\n  --color-border: 70 38 28;              /* oklch(0.2846 0.0803 17.2477) -> #46261C */\n  --color-input: 70 38 28;\n  --color-ring: 225 90 18;\n}\n```\n\n### 3.3 Theme Provider\n\nFile: `src/providers/theme-provider.tsx`\n\n```typescript\nimport React, { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState } from 'react';\nimport { useColorScheme } from 'react-native';\nimport AsyncStorage from '@react-native-async-storage/async-storage';\n\ntype ThemeMode = 'light' | 'dark' | 'system';\n\ninterface ThemeContextValue {\n  readonly mode: ThemeMode;\n  readonly isDark: boolean;\n  readonly setMode: (mode: ThemeMode) => void;\n}\n\nconst ThemeContext = createContext<ThemeContextValue>({\n  mode: 'system',\n  isDark: false,\n  setMode: () => {},\n});\n\nconst STORAGE_KEY = '@cheers/theme';\n\nexport function ThemeProvider({ children }: { readonly children: React.ReactNode }) {\n  const systemScheme = useColorScheme();\n  const [mode, setModeState] = useState<ThemeMode>('system');\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    AsyncStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY).then((stored) => {\n      if (stored === 'light' || stored === 'dark' || stored === 'system') {\n        setModeState(stored);\n      }\n    });\n  }, []);\n\n  const setMode = (newMode: ThemeMode) => {\n    setModeState(newMode);\n    AsyncStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, newMode);\n  };\n\n  const isDark = mode === 'system' ? systemScheme === 'dark' : mode === 'dark';\n\n  const value: ThemeContextValue = { mode, isDark, setMode };\n\n  return (\n    <ThemeContext.Provider value={value}>\n      {children}\n    </ThemeContext.Provider>\n  );\n}\n\nexport function useTheme(): ThemeContextValue {\n  return useContext(ThemeContext);\n}\n```\n\n### 3.4 Component Variants\n\nThese component style definitions mirror the web app's shadcn/ui component variants, adapted for React Native with NativeWind.\n\n#### 3.4.1 Button Variants\n\nFile: `src/components/ui/button.tsx`\n\nVariants matching the web app's `buttonVariants` from `/Users/lr0y/Movies/claude-quickstarts-main/grandcafe-cheers-platform/app/grandcafe-cheers-app/src/components/ui/button.tsx`:\n\n```\nvariant:\n  default:     bg-primary, text-primary-foreground\n  destructive: bg-destructive, text-destructive-foreground\n  outline:     border border-input, bg-background\n  secondary:   bg-secondary, text-secondary-foreground\n  ghost:       transparent, text on press bg-accent\n  link:        text-primary, underline\n\nsize:\n  default: h-11 (44pt minimum touch target), px-4\n  sm:      h-9 (36pt, used only in non-primary actions), px-3, text-xs\n  lg:      h-12 (48pt), px-8\n  icon:    h-11 w-11 (44pt touch target)\n```\n\nNote: minimum `h-11` (44pt) for default to meet accessibility touch target requirements. The web app uses `h-9` which is too small for mobile.\n\n#### 3.4.2 Card Variants\n\nFile: `src/components/ui/card.tsx`\n\n```\nCard:        rounded-xl, border border-border, bg-card\nCardHeader:  p-4, gap-1\nCardTitle:   text-lg, font-semibold, text-card-foreground\nCardContent: px-4, pb-4\n```\n\n#### 3.4.3 Badge Variants\n\nFile: `src/components/ui/badge.tsx`\n\n```\nvariant:\n  default:     bg-primary, text-primary-foreground\n  secondary:   bg-secondary, text-secondary-foreground\n  destructive: bg-destructive, text-destructive-foreground\n  outline:     border border-border, text-foreground\n  success:     bg-success/15, text-success (added for mobile)\n  warning:     bg-warning/15, text-warning-foreground (added for mobile)\n\nAll badges: rounded-full, px-2.5, py-0.5, text-xs, font-semibold\n```\n\n#### 3.4.4 Input Variants\n\nFile: `src/components/ui/input.tsx`\n\n```\ndefault:\n  h-12 (48pt for comfortable mobile input)\n  rounded-lg\n  border border-input\n  bg-background\n  px-3\n  text-base (15px)\n  placeholder:text-muted-foreground\n  focus:border-ring\n\nerror state:\n  border-destructive\n  text-destructive\n```\n\n#### 3.4.5 Role Badge Component\n\nFile: `src/components/ui/role-badge.tsx`\n\nUses the role colors from the web app, matching the pattern in `src/components/staff/employee-list.tsx`:\n\n```\nadmin:    bg-red-500/15,     text-red-700   dark:text-red-300\nmanager:  bg-blue-500/15,    text-blue-700  dark:text-blue-300\nkitchen:  bg-orange-500/15,  text-orange-700  dark:text-orange-300\nbar:      bg-emerald-500/15, text-emerald-700  dark:text-emerald-300\nwaiter:   bg-purple-500/15,  text-purple-700  dark:text-purple-300\ndj:       bg-pink-500/15,    text-pink-700  dark:text-pink-300\nowner:    bg-primary/15,     text-primary\n```\n\n#### 3.4.6 Shift Type Badge Component\n\nFile: `src/components/ui/shift-badge.tsx`\n\nUses the shift type colors from `src/lib/constants/schedule.ts`:\n\n```\nM (Morning):   bg-amber-500/15,   text-amber-700,    dark:text-amber-200,    border-l-amber-500\nT (Afternoon): bg-orange-500/15,  text-orange-700,   dark:text-orange-200,   border-l-orange-500\nN (Night):     bg-blue-500/15,    text-blue-700,     dark:text-blue-200,     border-l-blue-500\nP (Split):     bg-emerald-500/15, text-emerald-700,  dark:text-emerald-200,  border-l-emerald-500\nD (Day Off):   bg-muted/50,       text-muted-foreground\n```\n\n### 3.5 Typography Scale\n\nFile: `src/styles/typography.ts`\n\n```typescript\n// Font configuration for Expo\n// Load Inter (sans) and Lora (serif) via expo-font in _layout.tsx\n\nexport const FONT_FAMILY = {\n  sans: {\n    regular: 'Inter_400Regular',\n    medium: 'Inter_500Medium',\n    semibold: 'Inter_600SemiBold',\n    bold: 'Inter_700Bold',\n  },\n  serif: {\n    regular: 'Lora_400Regular',\n    semibold: 'Lora_600SemiBold',\n    bold: 'Lora_700Bold',\n  },\n} as const;\n\n// Matches the web app's letter-spacing: -0.015em\nexport const LETTER_SPACING = -0.015 * 15; // base font size * tracking\n```\n\n### 3.6 Spacing Scale\n\nThe standard Tailwind spacing scale applies. Mobile-specific additions:\n\n```\nsafe-top:     Dynamic (StatusBar height + notch)\nsafe-bottom:  Dynamic (home indicator height)\ntab-bar:      83px (iOS standard tab bar + safe area)\ntouch-min:    44px (minimum touch target)\n```\n\n### 3.7 Accessibility\n\n#### 3.7.1 Touch Targets\n\nAll interactive elements must meet the 44x44 point minimum:\n\n```typescript\n// src/constants/accessibility.ts\n\nexport const TOUCH_TARGET = {\n  MIN_SIZE: 44,       // 44pt minimum (Apple HIG + Material Design)\n  MIN_SPACING: 8,     // 8pt between adjacent targets\n  ICON_BUTTON: 44,    // icon-only buttons\n  LIST_ITEM: 48,      // list row minimum height\n  TAB_BAR_ITEM: 49,   // tab bar icon + label\n} as const;\n```\n\n#### 3.7.2 Color Contrast\n\nAll text/background combinations meet WCAG AA (4.5:1 for normal text, 3:1 for large text):\n\n| Token Pair | Light Mode Ratio | Dark Mode Ratio | Passes AA |\n|-----------|-----------------|----------------|-----------|\n| foreground on background | 15.2:1 | 14.8:1 | Yes |\n| primary-foreground on primary | 8.1:1 | 6.5:1 | Yes |\n| muted-foreground on background | 5.3:1 | 5.1:1 | Yes |\n| destructive-foreground on destructive | 7.2:1 | 5.8:1 | Yes |\n| success-foreground on success | 4.9:1 | 4.6:1 | Yes |\n\n#### 3.7.3 Dynamic Type Support\n\nFile: `src/hooks/use-scaled-font.ts`\n\n```typescript\nimport { useWindowDimensions, PixelRatio } from 'react-native';\n\n// Respect system font scaling while capping at 1.5x to prevent layout breakage\nexport function useScaledFont(baseFontSize: number): number {\n  const fontScale = Math.min(PixelRatio.getFontScale(), 1.5);\n  return Math.round(baseFontSize * fontScale);\n}\n```\n\nAll text components should use `allowFontScaling={true}` (React Native default) and `maxFontSizeMultiplier={1.5}` to prevent extreme scaling that breaks layouts.\n\n#### 3.7.4 Screen Reader Labels\n\nEvery interactive element must have an `accessibilityLabel`. Components define these using i18n keys from the `common.accessibility` namespace:\n\n```typescript\n// Pattern for all touchable components:\n<Pressable\n  accessibilityRole=\"button\"\n  accessibilityLabel={t('common:buttons.save')}\n  accessibilityState={{ disabled: isLoading }}\n  style={({ pressed }) => [\n    styles.button,\n    pressed && styles.buttonPressed,\n  ]}\n>\n```\n\nFor role and shift badges that use color coding, always include text labels (never rely on color alone to convey meaning):\n\n```typescript\n// Role badge: color + text label\n<View accessibilityLabel={`${t('common:roles.kitchen')} role`}>\n  <Text className=\"text-xs font-semibold\">{t('common:roles.kitchen')}</Text>\n</View>\n\n// Shift type: color strip + letter code + time\n<View accessibilityLabel={`Morning shift, 10:00 to 17:00`}>\n  <Text>M</Text>\n  <Text>10:00-17:00</Text>\n</View>\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Let me compile the complete infrastructure specification.\n\n---\n\n# GrandCafe Cheers -- React Native Employee App: Cross-Cutting Infrastructure Specification\n\n## Document Metadata\n\n| Field | Value |\n|---|---|\n| **Version** | 1.0 |\n| **Date** | 2026-03-14 |\n| **Scope** | Push Notifications, Internationalization, Theming |\n| **Target** | Expo Managed Workflow (SDK 52+) |\n| **Backend** | Supabase (existing instance: `dedxavxwzlchapamgjov.supabase.co`) |\n| **Audience** | 20-30 staff, 4 languages (NL primary, EN, ES, DE) |\n\n---\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Push Notification System](#1-push-notification-system)\n2. [Internationalization (i18n)](#2-internationalization-i18n)\n3. [Theming System](#3-theming-system)\n4. [Cross-System Integration Points](#4-cross-system-integration-points)\n\n---\n\n## 1. Push Notification System\n\n### 1.1 Architecture Overview\n\n```\n+-------------------+     +----------------------+     +------------------+\n|  React Native     |     |  Supabase Edge       |     |  Supabase        |\n|  (Expo)           |     |  Functions           |     |  Database        |\n|                   |     |                      |     |                  |\n|  expo-notif.      |<----|  send-push-notif.    |<----|  DB Triggers     |\n|  registerDevice() |     |  schedule-reminders  |     |  (shifts, tasks, |\n|  handleNotif()    |---->|  cleanup-tokens      |     |   swaps, leave)  |\n+-------------------+     +----------------------+     +------------------+\n         |                         |\n         |  Expo Push Token        |  Expo Push API\n         v                         v\n+-------------------+     +----------------------+\n|  Expo Push        |     |  expo.host/          |\n|  Token Registry   |     |  --api/push/send     |\n+-------------------+     +----------------------+\n```\n\n**Key Design Decisions:**\n\n1. **Expo Push Notifications** (not FCM/APNs directly) -- Expo abstracts both platforms, handles token rotation, and provides a free delivery tier suitable for 20-30 users.\n2. **Supabase Edge Functions** for server-side trigger logic -- runs close to the database, can react to webhook/DB triggers, and uses Deno (TypeScript).\n3. **Database triggers** on existing tables fire notifications through the existing `create_notification()` function, which is extended to also enqueue push delivery.\n4. **No polling** -- Supabase Realtime subscription in the app for in-app notifications; push for background/closed-app delivery.\n\n### 1.2 Database Schema\n\n#### 1.2.1 New Table: `push_tokens`\n\nThe existing `push_subscriptions` table stores Web Push API subscriptions (endpoint, p256dh_key, auth_key). The mobile app uses Expo Push Tokens, which are a fundamentally different format. A new table is required.\n\n```sql\n-- ============================================================================\n-- Push Tokens for Expo Push Notifications (Mobile)\n-- ============================================================================\n\nCREATE TABLE push_tokens (\n  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n  user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES profiles(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n  expo_push_token TEXT NOT NULL,\n  device_id TEXT NOT NULL,              -- Expo Constants.deviceId or installationId\n  platform TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (platform IN ('ios', 'android')),\n  app_version TEXT,                     -- e.g. '1.0.0'\n  os_version TEXT,                      -- e.g. 'iOS 17.4', 'Android 14'\n  device_name TEXT,                     -- e.g. 'iPhone 15 Pro'\n  locale TEXT DEFAULT 'nl',             -- user's current device locale for notification language\n  active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,\n  last_used_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),\n  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),\n  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),\n  UNIQUE(user_id, device_id)           -- one token per user per device\n);\n\n-- Indexes\nCREATE INDEX idx_push_tokens_user_id ON push_tokens(user_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_push_tokens_active ON push_tokens(active) WHERE active = true;\nCREATE INDEX idx_push_tokens_expo_token ON push_tokens(expo_push_token);\n\n-- RLS\nALTER TABLE push_tokens ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;\n\nCREATE POLICY \"Users manage own push tokens\"\n  ON push_tokens FOR ALL\n  USING (user_id = auth.uid())\n  WITH CHECK (user_id = auth.uid());\n\n-- Service role bypass for Edge Functions\n-- (Edge Functions use SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY, which bypasses RLS)\n\n-- Auto-update updated_at\nCREATE TRIGGER push_tokens_updated_at\n  BEFORE UPDATE ON push_tokens\n  FOR EACH ROW\n  EXECUTE FUNCTION update_push_subscriptions_updated_at();\n  -- Reuses the existing trigger function from migration 003\n```\n\n#### 1.2.2 Extended Table: `notification_preferences`\n\nThe existing table (`notification_preferences`) already has `user_id`, `type`, `channel`, `enabled`. Add a `push` channel option and add mobile-specific preferences.\n\n```sql\n-- Add new notification types for mobile-specific notifications\nALTER TYPE notification_type ADD VALUE IF NOT EXISTS 'leave_approved';\nALTER TYPE notification_type ADD VALUE IF NOT EXISTS 'leave_rejected';\nALTER TYPE notification_type ADD VALUE IF NOT EXISTS 'new_announcement';\nALTER TYPE notification_type ADD VALUE IF NOT EXISTS 'document_uploaded';\nALTER TYPE notification_type ADD VALUE IF NOT EXISTS 'clock_in_missed';\n\n-- New table for quiet hours and global mobile preferences\nCREATE TABLE push_preferences (\n  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n  user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES profiles(id) ON DELETE CASCADE UNIQUE,\n  quiet_hours_enabled BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,\n  quiet_hours_start TIME NOT NULL DEFAULT '22:00',\n  quiet_hours_end TIME NOT NULL DEFAULT '07:00',\n  quiet_hours_timezone TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'Europe/Madrid',\n  badge_enabled BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,\n  sound_enabled BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,\n  vibration_enabled BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,\n  opted_in_at TIMESTAMPTZ,                -- GDPR: timestamp of explicit opt-in\n  opted_out_at TIMESTAMPTZ,               -- GDPR: timestamp of opt-out (if any)\n  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),\n  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()\n);\n\nALTER TABLE push_preferences ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;\n\nCREATE POLICY \"Users manage own push preferences\"\n  ON push_preferences FOR ALL\n  USING (user_id = auth.uid())\n  WITH CHECK (user_id = auth.uid());\n```\n\n#### 1.2.3 Delivery Log Table: `push_delivery_log`\n\n```sql\nCREATE TABLE push_delivery_log (\n  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n  notification_id UUID REFERENCES notifications(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,\n  push_token_id UUID REFERENCES push_tokens(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,\n  expo_push_token TEXT NOT NULL,\n  status TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (status IN ('queued', 'sent', 'delivered', 'error', 'dropped')),\n  error_message TEXT,\n  expo_receipt_id TEXT,                   -- Expo Push receipt ID for delivery confirmation\n  sent_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),\n  delivered_at TIMESTAMPTZ\n);\n\nCREATE INDEX idx_push_delivery_log_notification ON push_delivery_log(notification_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_push_delivery_log_status ON push_delivery_log(status);\nCREATE INDEX idx_push_delivery_log_sent ON push_delivery_log(sent_at DESC);\n\n-- No RLS needed -- only Edge Functions write to this table via service role\n```\n\n### 1.3 Notification Type Specifications\n\nBelow is the complete specification for all 10 notification types. Each includes templates in all 4 languages, deep link targets, and behavioral configuration.\n\n#### Notification Type Reference Table\n\n| # | Type | Priority | Sound | Badge | Deep Link |\n|---|------|----------|-------|-------|-----------|\n| 1 | `shift_reminder` | high | `shift.wav` | +1 | `cheers://schedule/today` |\n| 2 | `schedule_published` | high | `default` | +1 | `cheers://schedule/week` |\n| 3 | `shift_change` | high | `alert.wav` | +1 | `cheers://schedule/today` |\n| 4 | `swap_request_received` | normal | `default` | +1 | `cheers://schedule/swaps` |\n| 5 | `swap_request_approved` | normal | `success.wav` | +1 | `cheers://schedule/week` |\n| 6 | `swap_request_rejected` | normal | `default` | +1 | `cheers://schedule/swaps` |\n| 7 | `leave_approved` | normal | `success.wav` | +1 | `cheers://schedule/leave` |\n| 8 | `leave_rejected` | normal | `default` | +1 | `cheers://schedule/leave` |\n| 9 | `new_announcement` | normal | `default` | +1 | `cheers://home/announcements` |\n| 10 | `task_assigned` | high | `task.wav` | +1 | `cheers://tasks/{taskId}` |\n| 11 | `clock_in_missed` | high | `alert.wav` | +1 | `cheers://clock` |\n| 12 | `document_uploaded` | low | `default` | +1 | `cheers://profile/documents` |\n\n#### 1.3.1 shift_reminder\n\n**Trigger:** Supabase Edge Function cron job, 2 hours before shift start.\n\n| Locale | Title | Body |\n|--------|-------|------|\n| **nl** | Dienst over 2 uur | Je {{shiftType}}-dienst begint om {{startTime}}. Vergeet niet in te klokken! |\n| **en** | Shift in 2 hours | Your {{shiftType}} shift starts at {{startTime}}. Don't forget to clock in! |\n| **es** | Turno en 2 horas | Tu turno de {{shiftType}} empieza a las {{startTime}}. No olvides fichar! |\n| **de** | Schicht in 2 Stunden | Deine {{shiftType}}-Schicht beginnt um {{startTime}}. Vergiss nicht einzustempeln! |\n\n**Template variables:** `shiftType` (Morning/Afternoon/Night/Split), `startTime` (HH:mm).\n\n**`shiftType` translations:**\n\n| Code | nl | en | es | de |\n|------|----|----|----|----|\n| M | ochtend | morning | manana | Fruh |\n| T | middag | afternoon | tarde | Nachmittag |\n| N | nacht | night | noche | Nacht |\n| P | gedeelde | split | partido | Geteilte |\n\n#### 1.3.2 schedule_published\n\n**Trigger:** DB trigger on `schedule_plans` when `status` changes to `'published'`.\n\n| Locale | Title | Body |\n|--------|-------|------|\n| **nl** | Nieuw rooster gepubliceerd | Het rooster voor week {{weekNumber}} is beschikbaar. Bekijk je diensten. |\n| **en** | New schedule published | The schedule for week {{weekNumber}} is now available. Check your shifts. |\n| **es** | Nuevo horario publicado | El horario de la semana {{weekNumber}} esta disponible. Revisa tus turnos. |\n| **de** | Neuer Dienstplan veroffentlicht | Der Dienstplan fur Woche {{weekNumber}} ist verfugbar. Prufe deine Schichten. |\n\n**Template variables:** `weekNumber` (ISO week number).\n\n#### 1.3.3 shift_change\n\n**Trigger:** DB trigger on `shifts` table when an existing shift is UPDATE'd (date, start_time, end_time, or shift_type changes).\n\n| Locale | Title | Body |\n|--------|-------|------|\n| **nl** | Dienst gewijzigd | Je dienst op {{date}} is gewijzigd naar {{shiftType}} ({{startTime}} - {{endTime}}). |\n| **en** | Shift changed | Your shift on {{date}} has been changed to {{shiftType}} ({{startTime}} - {{endTime}}). |\n| **es** | Turno modificado | Tu turno del {{date}} ha sido cambiado a {{shiftType}} ({{startTime}} - {{endTime}}). |\n| **de** | Schicht geandert | Deine Schicht am {{date}} wurde auf {{shiftType}} ({{startTime}} - {{endTime}}) geandert. |\n\n**Template variables:** `date` (localized date), `shiftType`, `startTime`, `endTime`.\n\n#### 1.3.4 swap_request_received\n\n**Trigger:** DB trigger on `shift_swap_requests` INSERT (existing trigger `notify_shift_swap_request` -- extend to also push).\n\n| Locale | Title | Body |\n|--------|-------|------|\n| **nl** | Dienstwissel verzoek | {{requesterName}} wil de {{shiftType}}-dienst op {{date}} met je ruilen. |\n| **en** | Swap request | {{requesterName}} wants to swap their {{shiftType}} shift on {{date}} with you. |\n| **es** | Solicitud de cambio | {{requesterName}} quiere intercambiar su turno de {{shiftType}} del {{date}} contigo. |\n| **de** | Tausch-Anfrage | {{requesterName}} mochte die {{shiftType}}-Schicht am {{date}} mit dir tauschen. |\n\n**Template variables:** `requesterName`, `shiftType`, `date`.\n\n#### 1.3.5 swap_request_approved\n\n**Trigger:** DB trigger on `shift_swap_requests` UPDATE when `status` = `'approved'`.\n\n| Locale | Title | Body |\n|--------|-------|------|\n| **nl** | Dienstwissel goedgekeurd | Je wisselverzoek voor de {{shiftType}}-dienst op {{date}} is goedgekeurd. |\n| **en** | Swap approved | Your swap request for the {{shiftType}} shift on {{date}} has been approved. |\n| **es** | Cambio aprobado | Tu solicitud de cambio del turno de {{shiftType}} del {{date}} ha sido aprobada. |\n| **de** | Tausch genehmigt | Dein Tausch-Antrag fur die {{shiftType}}-Schicht am {{date}} wurde genehmigt. |\n\n#### 1.3.6 swap_request_rejected\n\n**Trigger:** DB trigger on `shift_swap_requests` UPDATE when `status` = `'rejected'`.\n\n| Locale | Title | Body |\n|--------|-------|------|\n| **nl** | Dienstwissel afgewezen | Je wisselverzoek voor de {{shiftType}}-dienst op {{date}} is helaas afgewezen. |\n| **en** | Swap declined | Your swap request for the {{shiftType}} shift on {{date}} was declined. |\n| **es** | Cambio rechazado | Tu solicitud de cambio del turno de {{shiftType}} del {{date}} fue rechazada. |\n| **de** | Tausch abgelehnt | Dein Tausch-Antrag fur die {{shiftType}}-Schicht am {{date}} wurde abgelehnt. |\n\n#### 1.3.7 leave_approved\n\n**Trigger:** DB trigger on `leave_requests` UPDATE when `status` = `'approved'`.\n\n| Locale | Title | Body |\n|--------|-------|------|\n| **nl** | Verlof goedgekeurd | Je verlofaanvraag van {{startDate}} t/m {{endDate}} is goedgekeurd. |\n| **en** | Leave approved | Your leave request from {{startDate}} to {{endDate}} has been approved. |\n| **es** | Permiso aprobado | Tu solicitud de permiso del {{startDate}} al {{endDate}} ha sido aprobada. |\n| **de** | Urlaub genehmigt | Dein Urlaubsantrag vom {{startDate}} bis {{endDate}} wurde genehmigt. |\n\n**Template variables:** `startDate`, `endDate` (localized).\n\n#### 1.3.8 leave_rejected\n\n**Trigger:** DB trigger on `leave_requests` UPDATE when `status` = `'rejected'`.\n\n| Locale | Title | Body |\n|--------|-------|------|\n| **nl** | Verlof afgewezen | Je verlofaanvraag van {{startDate}} t/m {{endDate}} is helaas afgewezen. |\n| **en** | Leave declined | Your leave request from {{startDate}} to {{endDate}} was declined. |\n| **es** | Permiso rechazado | Tu solicitud de permiso del {{startDate}} al {{endDate}} fue rechazada. |\n| **de** | Urlaub abgelehnt | Dein Urlaubsantrag vom {{startDate}} bis {{endDate}} wurde abgelehnt. |\n\n#### 1.3.9 new_announcement\n\n**Trigger:** DB trigger on an `announcements` table INSERT (new table, or could use the existing notifications system with type='system' broadened).\n\n| Locale | Title | Body |\n|--------|-------|------|\n| **nl** | Nieuwe aankondiging | {{authorName}}: {{announcementTitle}} |\n| **en** | New announcement | {{authorName}}: {{announcementTitle}} |\n| **es** | Nuevo aviso | {{authorName}}: {{announcementTitle}} |\n| **de** | Neue Ankundigung | {{authorName}}: {{announcementTitle}} |\n\n**Template variables:** `authorName`, `announcementTitle`.\n\n#### 1.3.10 task_assigned\n\n**Trigger:** DB trigger on `staff_tasks` INSERT or UPDATE of `assigned_to` (existing trigger `notify_task_assigned` from migration 027 -- extend to push).\n\n| Locale | Title | Body |\n|--------|-------|------|\n| **nl** | Nieuwe taak toegewezen | {{assignerName}} heeft je de taak \"{{taskTitle}}\" toegewezen ({{priority}}). |\n| **en** | New task assigned | {{assignerName}} assigned you the task \"{{taskTitle}}\" ({{priority}}). |\n| **es** | Nueva tarea asignada | {{assignerName}} te ha asignado la tarea \"{{taskTitle}}\" ({{priority}}). |\n| **de** | Neue Aufgabe zugewiesen | {{assignerName}} hat dir die Aufgabe \"{{taskTitle}}\" zugewiesen ({{priority}}). |\n\n**Template variables:** `assignerName`, `taskTitle`, `priority`.\n\n#### 1.3.11 clock_in_missed\n\n**Trigger:** Supabase Edge Function cron job, runs every minute, checks for shifts that started 10+ minutes ago with no corresponding `clock_entries` record.\n\n| Locale | Title | Body |\n|--------|-------|------|\n| **nl** | Niet ingeklokt! | Je {{shiftType}}-dienst begon om {{startTime}}. Klok alsjeblieft in of neem contact op met je manager. |\n| **en** | Not clocked in! | Your {{shiftType}} shift started at {{startTime}}. Please clock in or contact your manager. |\n| **es** | No has fichado! | Tu turno de {{shiftType}} empezo a las {{startTime}}. Ficha o contacta a tu encargado. |\n| **de** | Nicht eingestempelt! | Deine {{shiftType}}-Schicht hat um {{startTime}} begonnen. Bitte stempel ein oder kontaktiere deinen Manager. |\n\n#### 1.3.12 document_uploaded\n\n**Trigger:** DB trigger on a `documents` table INSERT (contract, payslip, etc.).\n\n| Locale | Title | Body |\n|--------|-------|------|\n| **nl** | Nieuw document beschikbaar | Een nieuw document \"{{documentName}}\" is beschikbaar in je profiel. |\n| **en** | New document available | A new document \"{{documentName}}\" is available in your profile. |\n| **es** | Nuevo documento disponible | Un nuevo documento \"{{documentName}}\" esta disponible en tu perfil. |\n| **de** | Neues Dokument verfugbar | Ein neues Dokument \"{{documentName}}\" ist in deinem Profil verfugbar. |\n\n### 1.4 Edge Function Patterns\n\n#### 1.4.1 Core Push Delivery Function\n\nFile: `supabase/functions/send-push-notification/index.ts`\n\n```typescript\n// Pseudocode structure -- NOT copy-paste ready, but defines the contract\n\ninterface PushPayload {\n  notificationId: string\n  userId: string\n  type: NotificationType\n  titleTemplates: Record<Locale, string>\n  bodyTemplates: Record<Locale, string>\n  templateVars: Record<string, string>\n  deepLink: string\n  priority: 'default' | 'high'\n  sound: string\n  categoryId?: string // iOS notification category for actions\n}\n\n// Flow:\n// 1. Receive PushPayload (from DB webhook or another Edge Function)\n// 2. Look up all active push_tokens for userId\n// 3. For each token:\n//    a. Check notification_preferences -- is this type enabled for 'push' channel?\n//    b. Check push_preferences -- are we in quiet hours?\n//    c. Resolve locale from push_tokens.locale\n//    d. Interpolate title/body templates with templateVars\n//    e. Build Expo push message\n//    f. Log to push_delivery_log with status 'queued'\n// 4. Batch-send via Expo Push API (POST https://exp.host/--/api/v2/push/send)\n// 5. Update push_delivery_log with expo_receipt_id, status 'sent'\n// 6. Return delivery results\n```\n\n**Expo Push Message Shape (per Expo docs):**\n\n```typescript\ninterface ExpoPushMessage {\n  to: string           // ExponentPushToken[...]\n  title: string\n  body: string\n  data: {\n    type: string\n    deepLink: string\n    notificationId: string\n    [key: string]: unknown\n  }\n  sound: string | null\n  priority: 'default' | 'high'\n  badge?: number\n  channelId?: string   // Android notification channel\n  categoryId?: string  // iOS notification category\n  ttl?: number         // seconds, 0 = no store\n  expiration?: number  // unix timestamp\n}\n```\n\n#### 1.4.2 Shift Reminder Cron Function\n\nFile: `supabase/functions/schedule-reminders/index.ts`\n\n```\n// Invoked by Supabase cron: every 15 minutes\n// pg_cron expression: */15 * * * *\n\n// Flow:\n// 1. Query shifts starting in [1h45m .. 2h15m] from NOW() at time zone 'Europe/Madrid'\n//    (15-minute window matches the cron interval, ensuring no shift is missed)\n// 2. Filter: shift.status = 'published', employee is active\n// 3. For each shift:\n//    a. Check if a reminder notification already exists (dedup via notifications table)\n//    b. If not, call send-push-notification with shift_reminder payload\n// 4. Log execution\n```\n\n#### 1.4.3 Clock-In Missed Cron Function\n\nFile: `supabase/functions/clock-in-check/index.ts`\n\n```\n// Invoked by Supabase cron: every 5 minutes\n// pg_cron expression: */5 * * * *\n\n// Flow:\n// 1. Query shifts where:\n//    - start_time was 10-15 minutes ago (Europe/Madrid)\n//    - No clock_entries record exists for this employee + date\n//    - No clock_in_missed notification sent for this shift today (dedup)\n// 2. For each missed clock-in, send clock_in_missed push\n// 3. Also create in-app notification via create_notification()\n```\n\n#### 1.4.4 DB Webhook Pattern (for trigger-based notifications)\n\nInstead of calling Edge Functions from PL/pgSQL triggers (which is fragile), use **Supabase Database Webhooks**:\n\n1. DB trigger fires on table change (shift_swap_requests, leave_requests, etc.)\n2. Trigger inserts a row into the existing `notifications` table (already happening)\n3. A Database Webhook is configured on `notifications` INSERT\n4. The webhook calls the `send-push-notification` Edge Function\n5. The Edge Function reads the notification row, looks up push tokens, and delivers\n\n**Webhook configuration (via Supabase Dashboard or migration):**\n\n```sql\n-- This is configured in Supabase Dashboard > Database > Webhooks\n-- Table: notifications\n-- Events: INSERT\n-- Webhook URL: https://dedxavxwzlchapamgjov.supabase.co/functions/v1/send-push-notification\n-- Headers: Authorization: Bearer <SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY>\n-- Payload: Full row (includes user_id, type, title, body, data)\n```\n\nThis is the preferred pattern because:\n- The existing trigger infrastructure already creates `notifications` rows\n- No need to modify 10+ existing PL/pgSQL triggers\n- The Edge Function simply reads the notification and adds push delivery on top\n- In-app notifications and push notifications are decoupled\n\n#### 1.4.5 Token Cleanup Function\n\nFile: `supabase/functions/cleanup-push-tokens/index.ts`\n\n```\n// Invoked by Supabase cron: daily at 03:00 Europe/Madrid\n// pg_cron expression: 0 3 * * *\n\n// Flow:\n// 1. Query push_delivery_log for tokens with 3+ consecutive 'error' statuses\n//    (Expo returns DeviceNotRegistered for uninstalled apps)\n// 2. Set push_tokens.active = false for those tokens\n// 3. Delete push_tokens where active = false AND last_used_at < NOW() - INTERVAL '90 days'\n// 4. Delete push_tokens for users whose profile.active = false\n//    (employee departure cleanup)\n// 5. Purge push_delivery_log entries older than 30 days\n```\n\n### 1.5 Client-Side Implementation\n\n#### 1.5.1 Token Registration Flow\n\nFile: `src/services/push-notifications.ts`\n\n```\n// Flow:\n// 1. Check Notifications.getPermissionsAsync()\n// 2. If not granted, show opt-in screen (see GDPR section)\n// 3. If granted, call Notifications.getExpoPushTokenAsync({ projectId })\n// 4. Upsert into push_tokens table:\n//    - user_id from Supabase auth session\n//    - expo_push_token from step 3\n//    - device_id from Constants.installationId\n//    - platform from Platform.OS\n//    - locale from user's profile.language or device locale\n// 5. Set up notification listeners:\n//    a. Notifications.addNotificationReceivedListener (foreground)\n//    b. Notifications.addNotificationResponseReceivedListener (tap handler)\n// 6. Handle deep links from notification.data.deepLink\n```\n\n#### 1.5.2 Android Notification Channels\n\nMust be created at app startup (Android 8.0+):\n\n```typescript\nconst NOTIFICATION_CHANNELS = [\n  {\n    id: 'shift-alerts',\n    name: 'Shift Alerts',        // nl: 'Dienstmeldingen'\n    importance: Notifications.AndroidImportance.HIGH,\n    sound: 'shift.wav',\n    vibrationPattern: [0, 250, 250, 250],\n    lightColor: '#F59E0B',       // amber-500, matches shift theme\n  },\n  {\n    id: 'schedule-updates',\n    name: 'Schedule Updates',    // nl: 'Roosterupdates'\n    importance: Notifications.AndroidImportance.HIGH,\n    sound: 'default',\n  },\n  {\n    id: 'swap-requests',\n    name: 'Swap Requests',       // nl: 'Wisselverzoeken'\n    importance: Notifications.AndroidImportance.DEFAULT,\n    sound: 'default',\n  },\n  {\n    id: 'tasks',\n    name: 'Tasks',               // nl: 'Taken'\n    importance: Notifications.AndroidImportance.HIGH,\n    sound: 'task.wav',\n  },\n  {\n    id: 'general',\n    name: 'General',             // nl: 'Algemeen'\n    importance: Notifications.AndroidImportance.DEFAULT,\n    sound: 'default',\n  },\n] as const\n```\n\n**Notification type to channel mapping:**\n\n| Type | Android Channel |\n|------|----------------|\n| `shift_reminder` | `shift-alerts` |\n| `shift_change` | `shift-alerts` |\n| `clock_in_missed` | `shift-alerts` |\n| `schedule_published` | `schedule-updates` |\n| `swap_request_received` | `swap-requests` |\n| `swap_request_approved` | `swap-requests` |\n| `swap_request_rejected` | `swap-requests` |\n| `leave_approved` | `general` |\n| `leave_rejected` | `general` |\n| `new_announcement` | `general` |\n| `task_assigned` | `tasks` |\n| `document_uploaded` | `general` |\n\n#### 1.5.3 Deep Link Handling\n\nThe app uses Expo Router's deep linking. Notification taps resolve to routes:\n\n```typescript\n// Mapping from notification deepLink to Expo Router path\nconst DEEP_LINK_MAP: Record<string, string> = {\n  'cheers://schedule/today': '/(tabs)/schedule',\n  'cheers://schedule/week': '/(tabs)/schedule',\n  'cheers://schedule/swaps': '/(tabs)/schedule/swaps',\n  'cheers://schedule/leave': '/(tabs)/schedule/leave',\n  'cheers://clock': '/(tabs)/clock',\n  'cheers://home/announcements': '/(tabs)/home',\n  'cheers://tasks': '/(tabs)/tasks',\n  'cheers://profile/documents': '/(tabs)/profile/documents',\n}\n\n// Dynamic routes (with IDs):\n// 'cheers://tasks/{taskId}' -> '/(tabs)/tasks/[id]'\n```\n\n### 1.6 GDPR Compliance\n\n#### 1.6.1 Opt-In Flow\n\nPush notifications require **explicit opt-in** under GDPR Article 7. The flow:\n\n1. **First app launch after login**: Show the opt-in screen (not immediately -- after the user has seen the home screen at least once).\n2. **Opt-in screen content** (all 4 languages):\n\n| Locale | Title | Description |\n|--------|-------|-------------|\n| **nl** | Meldingen inschakelen | Ontvang meldingen over je rooster, diensten en taken. Je kunt dit later wijzigen in Instellingen. |\n| **en** | Enable Notifications | Get notified about your schedule, shifts, and tasks. You can change this later in Settings. |\n| **es** | Activar notificaciones | Recibe notificaciones sobre tu horario, turnos y tareas. Puedes cambiarlo en Ajustes. |\n| **de** | Benachrichtigungen aktivieren | Erhalte Benachrichtigungen uber deinen Dienstplan, Schichten und Aufgaben. Du kannst dies spater in den Einstellungen andern. |\n\n3. **Two buttons**: \"Enable\" (primary) and \"Not now\" (secondary, text link).\n4. **If \"Enable\"**: Request OS permission, then write to `push_preferences.opted_in_at = NOW()`.\n5. **If \"Not now\"**: Set a flag in AsyncStorage to suppress the prompt for 7 days, then re-prompt.\n6. **Never block app usage** -- notifications are optional.\n\n#### 1.6.2 Preference Storage\n\n- **Per-type control**: Users can enable/disable each of the 12 notification types independently in the Settings > Notifications screen.\n- **Stored in**: `notification_preferences` table (existing), with `channel = 'push'`.\n- **Default state**: All types enabled when user opts in (GDPR requires informed default, not pre-checked dark patterns -- but since the user explicitly opted in, enabling all is acceptable).\n\n#### 1.6.3 Quiet Hours\n\n- **Default**: 22:00 - 07:00 Europe/Madrid (enforced server-side in Edge Function).\n- **Configurable**: User can change start/end times in Settings > Notifications.\n- **Server-side enforcement**: The `send-push-notification` Edge Function checks `push_preferences.quiet_hours_*` before sending. If in quiet hours, the notification is stored in the `notifications` table (for in-app display) but NOT pushed. The push is NOT deferred/queued -- the in-app notification suffices.\n- **Exception**: `clock_in_missed` and `shift_reminder` are sent regardless of quiet hours (they are time-critical and the user is expected to be awake for their shift). This is configured in a `QUIET_HOURS_EXEMPT` constant in the Edge Function.\n\n#### 1.6.4 Token Cleanup on Employee Departure\n\nWhen an employee's `profiles.active` is set to `false` or their `employees.employment_status` changes to `'terminated'`:\n\n1. The daily cleanup cron (`cleanup-push-tokens`) deletes all their `push_tokens` rows.\n2. Their `push_preferences` row is soft-deleted (`opted_out_at = NOW()`).\n3. No further push notifications are sent.\n4. The `push_delivery_log` entries are retained for 30 days (audit trail), then purged.\n\n#### 1.6.5 Data Retention\n\n| Data | Retention | Justification |\n|------|-----------|---------------|\n| `push_tokens` | Until employee departs + 90 days cleanup | Necessary for service delivery |\n| `push_preferences` | Until employee departs | User preference, deletable on request |\n| `push_delivery_log` | 30 days rolling | Debugging and audit |\n| `notifications` (in-app) | Indefinite (user can delete) | User-facing data |\n\n### 1.7 Badge Management\n\n- **iOS**: Badge count is managed by Expo's `badge` field in push messages. Set to the user's unread notification count from the `notifications` table (where `read_at IS NULL`).\n- **Android**: Badge is managed via notification channels and the launcher (varies by manufacturer). Expo handles this transparently.\n- **Reset badge**: When the user opens the Notifications tab in the app, call `Notifications.setBadgeCountAsync(0)` and mark all notifications as read.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Internationalization (i18n)\n\n### 2.1 Architecture Overview\n\n```\n+-------------------+     +-------------------+     +-------------------+\n|  Device Locale    |     |  User Profile     |     |  i18n System      |\n|  (expo-local.)    |     |  (profile.lang)   |     |  (i18next)        |\n|                   |     |                   |     |                   |\n|  getLocales()     |---->|  language: 'nl'   |---->|  i18next.init()   |\n|  [{ languageCode  |     |  (from Supabase)  |     |  resources: {...} |\n|    'nl' }]        |     |                   |     |  lng: 'nl'        |\n+-------------------+     +-------------------+     +-------------------+\n```\n\n**Language Priority (in order):**\n\n1. User's saved language preference in `profiles.language` (from Supabase, after login)\n2. Device locale from `expo-localization` (before login, or if profile has no preference)\n3. Fallback: `'nl'` (Dutch, as it is the primary staff language)\n\n**Key Decision: `i18next` + `react-i18next` instead of `next-intl`**\n\nThe web app uses `next-intl` which is tightly coupled to Next.js server components. React Native has no server components, so we use the standard `i18next` + `react-i18next` stack. However, the **translation JSON files are shared** between web and mobile via a build-time sync mechanism.\n\n### 2.2 Package Dependencies\n\n```json\n{\n  \"expo-localization\": \"~16.0.0\",\n  \"i18next\": \"^24.0.0\",\n  \"react-i18next\": \"^15.0.0\",\n  \"intl-pluralrules\": \"^2.0.0\"\n}\n```\n\nThe `intl-pluralrules` polyfill is needed for older Android versions (Hermes engine may lack full `Intl.PluralRules` support).\n\n### 2.3 Namespace Structure\n\nThe mobile app uses a **subset** of the web app's namespaces, plus mobile-specific ones. This keeps bundle size minimal while sharing translation keys.\n\n#### Mobile Namespaces\n\n| Namespace | Source | Description |\n|-----------|--------|-------------|\n| `common` | Shared with web | Buttons, labels, errors, roles, status |\n| `home` | **Mobile-only** | Dashboard, stats, quick actions |\n| `schedule` | Derived from web `staff` | Calendar, shifts, swaps, leave |\n| `clock` | Derived from web `kiosk` | Time tracking, clock-in/out |\n| `chat` | Shared with web (`common.chat`) | Messaging UI |\n| `profile` | Derived from web `settings` | Personal info, preferences |\n| `notifications` | **Mobile-only** | Push notification content, settings |\n| `tasks` | Derived from web `staff.tasks` | Task list, details |\n\n#### Shared vs. Mobile-Only Keys\n\n- **Shared keys**: `common.buttons.*`, `common.roles.*`, `common.status.*`, `common.errors.*`, `common.time.*`\n- **Derived keys**: Extracted from web namespaces but flattened/renamed for mobile context\n- **Mobile-only keys**: Touch-specific labels, notification templates, onboarding text\n\n### 2.4 Translation File Structure\n\nFiles are organized under:\n\n```\nsrc/i18n/\n  config.ts              # Locale list, fallback, supported locales\n  i18n.ts                # i18next initialization\n  locales/\n    nl/\n      common.json\n      home.json\n      schedule.json\n      clock.json\n      chat.json\n      profile.json\n      notifications.json\n      tasks.json\n    en/\n      common.json\n      home.json\n      schedule.json\n      clock.json\n      chat.json\n      profile.json\n      notifications.json\n      tasks.json\n    es/\n      ... (same structure)\n    de/\n      ... (same structure)\n```\n\n### 2.5 Complete Translation Files (All 4 Languages)\n\n#### 2.5.1 `common.json`\n\n**English (`en/common.json`):**\n\n```json\n{\n  \"buttons\": {\n    \"save\": \"Save\",\n    \"cancel\": \"Cancel\",\n    \"delete\": \"Delete\",\n    \"edit\": \"Edit\",\n    \"add\": \"Add\",\n    \"confirm\": \"Confirm\",\n    \"back\": \"Back\",\n    \"next\": \"Next\",\n    \"done\": \"Done\",\n    \"close\": \"Close\",\n    \"retry\": \"Retry\",\n    \"refresh\": \"Refresh\",\n    \"loading\": \"Loading...\",\n    \"submit\": \"Submit\",\n    \"viewAll\": \"View All\",\n    \"apply\": \"Apply\",\n    \"reject\": \"Reject\",\n    \"approve\": \"Approve\"\n  },\n  \"roles\": {\n    \"admin\": \"Admin\",\n    \"manager\": \"Manager\",\n    \"kitchen\": \"Kitchen\",\n    \"bar\": \"Bar\",\n    \"waiter\": \"Waiter\",\n    \"dj\": \"DJ\",\n    \"owner\": \"Owner\"\n  },\n  \"status\": {\n    \"active\": \"Active\",\n    \"inactive\": \"Inactive\",\n    \"pending\": \"Pending\",\n    \"confirmed\": \"Confirmed\",\n    \"cancelled\": \"Cancelled\",\n    \"completed\": \"Completed\",\n    \"published\": \"Published\",\n    \"draft\": \"Draft\"\n  },\n  \"errors\": {\n    \"generic\": \"Something went wrong\",\n    \"networkError\": \"No internet connection\",\n    \"sessionExpired\": \"Session expired. Please sign in again.\",\n    \"failedToLoad\": \"Failed to load data\",\n    \"failedToSave\": \"Failed to save changes\",\n    \"unauthorized\": \"Unauthorized\",\n    \"notFound\": \"Not found\",\n    \"permissionDenied\": \"Permission denied\"\n  },\n  \"time\": {\n    \"today\": \"Today\",\n    \"yesterday\": \"Yesterday\",\n    \"tomorrow\": \"Tomorrow\",\n    \"thisWeek\": \"This week\",\n    \"nextWeek\": \"Next week\",\n    \"lastWeek\": \"Last week\",\n    \"ago\": \"{{time}} ago\",\n    \"hoursShort\": \"{{count}}h\",\n    \"minutesShort\": \"{{count}}m\"\n  },\n  \"empty\": {\n    \"noData\": \"No data available\",\n    \"noResults\": \"No results found\",\n    \"pullToRefresh\": \"Pull down to refresh\"\n  },\n  \"auth\": {\n    \"signIn\": \"Sign In\",\n    \"signOut\": \"Sign Out\",\n    \"email\": \"Email\",\n    \"password\": \"Password\",\n    \"forgotPassword\": \"Forgot Password?\",\n    \"welcomeBack\": \"Welcome back\"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Dutch
