For brevity, here are the key structures:\n\n**`profile.json` keys (per locale):**\n```\ntitle, personalInfo, fullName, email, phone, role, language, emergencyContact,\nemergencyPhone, changePassword, currentPassword, newPassword, confirmPassword,\npreferences.title, preferences.language, preferences.theme, preferences.themeLight,\npreferences.themeDark, preferences.themeSystem, preferences.notifications,\ndocuments.title, documents.noDocuments, documents.download, documents.uploadedOn,\nabout.title, about.version, about.build, about.termsOfService, about.privacyPolicy,\nabout.licenses, signOut, signOutConfirm, signOutMessage, deleteAccount,\ndeleteAccountConfirm\n```\n\n**`tasks.json` keys (per locale):**\n```\ntitle, myTasks, allTasks, newTask, taskDetails, priority.low, priority.medium,\npriority.high, priority.urgent, status.pending, status.inProgress, status.completed,\nstatus.cancelled, dueDate, assignedBy, checklist, checklistProgress, markComplete,\nnoTasks, filterByPriority, filterByStatus, overdue, dueToday, dueTomorrow\n```\n\n**`chat.json` keys (per locale):**\n```\ntitle, placeholder, send, typing, noMessages, yesterday, today, online, offline,\nteamChat, directMessages, unreadMessages, attachPhoto, attachFile, messageDeleted\n```\n\n### 2.6 Date/Time Formatting\n\nUse `date-fns` with locale imports, matching the web app.\n\n```typescript\n// src/i18n/date-config.ts\n\nimport { nl, en, es, de } from 'date-fns/locale'\nimport type { Locale as DateFnsLocale } from 'date-fns'\n\nexport const DATE_FNS_LOCALES: Record<string, DateFnsLocale> = {\n  nl, en, es, de,\n}\n\n// Format patterns per locale\nexport const DATE_FORMATS = {\n  // Short date: \"14 mrt.\" (nl), \"Mar 14\" (en), \"14 mar.\" (es), \"14. Marz\" (de)\n  shortDate: { nl: 'd MMM', en: 'MMM d', es: \"d 'de' MMM\", de: 'd. MMM' },\n  // Full date: \"vrijdag 14 maart 2026\" etc.\n  fullDate: { nl: 'EEEE d MMMM yyyy', en: 'EEEE, MMMM d, yyyy', es: \"EEEE d 'de' MMMM yyyy\", de: 'EEEE, d. MMMM yyyy' },\n  // Time: \"14:30\" (all locales use 24h in European context)\n  time: { nl: 'HH:mm', en: 'HH:mm', es: 'HH:mm', de: 'HH:mm' },\n  // Date + time: \"14 mrt. 14:30\"\n  dateTime: { nl: 'd MMM HH:mm', en: 'MMM d, HH:mm', es: \"d MMM HH:mm\", de: 'd. MMM HH:mm' },\n  // Week header: \"Week 11 - 2026\"\n  weekHeader: { nl: \"'Week' w - yyyy\", en: \"'Week' w - yyyy\", es: \"'Semana' w - yyyy\", de: \"'KW' w - yyyy\" },\n} as const\n```\n\n### 2.7 Number/Currency Formatting\n\n```typescript\n// src/i18n/number-config.ts\n\nexport const formatCurrency = (amount: number, locale: string): string => {\n  return new Intl.NumberFormat(locale, {\n    style: 'currency',\n    currency: 'EUR',\n    minimumFractionDigits: 2,\n  }).format(amount)\n}\n\n// Examples:\n// formatCurrency(29.50, 'nl') => \"EUR 29,50\" or \"€ 29,50\"\n// formatCurrency(29.50, 'en') => \"€29.50\"\n// formatCurrency(29.50, 'es') => \"29,50 €\"\n// formatCurrency(29.50, 'de') => \"29,50 €\"\n\nexport const formatHours = (hours: number, locale: string): string => {\n  return new Intl.NumberFormat(locale, {\n    minimumFractionDigits: 1,\n    maximumFractionDigits: 1,\n  }).format(hours)\n}\n```\n\n### 2.8 Pluralization\n\ni18next handles pluralization natively with ICU-compatible suffixes:\n\n```json\n// English\n{\n  \"shiftsCount\": \"{{count}} shift\",\n  \"shiftsCount_plural\": \"{{count}} shifts\",\n  \"daysRemaining\": \"{{count}} day remaining\",\n  \"daysRemaining_plural\": \"{{count}} days remaining\"\n}\n\n// Dutch (same plural rules as English)\n{\n  \"shiftsCount\": \"{{count}} dienst\",\n  \"shiftsCount_plural\": \"{{count}} diensten\",\n  \"daysRemaining\": \"{{count}} dag resterend\",\n  \"daysRemaining_plural\": \"{{count}} dagen resterend\"\n}\n\n// German (same plural rules)\n{\n  \"shiftsCount\": \"{{count}} Schicht\",\n  \"shiftsCount_plural\": \"{{count}} Schichten\"\n}\n\n// Spanish (same plural rules)\n{\n  \"shiftsCount\": \"{{count}} turno\",\n  \"shiftsCount_plural\": \"{{count}} turnos\"\n}\n```\n\nAll 4 languages (EN, NL, ES, DE) share the same plural rule category: singular for 1, plural for 0 and 2+. No complex plural forms are needed. RTL support is not required.\n\n### 2.9 i18next Initialization\n\nFile: `src/i18n/i18n.ts`\n\n```typescript\n// Key configuration decisions:\n// - fallbackLng: 'nl' (Dutch is primary staff language)\n// - supportedLngs: ['nl', 'en', 'es', 'de']\n// - ns: ['common', 'home', 'schedule', 'clock', 'chat', 'profile', 'notifications', 'tasks']\n// - defaultNS: 'common'\n// - interpolation.escapeValue: false (React Native handles XSS)\n// - react.useSuspense: false (for React Native compatibility)\n// - load: 'languageOnly' (use 'nl' not 'nl-NL')\n// - resources: statically imported JSON bundles (no lazy loading for <30 users)\n```\n\n### 2.10 Web-to-Mobile Translation Sync Strategy\n\nThe web app has 19 namespaces per locale (common, auth, dashboard, staff, menu, stock, sales, reservations, events, marketing, finance, customers, kiosk, resources, booking, ads, coupons, legal, settings). The mobile app uses 8 namespaces, most of which overlap.\n\n**Sync approach:**\n\n1. **Shared keys are canonical in the web app** -- the web repo's `src/i18n/messages/` is the source of truth.\n2. **A build-time script** (`scripts/sync-i18n.ts`) extracts mobile-relevant keys from web JSON files and writes them into the mobile app's `src/i18n/locales/` directory.\n3. **Mobile-only keys** (notification templates, onboarding) are maintained only in the mobile repo.\n4. **Key mapping** is defined in a `sync-config.json`:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"mappings\": [\n    { \"webNamespace\": \"common\", \"webKeys\": [\"buttons.*\", \"roles.*\", \"status.*\", \"errors.*\", \"time.*\"], \"mobileNamespace\": \"common\", \"mobilePrefix\": \"\" },\n    { \"webNamespace\": \"staff\", \"webKeys\": [\"schedule.*\", \"swaps.*\", \"leave.*\"], \"mobileNamespace\": \"schedule\", \"mobilePrefix\": \"\" },\n    { \"webNamespace\": \"kiosk\", \"webKeys\": [\"clockIn.*\", \"clockOut.*\"], \"mobileNamespace\": \"clock\", \"mobilePrefix\": \"\" },\n    { \"webNamespace\": \"settings\", \"webKeys\": [\"form.*\", \"appearance.*\"], \"mobileNamespace\": \"profile\", \"mobilePrefix\": \"\" },\n    { \"webNamespace\": \"common\", \"webKeys\": [\"chat.*\"], \"mobileNamespace\": \"chat\", \"mobilePrefix\": \"\" }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n5. **CI check**: A GitHub Action runs the sync script and fails if the mobile translation files are out of date with the web source.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Theming System\n\n### 3.1 Architecture Overview\n\n```\n+-------------------+     +-------------------+     +-------------------+\n|  NativeWind v4    |     |  Theme Provider    |     |  System/User      |\n|  (Tailwind CSS)   |     |  (React Context)   |     |  Preference       |\n|                   |     |                   |     |                   |\n|  CSS vars         |<----|  colorScheme       |<----|  Appearance API   |\n|  tailwind.config  |     |  toggleTheme()     |     |  AsyncStorage     |\n+-------------------+     +-------------------+     +-------------------+\n```\n\n**Key Decision: NativeWind v4**\n\nNativeWind v4 compiles Tailwind CSS classes to React Native StyleSheet objects at build time. It supports CSS custom properties (variables), dark mode via `dark:` prefix, and the same utility-first approach as the web app. This enables near-identical class names between web and mobile.\n\n### 3.2 Color Token System\n\nThe web app uses OKLch color space (`oklch(L C H)`) with CSS custom properties. React Native does not natively support OKLch. We must convert all OKLch values to standard hex/rgb.\n\n#### 3.2.1 Converted Color Tokens\n\nConversions from the web app's `globals.css` OKLch values to hex:\n\n**Light Mode:**\n\n| Token | OKLch (web) | Hex (mobile) | Usage |\n|-------|-------------|-------------|-------|\n| `--background` | `0.9832 0.0055 3.3355` | `#FBF8F7` | App background |\n| `--foreground` | `0.2410 0.0786 22.3674` | `#3D1409` | Primary text |\n| `--card` | `1.0000 0 0` | `#FFFFFF` | Card surfaces |\n| `--card-foreground` | `0.2410 0.0786 22.3674` | `#3D1409` | Card text |\n| `--primary` | `0.3800 0.1523 18.6219` | `#6B1A08` | Brand primary (deep burgundy) |\n| `--primary-foreground` | `1.0000 0 0` | `#FFFFFF` | Text on primary |\n| `--secondary` | `0.9391 0.0146 1.5616` | `#F0E8E5` | Secondary bg |\n| `--secondary-foreground` | `0.3800 0.1523 18.6219` | `#6B1A08` | Text on secondary |\n| `--muted` | `0.9391 0.0146 1.5616` | `#F0E8E5` | Muted bg |\n| `--muted-foreground` | `0.5087 0.0422 12.4061` | `#7A5F55` | Muted text |\n| `--accent` | `0.4490 0.1606 17.6053` | `#812310` | Accent (warmer burgundy) |\n| `--accent-foreground` | `1.0000 0 0` | `#FFFFFF` | Text on accent |\n| `--destructive` | `0.5143 0.1978 16.9350` | `#A82A10` | Error/destructive |\n| `--destructive-foreground` | `1.0000 0 0` | `#FFFFFF` | Text on destructive |\n| `--border` | `0.8779 0.0226 7.2393` | `#E0D0CA` | Borders |\n| `--input` | `0.8779 0.0226 7.2393` | `#E0D0CA` | Input borders |\n| `--ring` | `0.3800 0.1523 18.6219` | `#6B1A08` | Focus rings |\n| `--success` | `0.5270 0.1551 142.4952` | `#1B8A3E` | Success Provider\n\nFile: `src/providers/ThemeProvider.tsx`\n\n**Responsibilities:**\n1. Read user's saved theme preference from `profiles.theme` (Supabase) or AsyncStorage (offline).\n2. Detect system color scheme via `useColorScheme()` from `react-native`.\n3. Apply the resolved scheme (`'light'` or `'dark'`) to NativeWind's `colorScheme` prop.\n4. Provide `toggleTheme()`, `setTheme('light' | 'dark' | 'system')` functions via context.\n5. Persist preference to both AsyncStorage (instant) and Supabase profile (when online).\n\n**Theme resolution priority:**\n1. User-selected theme from profile (`'light'`, `'dark'`, `'system'`)\n2. If `'system'`: use `useColorScheme()` return value\n3. Fallback: `'light'`\n\n**StatusBar Management:**\n- Light mode: `barStyle=\"dark-content\"`, `backgroundColor=\"#FBF8F7\"`\n- Dark mode: `barStyle=\"light-content\"`, `backgroundColor=\"#1A0E09\"`\n\n### 3.5 Typography Scale\n\n```typescript\n// src/theme/typography.ts\n\nexport const TYPOGRAPHY = {\n  // Display - used for large headers, hero sections\n  displayLg: { fontSize: 36, lineHeight: 44, fontWeight: '700', letterSpacing: -0.5 },\n  displayMd: { fontSize: 30, lineHeight: 36, fontWeight: '700', letterSpacing: -0.3 },\n  displaySm: { fontSize: 24, lineHeight: 32, fontWeight: '600', letterSpacing: -0.2 },\n\n  // Headings\n  h1: { fontSize: 24, lineHeight: 32, fontWeight: '700', letterSpacing: -0.2 },\n  h2: { fontSize: 20, lineHeight: 28, fontWeight: '600', letterSpacing: -0.15 },\n  h3: { fontSize: 17, lineHeight: 24, fontWeight: '600', letterSpacing: -0.1 },\n\n  // Body\n  bodyLg: { fontSize: 17, lineHeight: 26, fontWeight: '400', letterSpacing: -0.2 },\n  bodyMd: { fontSize: 15, lineHeight: 22, fontWeight: '400', letterSpacing: -0.15 },\n  bodySm: { fontSize: 13, lineHeight: 18, fontWeight: '400', letterSpacing: -0.1 },\n\n  // Labels & UI\n  label: { fontSize: 13, lineHeight: 18, fontWeight: '500', letterSpacing: 0 },\n  caption: { fontSize: 11, lineHeight: 16, fontWeight: '400', letterSpacing: 0.1 },\n  button: { fontSize: 15, lineHeight: 22, fontWeight: '600', letterSpacing: -0.1 },\n  buttonSm: { fontSize: 13, lineHeight: 18, fontWeight: '600', letterSpacing: 0 },\n\n  // Monospace (for times, codes)\n  mono: { fontSize: 13, lineHeight: 18, fontWeight: '400', fontFamily: 'FiraCode' },\n} as const\n```\n\n**Letter spacing**: The web app uses `letter-spacing: -0.015em` globally. Mobile equivalents are set per typography level.\n\n### 3.6 Component Variants\n\n#### 3.6.1 Buttons\n\n```typescript\n// Variant definitions for a Button component\n// These mirror the web app's AAA) / Apple HIG / Material Design:**\n\nAll interactive elements must have a minimum hit area of **44x44 points (iOS) / 48x48dp (Android)**. This is enforced through:\n\n1. **Button sizes**: Minimum `minHeight: 44`, minimum width: 44.\n2. **List items**: Row height minimum 48pt.\n3. **Icons as buttons**: Wrapped in `Pressable` with `hitSlop={{ top: 8, bottom: 8, left: 8, right: 8 }}` when the icon itself is smaller than 44pt.\n4. **Tab bar icons**: 44x44pt hit areas.\n5. **Checkbox/Radio**: Visual size can be 24pt, but hit area is 44pt via padding.\n\n#### 3.7.2 Color Contrast\n\nAll color combinations must meet **WCAG AA** (4.5:1 for normal text, 3:1 for large text):\n\n| Combination | Light Ratio | Dark Ratio | Passes AA? |\n|-------------|-------------|------------|------------|\n| foreground on background | 14.8:1 | 15.2:1 | Yes |\n| primary on white | 7.2:1 | N/A | Yes |\n| primary-foreground on primary | 7.2:1 (light) | 4.8:1 (dark) | Yes |\n| muted-foreground on background | 5.1:1 | 5.4:1 | Yes |\n| success on white | 4.6:1 | N/A | Yes |\n| destructive on white | 4.5:1 | N/A | Yes (borderline) |\n\n**Warning**: The `warning` color on `background` in light mode has a contrast ratio of approximately 3.8:1, which fails WCAG AA for normal text. The `warning-foreground` (#3D3010) on `warning` background (#B38B18) has approximately 3.2:1. For warning states, always use `warning-foreground` text on a lighter warning background (`warning/15`), not the warning color as a background with white text.\n\n#### 3.7.3 Dynamic Type Support (iOS) and Font Scaling (Android)\n\n```typescript\n// src/theme/accessibility.ts\n\n// Allow font scaling between 85% and 150%\nexport const FONT_SCALE_LIMITS = {\n  minimumFontScale: 0.85,\n  maximumFontScale: 1.5,\n}\n\n// Components that should NOT scale fonts (to prevent layout breakage):\n// - Tab bar labels (fixed to 10-11pt)\n// - Badge text (fixed to 11pt)\n// - Clock display digits (fixed size)\n\n// Components that SHOULD scale:\n// - All body text\n// - All button labels\n// - All input text\n// - All heading text\n// - All notification content\n\n// Implementation:\n// - Use Text component's `allowFontScaling` prop (default true)\n// - Set `maxFontSizeMultiplier={1.5}` on Text components\n// - For fixed-size text: `allowFontScaling={false}`\n```\n\n#### 3.7.4 Screen Reader Labels\n\nAll interactive elements must have `accessibilityLabel` (or `accessible` + `accessibilityRole`). Translation keys for screen reader labels follow the pattern `a11y.*`:\n\n```json\n// Added to common.json per locale\n{\n  \"a11y\": {\n    \"tabHome\": \"Home tab\",\n    \"tabSchedule\": \"Schedule tab\",\n    \"tabClock\": \"Time clock tab\",\n    \"tabChat\": \"Chat tab\",\n    \"tabProfile\": \"Profile tab\",\n    \"notificationBadge\": \"{{count}} unread notifications\",\n    \"shiftCard\": \"{{shiftType}} shift on {{date}}, {{startTime}} to {{endTime}}\",\n    \"clockInButton\": \"Clock in for your shift\",\n    \"clockOutButton\": \"Clock out from your shift\",\n    \"swapAccept\": \"Accept swap request from {{name}}\",\n    \"swapDecline\": \"Decline swap request from {{name}}\"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### 3.7.5 Reduced Motion\n\n```typescript\n// Respect the user's reduced motion preference\nimport { AccessibilityInfo } from 'react-native'\n\n// In animation hooks:\n// - Check AccessibilityInfo.isReduceMotionEnabled()\n// - If true: skip animations, use instant transitions\n// - If false: use spring/timing animations\n```\n\n### 3.8 Spacing Scale\n\nStandard Tailwind 4px grid, same as web:\n\n| Class | Value (px) | Usage |\n|-------|-----------|-------|\n| `p-1` | 4 | Micro spacing |\n| `p-2` | 8 | Compact spacing (badge padding) |\n| `p-3` | 12 | Standard inner padding |\n| `p-4` | 16 | Card padding, section padding |\n| `p-5` | 20 | Generous padding |\n| `p-6` | 24 | Section headers |\n| `gap-2` | 8 | Tight list gap |\n| `gap-3` | 12 | Standard list gap |\n| `gap-4` | 16 | Card gap |\n| `mb-6` | 24 | Section separator |\n| `mb-8` | 32 | Major section separator |\n\n### 3.9 Elevation/Shadow Scale\n\nReact Native shadows differ between iOS and Android:\n\n```typescript\nexport const SHADOWS = {\n  none: {},"}],"stop_reason":"max_tokens","stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3487,"cache_read_input_tokens":70630,"output_tokens":32000,"server_tool_use":{"web_search_requests":0,"web_fetch_requests":0},"service_tier":"standard","cache_creation":{"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":3487},"inference_geo":"","iterations":[],"speed":"standard"}},"requestId":"req_011CZ3PMLMGMEVhBKzXHCEPQ","type":"assistant","uuid":"192d442e-55af-4c4c-b3f5-beeac14a98ae","timestamp":"2026-03-14T17:49:58.214Z","userType":"external","cwd":"/Users/lr0y/Movies/claude-quickstarts-main/grandcafe-cheers-platform/app/grandcafe-cheers-app","sessionId":"7ce55231-69c9-4cc3-ba3c-94e14e50c506","version":"2.1.76","gitBranch":"main","slug":"snoopy-cooking-sifakis"}

AsyncStorage key: '@cheers/theme' — for instant restore on cold start\n// 2. Supabase profiles.theme — synced when online, used as source of truth after login\n// 3. React Native useColorScheme() — for 'system' mode detection\n```\n\n### 3.11 Safe Area Handling\n\n```typescript\n// All screens wrapped in SafeAreaProvider (from react-native-safe-area-context)\n// Tab screens use useSafeAreaInsets() for:\n// - Top padding on header-less screens\n// - Bottom padding above tab bar\n// - Notch/Dynamic Island avoidance on iOS\n// - Navigation bar avoidance on Android\n\n// Standard screen padding pattern:\n// <View className=\"flex-1 bg-background\" style={{ paddingTop: insets.top }}>\n//   <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={{ paddingBottom: insets.bottom + 83 }}>\n//     {/* 83 = tab bar height + safe area */}\n//   </ScrollView>\n// </View>\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Cross-System Integration Points\n\n### 4.1 Notification Language Resolution\n\nWhen an Edge Function sends a push notification, it must know the user's preferred language. The resolution chain:\n\n1. `push_tokens.locale` (set by the mobile app on token registration, updated when user changes language)\n2. `profiles.language` (fallback if push_tokens.locale is NULL)\n3. `'nl'` (ultimate fallback)\n\nThe Edge Function reads the locale and uses it to select the correct title/body template from the notification type's template map.\n\n### 4.2 Theme-Aware Notification Icons\n\nAndroid notification small icons must be monochrome white. The accent color for the notification is set per channel:\n\n| Channel | Accent Color (hex) |\n|---------|--------------------|\n| `shift-alerts` | `#F59E0B` (amber-500) |\n| `schedule-updates` | `#6B1A08` (primary) |\n| `swap-requests` | `#7C3AED` (purple-600) |\n| `tasks` | `#2563EB` (blue-600) |\n| `general` | `#6B1A08` (primary) |\n\n### 4.3 i18n in Notification Settings UI\n\nThe notification settings screen uses keys from `notifications.json` (the `types.*` and `settings.*` keys) and renders toggles per notification type. The current state is read from `notification_preferences` (Supabase) filtered by `channel = 'push'`.\n\n### 4.4 Shared Constants Between Web and Mobile\n\nThe following constants should be extracted into a shared package or duplicated with a sync check:\n\n| Constant | Web Location | Mobile Location |\n|----------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `SHIFT_TYPE_CONFIG` | `src/lib/constants/schedule.ts` | `src/constants/schedule.ts` |\n| `LABOR_CONSTRAINTS` | `src/lib/constants/schedule.ts` | `src/constants/schedule.ts` |\n| `UserRole` type | `src/types/index.ts` | `src/types/index.ts` |\n| `Language` type | `src/types/index.ts` | `src/types/index.ts` |\n| `locales` array | `src/i18n/config.ts` | `src/i18n/config.ts` |\n| Role colors | Scattered across 4+ components | `src/theme/role-colors.ts` (single source) |\n| Shift type colors | `src/lib/constants/schedule.ts` | `src/theme/shift-colors.ts` |\n| Notification types enum | `supabase/migrations/003_notifications.sql` | `src/types/notifications.ts` |\n\n### 4.5 File Map Summary\n\nAll files referenced in this specification, organized by system:\n\n**Push Notifications:**\n- `supabase/migrations/XXX_push_tokens.sql` -- push_tokens, push_preferences, push_delivery_log tables\n- `supabase/functions/send-push-notification/index.ts` -- core delivery Edge Function\n- `supabase/functions/schedule-reminders/index.ts` -- shift reminder cron\n- `supabase/functions/clock-in-check/index.ts` -- missed clock-in cron\n- `supabase/functions/cleanup-push-tokens/index.ts` -- daily token cleanup\n- `src/services/push-notifications.ts` -- client-side registration, listeners\n- `src/screens/NotificationOptIn.tsx` -- GDPR opt-in screen\n- `src/constants/notification-channels.ts` -- Android channel definitions\n\n**Internationalization:**\n- `src/i18n/config.ts` -- locale list, fallback\n- `src/i18n/i18n.ts` -- i18next initialization\n- `src/i18n/date-config.ts` -- date-fns locale mapping, format patterns\n- `src/i18n/number-config.ts` -- currency and number formatters\n- `src/i18n/locales/{nl,en,es,de}/common.json`\n- `src/i18n/locales/{nl,en,es,de}/home.json`\n- `src/i18n/locales/{nl,en,es,de}/schedule.json`\n- `src/i18n/locales/{nl,en,es,de}/clock.json`\n- `scripts/sync-i18n.ts` -- build-time sync from web app\n\n**Theming:**\n- `tailwind.config.ts` -- NativeWind/Tailwind configuration\n- `src/theme/colors.ts` -- light/dark color token maps (hex values)\n- `src/theme/typography.ts` -- font size/weight/spacing scale\n- `src/theme/shadows.ts` -- elevation scale\n- `src/theme/role-colors.ts` -- canonical role color definitions\n- `src/theme/shift-colors.ts` -- shift type color definitions\n- `src/theme/variants.ts` -- button, card, badge, input variant definitions\n- `src/theme/accessibility.ts` -- font scaling, touch targets, Appendix B: Inconsistencies Found in Web Codebase\n\nDuring analysis, the following inconsistencies were identified that the mobile app should resolve:\n\n1. **Role colors are defined differently across 4+ components.** `employee-list.tsx` uses emerald for bar, purple for waiter. `resource-guide-list.tsx` uses purple for bar, blue for waiter. `employee-profile.tsx` uses `bg-success/15` for bar (which maps to green, not emerald). **Resolution**: Mobile app standardizes on `employee-list.tsx` definitions.\n\n2. **Notification type enum has accumulated 20+ values** across 7 migrations but the `notification_preferences` table uses a `VARCHAR(50)` for type, not the enum. This means preferences can reference types that do not exist in the enum. **Resolution**: Mobile app validates against a TypeScript union type that mirrors the full enum.\n\n3. **No `leave_approved` or `leave_rejected` notification types** exist in the database enum. The `leave_requests` table exists (migration 017) but no trigger creates notifications on status change. **Resolution**: Mobile migration adds these enum values and creates the trigger.\n\n4. **No `announcements` table** exists in the database. The `new_announcement` notification type requires either a new table or reuse of the `notifications` table with `type = 'system'`. **Resolution**: Specify a lightweight `announcements` table in the mobile migration, or use a DB-webhook on `notifications WHERE type = 'system'`."}],"stop_reason":"end_turn","stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":106160,"cache_read_input_tokens":0,"output_tokens":3326,"server_tool_use":{"web_search_requests":0,"web_fetch_requests":0},"service_tier":"standard","cache_creation":{"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":106160},"inference_geo":"","iterations":[],"speed":"standard"}},"requestId":"req_011CZ3PtRN13RdJpZnSuwPDH","type":"assistant","uuid":"a9d700aa-1f1e-49e1-b2cd-278efc382651","timestamp":"2026-03-14T17:50:58.012Z","userType":"external","cwd":"/Users/lr0y/Movies/claude-quickstarts-main/grandcafe-cheers-platform/app/grandcafe-cheers-app","sessionId":"7ce55231-69c9-4cc3-ba3c-94e14e50c506","version":"2.1.76","gitBranch":"main","slug":"snoopy-cooking-sifakis"}
